def export_files() -> None:
  lines: list[str] = []
  lines.append('=' * 50)
  lines.append('PROJECT EXPORT')
  lines.append('=' * 50)
  lines.append('')

  for relative_path in PROJECT_FILES:
    file_path = ROOT / relative_path

    lines.append('=' * 50)
    lines.append(f'FILE: {relative_path}')
    lines.append('=' * 50)
    lines.append('')

    if not file_path.exists():
      lines.append('[FILE NOT FOUND]')
      lines.append('')
      continue

    try:
      content = file_path.read_text(encoding='utf-8')
    except UnicodeDecodeError:
      content = file_path.read_text(encoding='utf-8', errors='replace')

    lines.append(content)
    lines.append('')

  OUTPUT_FILE.write_text('\n'.join(lines), encoding='utf-8')
  print(f'Export finished: {OUTPUT_FILE}')


if __name__ == '__main__':
  export_files()

==================================================
FILE: tools/metagen/metagen_siemens_generator.py
==================================================

#!/usr/bin/env python3
from __future__ import annotations

import argparse
import ast
import re
import sys
import shutil
from collections import OrderedDict
from dataclasses import dataclass
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Any, Iterable

import yaml

METAGEN_KIND = "metagen.component"
SCL_ENCODING = "utf-8"
TEMPLATE_VERSION = "0.1"
TEMPLATE_OPTIMIZED_ACCESS = "TRUE"
CONF_DB_NAME = "Conf_DB"
MAIN_FB_NAME = "_MetaGenMain"
MAIN_DB_NAME = None

# Defaults for library instance DBs. Unknown FB types fall back to DEFAULT_LIBRARY_* values.
DEFAULT_LIBRARY_VERSION = "0.1"
DEFAULT_LIBRARY_OPTIMIZED_ACCESS = "TRUE"
LIBRARY_INSTANCE_METADATA: dict[str, dict[str, str]] = {
    "CCabinetController": {"version": "2.3", "optimized_access": "TRUE"},
    "CCascade": {"version": "0.2", "optimized_access": "FALSE"},
}

PARAM_TOKEN_RE = re.compile(r"\|([^|]+)\|")
EVAL_TOKEN_RE = re.compile(r"%(.*?)%", re.DOTALL)

DATA_COLUMN_TYPE = "Тип"
DATA_COLUMN_DB = "Блок данных"
DATA_COLUMN_TAG = "Имя переменной"
DATA_COLUMN_VALUE = "Значение"
DATA_COLUMN_COMMENT = "Комментарий"
DATA_COLUMN_CONF = "Conf"


@dataclass(frozen=True)
class InstanceSpec:
    name: str
    fb_type: str


@dataclass(frozen=True)
class ConfEntry:
    tag: str
    data_type: str
    value: str
    comment: str


@dataclass
class TemplateDoc:
    source_path: Path
    name: str
    params_header: list[str]
    params_rows: list[list[str]]
    data_columns: list[str]
    data_rows: list[list[str]]
    instances_rows: list[list[str]]
    code_text: str


def parse_args() -> argparse.Namespace:
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(
        description=(
            "Generate Siemens SCL artifacts from MetaGen YAML documents. "
            "Inputs may be YAML files and/or directories. Directories are searched recursively "
            "for YAML files with kind: metagen.component."
        )
    )
    parser.add_argument(
        "inputs",
        nargs="+",
        help="YAML files and/or directories to scan recursively.",
    )
    parser.add_argument(
        "--output-dir",
        "-o",
        required=True,
        help="Directory where generated .scl files will be written. No subdirectories are created.",
    )
    return parser.parse_args()


def sanitize_cli_path(value: str) -> str:
    """Normalize Windows shell path quirks.

    In PowerShell/native Windows process launching, a quoted path ending with a backslash
    may arrive with a stray trailing double quote, for example:
    Such a quote is never valid in a Windows path, so we can safely trim it.
    """
    sanitized = value.strip()
    while sanitized.endswith(('"', "'")):
        sanitized = sanitized[:-1]
    return sanitized


def main() -> int:
    args = parse_args()
    input_paths = [Path(sanitize_cli_path(value)).expanduser().resolve() for value in args.inputs]
    output_dir = Path(sanitize_cli_path(args.output_dir)).expanduser().resolve()

    yaml_paths = discover_metagen_yaml_paths(input_paths)
    if not yaml_paths:
        raise SystemExit("No MetaGen YAML documents found in the provided inputs.")

    documents = [load_template_doc(path) for path in yaml_paths]

    output_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    clean_output_directory(output_dir)

    conf_entries = collect_conf_entries(documents)
    library_instances = collect_library_instances(documents)
    template_names = [document.name for document in documents]

    write_text(output_dir / f"{CONF_DB_NAME}.scl", render_conf_db(conf_entries))

    for instance in library_instances.values():
        write_text(output_dir / f"{instance.name}.scl", render_library_instance_db(instance))

    for document in documents:
        fb_name = document.name
        db_name = f"{fb_name}_DB"
        write_text(output_dir / f"{fb_name}.scl", render_template_fb(document))
        write_text(output_dir / f"{db_name}.scl", render_template_db(fb_name))

    write_text(output_dir / f"{MAIN_FB_NAME}.scl", render_main_fb(template_names))

    return 0


def discover_metagen_yaml_paths(input_paths: Iterable[Path]) -> list[Path]:
    discovered: list[Path] = []
    seen: set[Path] = set()

    for input_path in input_paths:
        if not input_path.exists():
            raise FileNotFoundError(f"Input path does not exist: {input_path}")

        if input_path.is_dir():
            candidates = sorted(
                path for path in input_path.rglob("*") if path.is_file() and path.suffix.lower() in {".yaml", ".yml"}
            )
        else:
            candidates = [input_path]

        for candidate in candidates:
            resolved = candidate.resolve()
            if resolved in seen:
                continue
            if is_metagen_component_yaml(resolved):
                discovered.append(resolved)
                seen.add(resolved)

    return discovered


def is_metagen_component_yaml(path: Path) -> bool:
    if path.suffix.lower() not in {".yaml", ".yml"}:
        return False
    try:
        text = path.read_text(encoding=SCL_ENCODING)
    except UnicodeDecodeError:
        text = path.read_text(encoding="utf-8-sig")
    try:
        payload = yaml.safe_load(text)
    except yaml.YAMLError:
        return False
    return isinstance(payload, dict) and payload.get("kind") == METAGEN_KIND


def load_template_doc(path: Path) -> TemplateDoc:
    payload = yaml.safe_load(path.read_text(encoding=SCL_ENCODING))
    if not isinstance(payload, dict) or payload.get("kind") != METAGEN_KIND:
        raise ValueError(f"Unsupported MetaGen document: {path}")

    component = require_dict(payload, "component", path)
    params = require_dict(payload, "params", path)
    data = require_dict(payload, "data", path)
    instances = require_dict(payload, "instances", path)
    code = require_dict(payload, "code", path)

    name = str(component.get("name") or "").strip()
    if not name:
        raise ValueError(f"component.name is required in {path}")

    params_header = normalize_string_list(params.get("header", []), path, "params.header")
    params_rows = normalize_rows(params.get("rows", []), len(params_header), path, "params.rows")

    data_columns = normalize_string_list(data.get("columns", []), path, "data.columns")
    if not data_columns:
        raise ValueError(f"data.columns is required in {path}")
    data_rows = normalize_rows(data.get("rows", []), len(data_columns), path, "data.rows")

    instances_rows = normalize_rows(instances.get("rows", []), 2, path, "instances.rows")
    code_text = str(code.get("text") or "")

    return TemplateDoc(
        source_path=path,
        name=name,
        params_header=params_header,
        params_rows=params_rows,
        data_columns=data_columns,
        data_rows=data_rows,
        instances_rows=instances_rows,
        code_text=code_text,
    )


def require_dict(payload: dict[str, Any], key: str, path: Path) -> dict[str, Any]:
    value = payload.get(key)
    if not isinstance(value, dict):
        raise ValueError(f"{key} must be a mapping in {path}")
    return value


def normalize_string_list(values: Any, path: Path, field_name: str) -> list[str]:
    if not isinstance(values, list):
        raise ValueError(f"{field_name} must be a list in {path}")
    return ["" if value is None else str(value) for value in values]


def normalize_rows(values: Any, expected_length: int, path: Path, field_name: str) -> list[list[str]]:
    if not isinstance(values, list):
        raise ValueError(f"{field_name} must be a list in {path}")

    normalized: list[list[str]] = []
    for index, row in enumerate(values):
        if row is None:
            normalized.append([""] * expected_length)
            continue
        if not isinstance(row, list):
            raise ValueError(f"{field_name}[{index}] must be a list in {path}")
        if len(row) > expected_length:
            raise ValueError(
                f"{field_name}[{index}] has {len(row)} items, expected at most {expected_length} in {path}"
            )
        normalized_row = ["" if value is None else stringify_scalar(value) for value in row]
        if len(normalized_row) < expected_length:
            normalized_row.extend([""] * (expected_length - len(normalized_row)))
        normalized.append(normalized_row)
    return normalized


def stringify_scalar(value: Any) -> str:
    if isinstance(value, bool):
        return "true" if value else "false"
    if isinstance(value, (int, float)):
        return str(value)
    return str(value)


def build_param_contexts(document: TemplateDoc) -> list[dict[str, str]]:
    header = document.params_header
    rows = document.params_rows
    if not header:
        return [{}]

    if not rows:
        return [dict(zip(header, [""] * len(header), strict=False))]

    return [dict(zip(header, row, strict=False)) for row in rows]


def apply_template(text: str, context: dict[str, str]) -> str:
    def replace_param(match: re.Match[str]) -> str:
        key = match.group(1)
        return context.get(key, match.group(0))

    substituted = PARAM_TOKEN_RE.sub(replace_param, text)

    def replace_eval(match: re.Match[str]) -> str:
        expr = match.group(1)
        env: dict[str, Any] = {}
        env.update(context)
        try:
            env.update({name: parse_eval_value(value) for name, value in context.items()})
        except Exception:
            pass
        value = eval(expr, {"__builtins__": __builtins__}, env)
        return stringify_scalar(value)

    return EVAL_TOKEN_RE.sub(replace_eval, substituted)


def parse_eval_value(value: str) -> Any:
    if value == "":
        return ""
    lowered = value.strip().lower()
    if lowered in {"true", "false"}:
        return lowered == "true"
    try:
        return ast.literal_eval(value)
    except Exception:
        return value


def collect_conf_entries(documents: Iterable[TemplateDoc]) -> list[ConfEntry]:
    entries: list[ConfEntry] = []
    seen_tags: set[str] = set()

    for document in documents:
        contexts = build_param_contexts(document)
        column_index = build_column_index(document.data_columns)
        required_columns = {DATA_COLUMN_TYPE, DATA_COLUMN_TAG, DATA_COLUMN_VALUE, DATA_COLUMN_COMMENT, DATA_COLUMN_CONF}
        missing = required_columns - set(column_index)
        if missing:
            raise ValueError(f"Missing required data columns {sorted(missing)} in {document.source_path}")

        for context in contexts:
            for row in document.data_rows:
                mapped = row_to_mapping(document.data_columns, row)
                conf_flag = mapped.get(DATA_COLUMN_CONF, "").strip()
                if not conf_flag:
                    continue
                tag = apply_template(mapped[DATA_COLUMN_TAG], context).strip()
                if not tag:
                    continue
                if tag in seen_tags:
                    continue
                seen_tags.add(tag)
                data_type = normalize_scl_type(apply_template(mapped[DATA_COLUMN_TYPE], context).strip())
                entries.append(
                    ConfEntry(
                        tag=tag,
                        data_type=data_type,
                        value=normalize_scl_value(apply_template(mapped[DATA_COLUMN_VALUE], context).strip(), data_type),
                        comment=apply_template(mapped[DATA_COLUMN_COMMENT], context).strip(),
                    )
                )
    return entries


def collect_library_instances(documents: Iterable[TemplateDoc]) -> OrderedDict[str, InstanceSpec]:
    instances: OrderedDict[str, InstanceSpec] = OrderedDict()
    for document in documents:
        contexts = build_param_contexts(document)
        for context in contexts:
            for row in document.instances_rows:
                if not any(cell.strip() for cell in row):
                    continue
                raw_name = row[0].strip()
                raw_type = row[1].strip() if len(row) > 1 else ""
                if not raw_name or not raw_type:
                    continue
                name = apply_template(raw_name, context).strip()
                fb_type = apply_template(raw_type, context).strip()
                existing = instances.get(name)
                if existing and existing.fb_type != fb_type:
                    raise ValueError(
                        f"Conflicting instance type for {name}: {existing.fb_type!r} vs {fb_type!r}"
                    )
                instances.setdefault(name, InstanceSpec(name=name, fb_type=fb_type))
    return instances


def build_column_index(columns: list[str]) -> dict[str, int]:
    return {name: index for index, name in enumerate(columns)}


def row_to_mapping(columns: list[str], row: list[str]) -> dict[str, str]:
    return {column: row[index] for index, column in enumerate(columns)}


def normalize_scl_type(value: str) -> str:
    if not value:
        return value
    mapping = {
        "bool": "Bool",
        "int": "Int",
        "dint": "DInt",
        "real": "Real",
        "word": "Word",
    }
    return mapping.get(value.lower(), value)


def normalize_scl_value(value: str, data_type: str) -> str:
    if value == "":
        return value
    lowered = value.lower()
    normalized_type = data_type.lower()

    if normalized_type == "bool":
        if lowered in {"0", "false"}:
            return "false"
        if lowered in {"1", "true"}:
            return "true"

    if normalized_type == "real":
        if re.fullmatch(r"[-+]?\d+", value):
            return f"{value}.0"

    if lowered in {"true", "false"}:
        return lowered

    return value


def render_conf_db(entries: list[ConfEntry]) -> str:
    header_lines = [
        f'DATA_BLOCK "{CONF_DB_NAME}"',
        "{ S7_Optimized_Access := 'TRUE' }",
        "VERSION : 0.1",
        "NON_RETAIN",
        "   VAR RETAIN",
    ]

    for entry in entries:
        comment = f"   // {entry.comment}" if entry.comment else ""
        header_lines.append(f"      {entry.tag} : {entry.data_type};{comment}")

    header_lines.extend(["   END_VAR", "", "", "BEGIN"])

    body_lines = [f"   {entry.tag} := {entry.value};" for entry in entries]

    return "\n".join(header_lines + body_lines + ["", "END_DATA_BLOCK", ""])


def render_library_instance_db(instance: InstanceSpec) -> str:
    metadata = LIBRARY_INSTANCE_METADATA.get(instance.fb_type, {})
    version = metadata.get("version", DEFAULT_LIBRARY_VERSION)
    optimized_access = metadata.get("optimized_access", DEFAULT_LIBRARY_OPTIMIZED_ACCESS)
    lines = [
        f'DATA_BLOCK "{instance.name}"',
        f"{{ S7_Optimized_Access := '{optimized_access}' }}",
        f"VERSION : {version}",
        "NON_RETAIN",
        f'"{instance.fb_type}"',
        "",
        "BEGIN",
        "",
        "END_DATA_BLOCK",
        "",
    ]
    return "\n".join(lines)


def render_template_db(fb_name: str) -> str:
    db_name = f"{fb_name}_DB"
    lines = [
        f'DATA_BLOCK "{db_name}"',
        "{ S7_Optimized_Access := 'TRUE' }",
        "VERSION : 0.1",
        "NON_RETAIN",
        f'"{fb_name}"',
        "",
        "BEGIN",
        "",
        "END_DATA_BLOCK",
        "",
    ]
    return "\n".join(lines)


def render_template_fb(document: TemplateDoc) -> str:
    rendered_body = render_template_code(document)
    lines = [
        f'FUNCTION_BLOCK "{document.name}"',
        "{ S7_Optimized_Access := 'TRUE' }",
        "VERSION : 0.1",
        "",
        "BEGIN",
        "",
    ]
    if rendered_body:
        lines.extend(rendered_body.splitlines())
    lines.extend(["", "END_FUNCTION_BLOCK", ""])
    return "\n".join(lines)


def render_main_fb(template_names: list[str]) -> str:
    body_lines: list[str] = []
    for template_name in template_names:
        body_lines.append(f'        "{template_name}_DB"();')
        body_lines.append("")
    lines = [
        f'FUNCTION_BLOCK "{MAIN_FB_NAME}"',
        "{ S7_Optimized_Access := 'TRUE' }",
        "VERSION : 0.1",
        "",
        "BEGIN",
        "",
        *body_lines,
        "END_FUNCTION_BLOCK",
        "",
    ]
    return "\n".join(lines)


def render_template_code(document: TemplateDoc) -> str:
    contexts = build_param_contexts(document)
    chunks: list[str] = []

    for context in contexts:
        rendered = apply_template(document.code_text, context)
        rendered = preserve_template_code(rendered)
        if rendered:
            chunks.append(rendered)
    return "\n".join(chunks)


def preserve_template_code(text: str) -> str:
    return text.replace("\r\n", "\n").replace("\r", "\n").strip("\n")

def write_text(path: Path, content: str) -> None:
    path.write_text(content, encoding=SCL_ENCODING, newline="\n")



def clean_output_directory(output_dir: Path) -> None:
    for child in output_dir.iterdir():
        if child.is_dir():
            shutil.rmtree(child)
        else:
            child.unlink()


if __name__ == "__main__":
    try:
        raise SystemExit(main())
    except Exception as exc:  # pragma: no cover - CLI friendly error path.
        print(f"Error: {exc}", file=sys.stderr)
        raise

export function getCurrentBackendProjectId({ projectManager, backendSource }) {
  const project = projectManager?.getCurrentProject?.();
  if (!project || project.source !== backendSource) {
    return '';
  }

  return String(
    project.backendProject?.projectId
    || project.project?.id
    || ''
  ).trim();
}

export function normalizeBackendLockedBy(lockedBy) {
  if (!lockedBy || typeof lockedBy !== 'object') {
    return null;
  }

  const userId = String(lockedBy.userId || '').trim();
  const displayName = String(lockedBy.displayName || '').trim();
  if (!userId) {
    return null;
  }

  return {
    userId,
    displayName: displayName || userId
  };
}

export function resolveBackendProjectLockState({ lockedBy, currentUserId }) {
  const normalizedLockedBy = normalizeBackendLockedBy(lockedBy);
  const normalizedCurrentUserId = String(currentUserId || '').trim();
  const isLocked = Boolean(normalizedLockedBy);
  const isOwnedLock = Boolean(
    isLocked
    && normalizedCurrentUserId
    && normalizedLockedBy.userId === normalizedCurrentUserId
  );

  return {
    lockedBy: normalizedLockedBy,
    isLocked,
    isOwnedLock,
    isForeignLock: isLocked && !isOwnedLock
  };
}

export function getBackendProjectCatalogPresentation({ project, currentUserId, text }) {
  const lockState = resolveBackendProjectLockState({
    lockedBy: project?.lockedBy,
    currentUserId
  });
  const projectName = String(project?.name || '').trim();
  const projectSlug = String(project?.slug || '').trim();
  const lockMarker = lockState.lockedBy
    ? ` [${text.backendProjectLockedMarker} ${text.backendProjectLockedByPrefix} ${lockState.lockedBy.displayName}]`
    : '';
  const lockText = lockState.lockedBy
    ? `${text.backendProjectLockedMarker} ${text.backendProjectLockedByPrefix} ${lockState.lockedBy.displayName}`
    : text.backendProjectLockFree;
  let openTitle = '';
  if (lockState.isForeignLock) {
    openTitle = `${text.backendOpenProjectLockedTooltipPrefix}: ${lockState.lockedBy.displayName}`;
  } else if (lockState.isOwnedLock) {
    openTitle = `${text.backendOpenProjectOwnedLockTooltipPrefix}: ${lockState.lockedBy.displayName}`;
  }

  return {
    lockState,
    projectName,
    projectSlug,
    lockText,
    projectLabel: `${projectName} (${projectSlug})${lockMarker}`,
    openDisabled: lockState.isForeignLock,
    openTitle
  };
}

export function applyBackendWorkspaceBrowserPresentationState({
  browserNode,
  hiddenClassName,
  isVisible
}) {
  const visible = Boolean(isVisible);
  if (!browserNode) {
    return visible;
  }

  browserNode.hidden = !visible;
  if (hiddenClassName) {
    browserNode.classList?.toggle?.(hiddenClassName, !visible);
  }
  browserNode.setAttribute?.('aria-hidden', String(!visible));
  return visible;
}

export function resolveBackendWorkspaceStartupRefreshDecision({
  startupListStrategy,
  startupListStrategies
}) {
  return startupListStrategy === startupListStrategies.autoRefreshOnce;
}

export function resolveBackendWorkspaceStartupIdlePresentation({ text }) {
  return {
    statusText: text.backendProjectsStatusIdle,
    emptyStateText: text.backendProjectsEmptyStateIdle,
    isEmptyStateVisible: true
  };
}

export function resolveBackendWorkspaceListRefreshPresentation({
  result,
  text
}) {
  if (!result) {
    return {
      projects: [],
      statusText: text.backendProjectsStatusUnavailable,
      emptyStateText: text.backendProjectsEmptyStateUnavailable,
      isEmptyStateVisible: true,
      isUnavailable: true
    };
  }

  const projects = Array.isArray(result?.projects) ? result.projects : [];
  return {
    projects,
    statusText: text.backendProjectsStatusReady,
    emptyStateText: text.backendProjectsEmptyState,
    isEmptyStateVisible: projects.length === 0,
    isUnavailable: false
  };
}

export function resolveBackendWorkspaceEntryFocusTarget({
  backendListButton,
  backendCreateInput,
  backendCatalogNode
}) {
  return backendListButton
    || backendCreateInput
    || backendCatalogNode
    || null;
}

export async function runNewProjectCreateFirstTransition({
  confirmSaveIfDirty,
  cancelDecision,
  releaseBackendProjectLockIfNeeded,
  stopReasonSwitch,
  closeAllTabs,
  clearLogs,
  closeProject,
  presentBackendWorkspaceBrowserForCreateFirst
}) {
  const canContinue = await confirmSaveIfDirty();
  if (canContinue === cancelDecision) {
    return false;
  }

  const releaseResult = await releaseBackendProjectLockIfNeeded({ reason: stopReasonSwitch });
  if (!releaseResult?.canContinue) {
    return false;
  }
  await closeAllTabs();
  clearLogs();
  await closeProject();
  await presentBackendWorkspaceBrowserForCreateFirst({
    refreshProjects: true,
    clearCreateInput: true
  });
  return true;
}

export async function runCloseProjectTransition({
  getCurrentProject,
  confirmSaveIfDirty,
  cancelDecision,
  releaseBackendProjectLockIfNeeded,
  stopReasonClose,
  closeAllTabs,
  clearLogs,
  closeProject,
  presentBackendWorkspaceBrowser
}) {
  if (!getCurrentProject?.()) {
    await presentBackendWorkspaceBrowser({ refreshProjects: false });
    return false;
  }

  const canContinue = await confirmSaveIfDirty();
  if (canContinue === cancelDecision) {
    return false;
  }

  const releaseResult = await releaseBackendProjectLockIfNeeded({ reason: stopReasonClose });
  if (!releaseResult?.canContinue) {
    return false;
  }
  await closeAllTabs();
  clearLogs();
  await closeProject();
  await presentBackendWorkspaceBrowser({ refreshProjects: false });
  return true;
}

export async function closeDeletedBackendProjectIfOpened({
  projectId,
  projectManager,
  backendSource,
  tabs,
  logger,
  tree,
  onBeforeClose = null
}) {
  const normalizedProjectId = String(projectId || '').trim();
  if (!normalizedProjectId) {
    return false;
  }

  const currentBackendProjectId = getCurrentBackendProjectId({
    projectManager,
    backendSource
  });
  if (!currentBackendProjectId || currentBackendProjectId !== normalizedProjectId) {
    return false;
  }

  await onBeforeClose?.();

  try {
    await tabs.closeAllTabs();
  } catch (_error) {
    // Continue close flow even if one tab fails to close cleanly.
  }
  logger.clear();
  await projectManager?.closeProject?.();
  await tree.render();
  return true;
}

export async function deleteBackendProjectFlow({
  project,
  confirmDelete,
  confirmPrefix,
  deleteCommandId,
  executeBackendCommand,
  closeDeletedProject,
  refreshBackendProjects
}) {
  const projectId = String(project?.id || '').trim();
  if (!projectId) {
    return false;
  }

  const projectLabel = `${project?.name || projectId}`;
  const confirmed = confirmDelete(`${confirmPrefix} ${projectLabel}`);
  if (!confirmed) {
    return false;
  }

  const commandResult = await executeBackendCommand(deleteCommandId, { projectId });
  if (!commandResult?.ok) {
    return false;
  }

  await closeDeletedProject(projectId);
  await refreshBackendProjects();
  return true;
}

export async function importBackendProjectFlow({
  openProjectImportArchiveDialog,
  importProjectArchive,
  refreshBackendProjects,
  setBackendResult,
  loggerWarn,
  loggerSource,
  backendImportFailedText,
  backendActiveProcessBusyText,
  activeProcessBusyErrorCode
}) {
  const selectedArchive = await openProjectImportArchiveDialog();
  if (!selectedArchive) {
    return false;
  }

  const response = await importProjectArchive({
    fileName: selectedArchive.fileName,
    bytes: selectedArchive.bytes
  });
  if (!response.ok) {
    const errorCode = String(response?.error?.code || '').trim();
    const warningText = errorCode === String(activeProcessBusyErrorCode || '').trim()
      ? backendActiveProcessBusyText
      : backendImportFailedText;
    loggerWarn(
      loggerSource,
      warningText,
      response.error || null
    );
    setBackendResult(response);
    return false;
  }

  setBackendResult(response.result || {});
  await refreshBackendProjects();
  return true;
}

export function resolveBackendCommandFailurePresentation({
  errorCode,
  errorCodes,
  text
}) {
  const normalizedErrorCode = String(errorCode || '').trim();
  if (!normalizedErrorCode) {
    return {
      lockErrorCode: '',
      warningText: text.backendCommandFailed
    };
  }

  if (normalizedErrorCode === errorCodes.projectLocked) {
    return {
      lockErrorCode: errorCodes.projectLocked,
      warningText: text.backendProjectLocked
    };
  }

  if (normalizedErrorCode === errorCodes.lostProjectLock) {
    return {
      lockErrorCode: errorCodes.lostProjectLock,
      warningText: text.backendProjectLockLost
    };
  }

  if (normalizedErrorCode === errorCodes.activeProcessBusy) {
    return {
      lockErrorCode: '',
      warningText: text.backendActiveProcessBusy
    };
  }

  return {
    lockErrorCode: '',
    warningText: text.backendCommandFailed
  };
}

export function resolveBackendProjectForExportFromCurrentProject({
  currentProject,
  backendSource
}) {
  if (!currentProject || currentProject.source !== backendSource) {
    return null;
  }

  const backendProject = currentProject.backendProject || {};
  const projectId = String(
    backendProject.id
    || backendProject.projectId
    || currentProject.project?.id
    || ''
  ).trim();
  if (!projectId) {
    return null;
  }

  return {
    ...backendProject,
    id: projectId
  };
}

export function resolvePlatformActionEnabledState({
  actionId,
  actionIds,
  currentProject,
  backendSource
}) {
  const hasProject = Boolean(currentProject);
  const exportProject = resolveBackendProjectForExportFromCurrentProject({
    currentProject,
    backendSource
  });

  if (actionId === actionIds.closeWorkspaceProject) {
    return hasProject;
  }
  if (
    actionId === actionIds.saveWorkspaceProject
    || actionId === actionIds.saveWorkspaceProjectAs
    || actionId === actionIds.exportWorkspaceProject
  ) {
    return Boolean(exportProject);
  }

  return true;
}

      baseUrl: APP_CONFIG.platform.backend.baseUrl,

      importEndpointPath: APP_CONFIG.platform.backend.projectImportsEndpoint,
      timeoutMs: APP_CONFIG.platform.backend.requestTimeoutMs,
      defaultHeaders: {
        [APP_CONFIG.platform.backend.userIdentity.headerName]: APP_CONFIG.platform.backend.userIdentity.userId
      },
      errorCodes: {
        internal: APP_CONFIG.platform.backend.commandContract.errorCodes.internal
      },
      importArchiveFieldName: APP_CONFIG.platform.backend.importContract.archiveFieldName
    })
  });

  let projectManager = null;
  const getProjectManager = () => projectManager;

  const metaGenModule = createMetaGenModule({ logger, getProjectManager });
  const metaLabModule = createMetaLabModule({ logger, getProjectManager });
  const metaViewModule = createMetaViewModule({ logger, getProjectManager });

  moduleRegistry.registerModule(metaGenModule);
  moduleRegistry.registerModule(metaLabModule);
  moduleRegistry.registerModule(metaViewModule);

  const paramsUndoButton = document.getElementById(APP_CONFIG.ui.dom.paramsUndoButtonId);
  const paramsRedoButton = document.getElementById(APP_CONFIG.ui.dom.paramsRedoButtonId);
  let disposeParamsUndoRedoSubscription = null;

  const tabs = createWorkbenchTabs({
    logger,
    onActiveEntryChanged: () => {
      disposeParamsUndoRedoSubscription?.();
      disposeParamsUndoRedoSubscription = null;

      const runtime = tabs.getActiveRuntime?.();
      if (typeof runtime?.subscribeParamsUndoRedoState === 'function') {
        disposeParamsUndoRedoSubscription = runtime.subscribeParamsUndoRedoState(() => {
          updateParamsUndoRedoButtonsState();
        });
      }

      updateParamsUndoRedoButtonsState();
    },
    projectManager: {
      renameDocument: async (...args) => projectManager?.renameDocument(...args),
      replaceDocumentRecord: async (...args) => projectManager?.replaceDocumentRecord(...args)
    },
    openEditor: async ({ documentRecord, mountElement }) => {
      const module = moduleRegistry.findModuleByDocumentKind(documentRecord.document?.kind);

      if (!module) {
        throw new Error(`Не найден модуль для kind=${documentRecord.document?.kind}`);
      }

      const runtime = await module.openDocument({
        documentRecord,
        mountElement,
        onDirty: () => projectManager?.markDocumentDirty(getDocumentIdentityKey(documentRecord))
      });

      decorateEditorPanelHeaders(mountElement);
      return runtime;
    }
  });

  function decorateEditorPanelHeaders(rootNode) {
    const headerIconByLabel = new Map([
      [APP_CONFIG.ui.panelHeaders.params, APP_CONFIG.ui.panelHeaderIcons.params],
      [APP_CONFIG.ui.panelHeaders.data, APP_CONFIG.ui.panelHeaderIcons.data],
      [APP_CONFIG.ui.panelHeaders.code, APP_CONFIG.ui.panelHeaderIcons.code],
      [METAGEN_CONFIG.ui.panelHeaders.instances, METAGEN_CONFIG.ui.panelHeaderIcons.instances]
    ]);
    const headerSelector = `.${APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.editorPanelHeader}`;
    const headerNodes = rootNode.querySelectorAll?.(headerSelector) || [];

    for (const headerNode of headerNodes) {
      const normalizedText = String(headerNode.textContent || '').trim();
      const iconAssetPath = headerIconByLabel.get(normalizedText);
      if (!iconAssetPath) {
        continue;
      }

      setNodeIconAndText(headerNode, {
        iconAssetPath,
        labelText: normalizedText,
        textClassName: APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.panelHeaderText
      });
    }
  }

  const backendCatalogNode = document.getElementById(APP_CONFIG.ui.dom.backendPanelId);
  const backendListButton = document.getElementById(APP_CONFIG.ui.dom.backendListButtonId);
  const backendImportButton = document.getElementById(APP_CONFIG.ui.dom.backendImportButtonId);
  const backendCreateInput = document.getElementById(APP_CONFIG.ui.dom.backendCreateInputId);
  const backendCreateButton = document.getElementById(APP_CONFIG.ui.dom.backendCreateButtonId);
  const backendStatusNode = document.getElementById(APP_CONFIG.ui.dom.backendStatusId);
  const backendStatusLabelNode = document.getElementById(APP_CONFIG.ui.dom.backendStatusLabelId);
  const backendListNode = document.getElementById(APP_CONFIG.ui.dom.backendListId);
  const backendListLabelNode = document.getElementById(APP_CONFIG.ui.dom.backendListLabelId);
  const backendEmptyStateNode = document.getElementById(APP_CONFIG.ui.dom.backendEmptyStateId);
  const backendTitleNode = document.getElementById(APP_CONFIG.ui.dom.backendTitleId);
  const backendSubtitleNode = document.getElementById(APP_CONFIG.ui.dom.backendSubtitleId);
  const processPanelNode = document.getElementById(APP_CONFIG.ui.dom.processPanelId);
  const processTitleNode = document.getElementById(APP_CONFIG.ui.dom.processTitleId);
  const processContextNode = document.getElementById(APP_CONFIG.ui.dom.processContextId);
  const processGenerateButton = document.getElementById(APP_CONFIG.ui.dom.processGenerateButtonId);
  const processStopButton = document.getElementById(APP_CONFIG.ui.dom.processStopButtonId);
  const processCommandLabelNode = document.getElementById(APP_CONFIG.ui.dom.processCommandLabelId);

  const processStatusLabelNode = document.getElementById(APP_CONFIG.ui.dom.processStatusLabelId);
  const processStatusNode = document.getElementById(APP_CONFIG.ui.dom.processStatusId);

  const platformActionBrowseWorkspaceProjectsButton = document.getElementById(APP_CONFIG.ui.dom.platformActionBrowseWorkspaceProjectsButtonId);
  const platformActionCloseWorkspaceProjectButton = document.getElementById(APP_CONFIG.ui.dom.platformActionCloseWorkspaceProjectButtonId);
  const platformActionSaveWorkspaceProjectButton = document.getElementById(APP_CONFIG.ui.dom.platformActionSaveWorkspaceProjectButtonId);
  const platformActionSaveWorkspaceProjectAsButton = document.getElementById(APP_CONFIG.ui.dom.platformActionSaveWorkspaceProjectAsButtonId);
  const platformActionImportWorkspaceProjectButton = document.getElementById(APP_CONFIG.ui.dom.platformActionImportWorkspaceProjectButtonId);
  const platformActionExportWorkspaceProjectButton = document.getElementById(APP_CONFIG.ui.dom.platformActionExportWorkspaceProjectButtonId);
  const platformActionExitButton = document.getElementById(APP_CONFIG.ui.dom.platformActionExitButtonId);
  const platformActionIds = APP_CONFIG.platform.app.platformActions.ids;

  const platformActionLoggerSource = APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.platformActions.loggerSource;
  const platformActionDispatchMessages = APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.platformActions.dispatchMessages;
  const platformActionTransitionPrefix = APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.transitionReasons.webActionPrefix;
  const webSurfacePlatformActionOrder = APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.platformActions.webSurfaceActionOrder;
  const webSurfacePlatformActionDomByActionId = APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.platformActions.webSurfaceDomByActionId;
  const platformActionLabels = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.platformActionLabels;
  const platformActionAriaLabels = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.platformActionAriaLabels;
  const platformActionDisabledHints = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.platformActionDisabledHints;
  const platformActionStatusMessages = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.platformActionStatusMessages;
  const platformActionButtonsById = new Map([
    [platformActionIds.createWorkspaceProject, platformActionCreateWorkspaceProjectButton],
    [platformActionIds.browseWorkspaceProjects, platformActionBrowseWorkspaceProjectsButton],
    [platformActionIds.closeWorkspaceProject, platformActionCloseWorkspaceProjectButton],
    [platformActionIds.saveWorkspaceProject, platformActionSaveWorkspaceProjectButton],
    [platformActionIds.saveWorkspaceProjectAs, platformActionSaveWorkspaceProjectAsButton],
    [platformActionIds.importWorkspaceProject, platformActionImportWorkspaceProjectButton],
    [platformActionIds.exportWorkspaceProject, platformActionExportWorkspaceProjectButton],
    [platformActionIds.exit, platformActionExitButton]
  ]);
  const backendStartupListStrategies = APP_CONFIG.platform.backend.startup.initialProjectListStrategies;
  const backendStartupListStrategy = APP_CONFIG.platform.backend.startup.initialProjectListStrategy;
  const backendListRefreshReasons = APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.backendWorkspaceStartup.listRefreshReasons;
  const backendLockReleaseStates = APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.backendLockLifecycle.releaseResultStates;
  const processRuntimeConfig = APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.processExecution;
  const processCommandIds = APP_CONFIG.platform.backend.commandContract.commands;
  const processStatusByCode = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.processStatusByCode;
  let isBackendWorkspaceBrowserVisible = !backendCatalogNode?.hidden;
  let backendRequestCounter = 0;

  if (backendCatalogNode) {
    backendCatalogNode.classList.add(APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.backendPanel);
  }

  if (backendTitleNode) {
    backendTitleNode.classList.add(APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.backendPanelTitle);
    backendTitleNode.textContent = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendProjectsTitle;
  }

  if (backendSubtitleNode) {
    backendSubtitleNode.classList.add(APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.backendPanelSubtitle);
    backendSubtitleNode.textContent = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendProjectsSubtitle;
  }

  if (backendStatusLabelNode) {
    backendStatusLabelNode.classList.add(APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.backendPanelStatusLabel);
    backendStatusLabelNode.textContent = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendProjectsStatusLabel;
  }

  if (backendListLabelNode) {
    backendListLabelNode.classList.add(APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.backendPanelListLabel);
    backendListLabelNode.textContent = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendProjectsListLabel;
  }

  if (backendEmptyStateNode) {
    backendEmptyStateNode.classList.add(APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.backendPanelEmptyState);
    backendEmptyStateNode.textContent = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendProjectsEmptyState;
  }

  if (backendListButton) {
    backendListButton.textContent = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendListProjects;
  }

  if (backendCreateInput) {
    backendCreateInput.placeholder = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendProjectPlaceholder;
  }

  if (backendImportButton) {
    backendImportButton.textContent = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendImportProject;
  }

  if (backendCreateButton) {
    backendCreateButton.textContent = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendCreateProject;
  }

  if (platformActionSurfaceNode) {
    platformActionSurfaceNode.classList.add(APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.platformActionSurface);
  }

  for (const actionId of webSurfacePlatformActionOrder) {
    const expectedDomId = webSurfacePlatformActionDomByActionId[actionId];
    const buttonNode = platformActionButtonsById.get(actionId);
    if (!buttonNode || buttonNode.id !== expectedDomId) {
      continue;
    }
    buttonNode.classList.add(APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.platformActionButton);
    buttonNode.textContent = platformActionLabels[actionId] || '';
    buttonNode.setAttribute('aria-label', platformActionAriaLabels[actionId] || '');
  }

  let platformActionSurfaceStateVersion = 0;
  function updatePlatformActionSurfaceState() {
    for (const actionId of webSurfacePlatformActionOrder) {
      const buttonNode = platformActionButtonsById.get(actionId);
      if (!buttonNode) {
        continue;
      }

      const isEnabled = resolvePlatformActionEnabledState({
        actionId,
        actionIds: platformActionIds,
        currentProject: projectManager?.getCurrentProject?.() || null,
        backendSource: APP_CONFIG.project.sources.backend
      });
      buttonNode.disabled = !isEnabled;
      if (!isEnabled) {
        buttonNode.title = platformActionDisabledHints[actionId] || '';
      } else {
        buttonNode.removeAttribute('title');
      }
    }
    platformActionSurfaceStateVersion += 1;
  }
  updatePlatformActionSurfaceState();

  if (processPanelNode) {
    processPanelNode.classList.add(APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.processPanel);
  }

  if (processTitleNode) {
    processTitleNode.classList.add(APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.processPanelTitle);
    processTitleNode.textContent = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.processPanelTitle;
  }

  if (processContextNode) {
    processContextNode.classList.add(APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.processPanelContext);
  }

  if (processCommandLabelNode) {
    processCommandLabelNode.classList.add(APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.processPanelMetaLabel);
    processCommandLabelNode.textContent = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.processMetaCommandLabel;
  }

  if (processStatusLabelNode) {
    processStatusLabelNode.classList.add(APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.processPanelMetaLabel);
    processStatusLabelNode.textContent = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.processMetaStatusLabel;
  }

  if (processExitCodeLabelNode) {
    processExitCodeLabelNode.classList.add(APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.processPanelMetaLabel);
    processExitCodeLabelNode.textContent = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.processMetaExitCodeLabel;
  }

  if (processGenerateButton) {
    processGenerateButton.classList.add(APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.processPanelActionPrimary);
    processGenerateButton.textContent = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.processGenerateButton;
  }

  if (processStopButton) {
    processStopButton.classList.add(APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.processPanelActionSecondary);
    processStopButton.textContent = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.processStopButton;
  }

  processCommandNode?.classList.add(APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.processPanelMetaValue);
  processStatusNode?.classList.add(APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.processPanelMetaValue);
  processExitCodeNode?.classList.add(APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.processPanelMetaValue);
  processOutputNode?.classList.add(APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.processPanelOutput);

  function setBackendResult(value) {
    if (!backendStatusNode) {
      return;
    }

    backendStatusNode.replaceChildren(
      typeof value === 'string'
        ? document.createTextNode(value)
        : document.createTextNode(JSON.stringify(value, null, 2))
    );
  }

  function setBackendEmptyStateVisible(isVisible) {
    if (backendEmptyStateNode) {
      backendEmptyStateNode.hidden = !isVisible;
    }
  }

  function setBackendEmptyStateMessage(message) {
    if (!backendEmptyStateNode) {
      return;
    }

    backendEmptyStateNode.textContent = message;
  }

  function resolveProcessContextProjectId() {
    return getCurrentBackendProjectId({
      projectManager,
      backendSource: APP_CONFIG.project.sources.backend
    });
  }

  function resolveProcessStatusText(status) {
    const normalizedStatus = String(status || '').trim();
    if (!normalizedStatus) {
      return APP_CONFIG.ui.text.processNone;
    }

    return processStatusByCode[normalizedStatus] || APP_CONFIG.ui.text.processUnknownStatus;
  }

  function resolveProcessModuleText(commandId) {
    const command = String(commandId || '').trim();
    if (!command) {
      return APP_CONFIG.ui.text.processNotAvailable;
    }

    const moduleLabel = processRuntimeConfig.commandModuleByCommand[command];
    return moduleLabel ? `${moduleLabel}.${command}` : command;
  }

  function isTerminalProcessStatus(status) {
    const normalizedStatus = String(status || '').trim();
    return processRuntimeConfig.terminalStatuses.includes(normalizedStatus);
  }

  function isStoppableProcessStatus(status) {
    const normalizedStatus = String(status || '').trim();
    return processRuntimeConfig.stoppableStatuses.includes(normalizedStatus);
  }

  function resolveProcessStreamLabel(streamName) {
    const normalizedStream = String(streamName || '').trim();
    return processRuntimeConfig.streamLabels[normalizedStream] || processRuntimeConfig.streamLabels.system;
  }

  function resolveProcessOutputLineClassName(streamName) {
    const normalizedStream = String(streamName || '').trim();
    if (normalizedStream === APP_CONFIG.platform.backend.commandContract.process.streams.stderr) {
      return APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.processPanelOutputLineStderr;
    }
    if (normalizedStream === APP_CONFIG.platform.backend.commandContract.process.streams.stdout) {
      return APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.processPanelOutputLineStdout;
    }
    return APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.processPanelOutputLineSystem;
  }

  const processViewState = {
    process: null,
    outputChunks: []
  };
  let processExecutionOrchestrator = null;

  function renderProcessPanel() {
    const contextProjectId = resolveProcessContextProjectId();
    const hasBackendContext = Boolean(contextProjectId);
    const process = processViewState.process;
    const status = String(process?.status || '').trim();
    const command = String(process?.command || '').trim();
    const stopAvailable = process && isStoppableProcessStatus(status);
    const terminalStatus = process && isTerminalProcessStatus(status);

    if (processContextNode) {
      processContextNode.textContent = hasBackendContext
        ? `${APP_CONFIG.ui.text.processContextReadyPrefix}: ${contextProjectId}`
        : APP_CONFIG.ui.text.processContextMissing;
    }

    if (processCommandNode) {
      processCommandNode.textContent = process
        ? resolveProcessModuleText(command)
        : APP_CONFIG.ui.text.processNotAvailable;
    }

    if (processStatusNode) {
      processStatusNode.textContent = resolveProcessStatusText(status);
    }

    if (processExitCodeNode) {
      processExitCodeNode.textContent = terminalStatus
        ? String(process?.exitCode ?? APP_CONFIG.ui.text.processNotAvailable)
        : APP_CONFIG.ui.text.processNotAvailable;
    }

    if (processGenerateButton) {
      const canGenerate = hasBackendContext && !stopAvailable;
      processGenerateButton.disabled = !canGenerate;
      processGenerateButton.classList.toggle(APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.processPanelActionDisabled, !canGenerate);
    }

    if (processStopButton) {
      const canStop = Boolean(stopAvailable);
      processStopButton.disabled = !canStop;
      processStopButton.classList.toggle(APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.processPanelActionDisabled, !canStop);
    }

    if (!processOutputNode) {
      return;
    }

    processOutputNode.replaceChildren();

    if (!processViewState.outputChunks.length) {
      processOutputNode.appendChild(document.createTextNode(APP_CONFIG.ui.text.processOutputEmpty));
      return;
    }

    for (const chunk of processViewState.outputChunks) {
      const lineNode = document.createElement('span');
      lineNode.classList.add(APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.processPanelOutputLine);
      lineNode.classList.add(resolveProcessOutputLineClassName(chunk?.stream));
      lineNode.textContent = `[${resolveProcessStreamLabel(chunk?.stream)}] ${String(chunk?.content || '')}`;
      processOutputNode.appendChild(lineNode);
      processOutputNode.appendChild(document.createTextNode('\n'));
    }
    processOutputNode.scrollTop = processOutputNode.scrollHeight;
  }

  function buildBackendProjectButton({
    text,
    className,
    title = '',
    disabled = false,
    ariaLabel = '',
    onClick
  }) {
    const button = document.createElement('button');
    button.type = 'button';
    button.classList.add(className);
    button.textContent = text;
    button.disabled = disabled;
    if (disabled) {
      button.classList.add(APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.backendBrowserButtonDisabled);
    }
    if (title) {
      button.title = title;
    }
    if (ariaLabel) {
      button.setAttribute('aria-label', ariaLabel);
    }
    button.addEventListener('click', () => {
      onClick?.();
    });
    return button;
  }

  function renderBackendProjects(projects = []) {
    if (!backendListNode) {
      return;
    }

    backendListNode.replaceChildren();

    if (!Array.isArray(projects) || projects.length === 0) {
      setBackendEmptyStateMessage(APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendProjectsEmptyState);
      setBackendEmptyStateVisible(true);
      return;
    }
    setBackendEmptyStateVisible(false);
    const currentUserId = APP_CONFIG.platform.backend.userIdentity.userId;

    for (const project of projects) {
      const projectPresentation = getBackendProjectCatalogPresentation({
        project,
        currentUserId,
        text: APP_CONFIG.ui.text
      });
      const projectId = String(project?.id || '').trim();
      const item = document.createElement('article');
      const mainRow = document.createElement('div');
      const identityNode = document.createElement('div');
      const nameNode = document.createElement('div');
      const slugNode = document.createElement('div');
      const lockNode = document.createElement('div');
      const primaryActions = document.createElement('div');
      const secondaryActions = document.createElement('div');

      item.classList.add(APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.backendBrowserItem);
      mainRow.classList.add(APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.backendBrowserItemMain);
      identityNode.classList.add(APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.backendBrowserIdentity);
      nameNode.classList.add(APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.backendBrowserName);
      slugNode.classList.add(APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.backendBrowserSlug);
      lockNode.classList.add(APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.backendBrowserLock);
      primaryActions.classList.add(APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.backendBrowserItemPrimaryActions);
      secondaryActions.classList.add(APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.backendBrowserItemSecondaryActions);

      nameNode.textContent = `${APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendProjectNameLabel}: ${projectPresentation.projectName || projectId}`;
      slugNode.textContent = `${APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendProjectSlugLabel}: ${projectPresentation.projectSlug || '-'}`;
      lockNode.textContent = `${APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendProjectLockLabel}: ${projectPresentation.lockText}`;

      const openButton = buildBackendProjectButton({
        text: APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendOpenProject,
        className: APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.backendBrowserPrimaryButton,
        title: projectPresentation.openTitle,
        disabled: projectPresentation.openDisabled,
        ariaLabel: `${APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendOpenProjectAriaPrefix}: ${projectPresentation.projectName || projectId}`,
        onClick: () => {
          void openBackendProject(project);
        }
      });

      const exportButton = buildBackendProjectButton({
        text: APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendExportProject,
        className: APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.backendBrowserSecondaryButton,
        onClick: () => {
          void exportBackendProject(project);
        }
      });

      const deleteButton = buildBackendProjectButton({
        text: APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendDeleteProject,
        className: APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.backendBrowserSecondaryButton,
        onClick: () => {
          void deleteBackendProject(project);
        }
      });

      identityNode.append(nameNode, slugNode, lockNode);
      primaryActions.appendChild(openButton);
      mainRow.append(identityNode, primaryActions);
      secondaryActions.append(exportButton, deleteButton);
      item.append(mainRow, secondaryActions);
      backendListNode.appendChild(item);
    }
  }

  const startupIdlePresentation = resolveBackendWorkspaceStartupIdlePresentation({
    text: APP_CONFIG.ui.text
  });
  setBackendResult(startupIdlePresentation.statusText);
  setBackendEmptyStateMessage(startupIdlePresentation.emptyStateText);
  setBackendEmptyStateVisible(startupIdlePresentation.isEmptyStateVisible);
  isBackendWorkspaceBrowserVisible = applyBackendWorkspaceBrowserPresentationState({
    browserNode: backendCatalogNode,
    hiddenClassName: APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.backendPanelHidden,
    isVisible: isBackendWorkspaceBrowserVisible
  });

  function nextBackendRequestId() {
    backendRequestCounter += 1;
    return `${APP_CONFIG.platform.backend.requestIdPrefix}${backendRequestCounter}`;
  }

  const backendCommandSessionOrchestrator = createBackendCommandSessionOrchestrator({
    backendRuntimeClient,
    nextBackendRequestId,
    getProjectManager: () => projectManager,
    resolveBackendCommandFailurePresentation,
    setBackendResult,
    loggerWarn: (...args) => logger.warn(...args),
    loggerSource: APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.loggerSources.backend,
    backendText: APP_CONFIG.ui.text,
    commandModuleId: APP_CONFIG.platform.backend.commandContract.moduleIds.platform,
    backendCommands: APP_CONFIG.platform.backend.commandContract.commands,
    backendErrorCodes: APP_CONFIG.platform.backend.commandContract.errorCodes,
    backendSource: APP_CONFIG.project.sources.backend,
    backendLockReleaseStates,
    backendHeartbeatIntervalMs: APP_CONFIG.platform.backend.lockSession.heartbeatIntervalMs,
    backendHeartbeatFailedText: APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendHeartbeatFailed,
    backendHeartbeatStopReasonLost: APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.backendLockLifecycle.stopReasonLost,
    backendHeartbeatStopReasonSwitch: APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.backendLockLifecycle.stopReasonSwitch
  });

  function stopBackendHeartbeat(reason = '') {
    backendCommandSessionOrchestrator.stopBackendHeartbeat(reason);
  }

  function handleLostBackendProjectLock() {
    backendCommandSessionOrchestrator.handleLostBackendProjectLock();
  }

  async function executeBackendCommand(command, payload = {}, options = {}) {
    return backendCommandSessionOrchestrator.executeBackendCommand(command, payload, options);
  }

  processExecutionOrchestrator = createProcessExecutionOrchestrator({
    executeBackendCommand: async (command, payload = {}, options = {}) => {
      const commandResult = await executeBackendCommand(command, payload, options);
      return commandResult?.ok ? (commandResult.result || null) : null;
    },
    commandIds: {
      metagenGenerate: processCommandIds.metagenGenerate,
      processGetState: processCommandIds.processGetState,
      processReadOutput: processCommandIds.processReadOutput,
      processStop: processCommandIds.processStop
    },
    terminalStatuses: processRuntimeConfig.terminalStatuses,
    pollingIntervalMs: processRuntimeConfig.pollingIntervalMs,
    onUpdate: (snapshot) => {
      processViewState.process = snapshot.process;
      processViewState.outputChunks = Array.isArray(snapshot.outputChunks)
        ? snapshot.outputChunks
        : [];
      renderProcessPanel();
    }
  });

  const metagenGeneratorBridge = createMetaGenGeneratorBridge({
    launchGenerate: (payload) => processExecutionOrchestrator.launchGenerate(payload)
  });

  async function syncProcessSurfaceWithContext() {
    const contextProjectId = resolveProcessContextProjectId();
    if (!contextProjectId) {
      processExecutionOrchestrator?.clearSnapshot?.();
      return;
    }
    await processExecutionOrchestrator.syncActiveProcess();
  }

  async function runMetagenGenerate() {
    const contextProjectId = resolveProcessContextProjectId();
    if (!contextProjectId) {
      processExecutionOrchestrator.clearSnapshot();
      return;
    }
    await metagenGeneratorBridge.generate({});
  }

  async function stopActiveProcess() {
    await processExecutionOrchestrator.stopProcess();
  }

  processGenerateButton?.addEventListener('click', () => {
    void runMetagenGenerate();
  });

  processStopButton?.addEventListener('click', () => {
    void stopActiveProcess();
  });

  renderProcessPanel();
  void syncProcessSurfaceWithContext();

  async function openBackendProject(project) {
    const projectId = String(project?.id || '').trim();
    if (!projectId) {
      return;
    }

    const canContinue = await confirmSaveIfDirty();
    if (canContinue === APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.closeFlowDecisions.cancel) {
      return;
    }

    const releaseResult = await releaseBackendProjectLockIfNeeded({
      reason: APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.backendLockLifecycle.stopReasonSwitch
    });
    if (!releaseResult?.canContinue) {
      return;
    }

    const commandResult = await executeBackendCommand(
      APP_CONFIG.platform.backend.commandContract.commands.openProject,
      { projectId }
    );

    if (!commandResult?.ok || !commandResult?.result?.snapshot || !commandResult?.result?.lockToken) {
      return;
    }

    await tabs.closeAllTabs();
    logger.clear();
    await projectManager.openProjectSnapshot(commandResult.result.snapshot, { lockToken: commandResult.result.lockToken });
    await tree.render();
    startBackendHeartbeatIfNeeded(APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.backendLockLifecycle.startReasonOpen);
  }

  async function releaseBackendProjectLockIfNeeded({ reason = '' } = {}) {
    return backendCommandSessionOrchestrator.releaseBackendProjectLockIfNeeded({ reason });
  }

  function startBackendHeartbeatIfNeeded(reason = '') {
    backendCommandSessionOrchestrator.startBackendHeartbeatIfNeeded(reason);
  }

  async function exportBackendProject(project) {
    await runBackendProjectExport({
      project,
      exportCommandId: APP_CONFIG.platform.backend.commandContract.commands.exportProject,
      executeBackendCommand: async (command, payload, options = {}) => {
        const commandResult = await executeBackendCommand(command, payload, options);
        return commandResult?.ok ? (commandResult.result || null) : null;
      },
      downloadBinary: (downloadUrl) => backendRuntimeClient.downloadBinary(downloadUrl),
      saveBinaryFileAsDialog: (payload) => shell.requestBinarySaveAs(payload),
      dialogs: APP_CONFIG.platform.app.dialogs,
      loggerWarn: (...args) => logger.warn(...args),
      loggerSource: APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.loggerSources.backend,
      downloadFailedText: APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendExportDownloadFailed,
      setResult: setBackendResult
    });
  }

  async function refreshBackendProjects({ reason = backendListRefreshReasons.userAction } = {}) {
    void reason;
    setBackendResult(APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendProjectsStatusLoading);
    const commandResult = await executeBackendCommand(APP_CONFIG.platform.backend.commandContract.commands.listProjects);
    const refreshPresentation = resolveBackendWorkspaceListRefreshPresentation({
      result: commandResult?.ok ? commandResult.result : null,
      text: APP_CONFIG.ui.text
    });
    if (refreshPresentation.isUnavailable) {
      setBackendResult(refreshPresentation.statusText);
      setBackendEmptyStateMessage(refreshPresentation.emptyStateText);
      setBackendEmptyStateVisible(refreshPresentation.isEmptyStateVisible);
      return;
    }
    renderBackendProjects(refreshPresentation.projects);
    setBackendResult(refreshPresentation.statusText);
  }

  function setBackendWorkspaceBrowserVisible(isVisible) {
    isBackendWorkspaceBrowserVisible = applyBackendWorkspaceBrowserPresentationState({
      browserNode: backendCatalogNode,
      hiddenClassName: APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.backendPanelHidden,
      isVisible
    });
    return isBackendWorkspaceBrowserVisible;
  }

  function revealBackendWorkspaceBrowser() {
    if (isBackendWorkspaceBrowserVisible) {
      return;
    }
    setBackendWorkspaceBrowserVisible(true);
  }

  function focusBackendWorkspaceBrowserEntry() {
    backendCatalogNode?.scrollIntoView?.({ block: 'nearest' });
    const focusTarget = resolveBackendWorkspaceEntryFocusTarget({
      backendListButton,
      backendCreateInput,
      backendCatalogNode
    });
    focusTarget?.focus?.();
  }

  function focusBackendWorkspaceBrowserCreateInput({ clearInput = false } = {}) {
    backendCatalogNode?.scrollIntoView?.({ block: 'nearest' });
    if (!backendCreateInput) {
      focusBackendWorkspaceBrowserEntry();
      return;
    }
    if (clearInput) {
      backendCreateInput.value = '';
    }
    backendCreateInput.focus();
    backendCreateInput.select?.();
  }

  async function presentBackendWorkspaceBrowser({
    refreshProjects = false,
    refreshReason = backendListRefreshReasons.userAction
  } = {}) {
    revealBackendWorkspaceBrowser();
    focusBackendWorkspaceBrowserEntry();
    if (refreshProjects) {
      await refreshBackendProjects({ reason: refreshReason });
    }
  }

  async function presentBackendWorkspaceBrowserForCreateFirst({
    refreshProjects = true,
    clearCreateInput = false,
    refreshReason = backendListRefreshReasons.userAction
  } = {}) {
    revealBackendWorkspaceBrowser();
    focusBackendWorkspaceBrowserCreateInput({ clearInput: clearCreateInput });
    if (refreshProjects) {
      await refreshBackendProjects({ reason: refreshReason });
      focusBackendWorkspaceBrowserCreateInput({ clearInput: false });
    }
  }

  function shouldStartupRefreshBackendProjects() {
    return resolveBackendWorkspaceStartupRefreshDecision({
      startupListStrategy: backendStartupListStrategy,
      startupListStrategies: backendStartupListStrategies
    });
  }

  async function deleteBackendProject(project) {
    await deleteBackendProjectFlow({
      project,
      confirmDelete: window.confirm,
      confirmPrefix: APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendDeleteConfirmPrefix,
      deleteCommandId: APP_CONFIG.platform.backend.commandContract.commands.deleteProject,
      executeBackendCommand,
      closeDeletedProject: async (projectId) => closeDeletedBackendProjectIfOpened({
        projectId,
        projectManager,
        backendSource: APP_CONFIG.project.sources.backend,
        tabs,
        logger,
        tree,
        onBeforeClose: async () => {
          stopBackendHeartbeat(APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.backendLockLifecycle.stopReasonDelete);
          projectManager?.clearBackendLockToken?.();
        }
      }),
      refreshBackendProjects: () => refreshBackendProjects({ reason: backendListRefreshReasons.delete })
    });
  }

  async function importBackendProject() {
    await importBackendProjectFlow({
      openProjectImportArchiveDialog: () => shell.requestProjectImportArchive(),
      importProjectArchive: (payload) => backendRuntimeClient.importProjectArchive(payload),
      refreshBackendProjects: () => refreshBackendProjects({ reason: backendListRefreshReasons.import }),
      setBackendResult,
      loggerWarn: (...args) => logger.warn(...args),
      loggerSource: APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.loggerSources.backend,
      backendImportFailedText: APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendImportFailed,
      backendActiveProcessBusyText: APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendActiveProcessBusy,
      activeProcessBusyErrorCode: APP_CONFIG.platform.backend.commandContract.errorCodes.activeProcessBusy
    });
  }

  backendListButton?.addEventListener('click', () => {
    void refreshBackendProjects({ reason: backendListRefreshReasons.userAction });
  });

  backendImportButton?.addEventListener('click', () => {
    void importBackendProject();
  });

  async function createBackendProject() {
    const name = String(backendCreateInput?.value || '').trim();
    if (!name) {
      return;
    }

    const commandResult = await executeBackendCommand(
      APP_CONFIG.platform.backend.commandContract.commands.createProject,
      { name }
    );
    if (commandResult?.ok && commandResult?.result?.project) {
      if (backendCreateInput) {
        backendCreateInput.value = '';
      }
      await refreshBackendProjects({ reason: backendListRefreshReasons.create });
    }
  }

  backendCreateButton?.addEventListener('click', () => {
    void createBackendProject();
  });

  backendCreateInput?.addEventListener('keydown', (event) => {
    if (event.key !== 'Enter') {
      return;
    }
    event.preventDefault();
    void createBackendProject();
  });

  function getActiveParamsUndoRedoState() {
    const runtime = tabs.getActiveRuntime?.();
    if (!runtime?.supportsParamsUndoRedo?.()) {
      return {
        runtime: null,
        supported: false,
        isContextActive: false,
        canUndo: false,
        canRedo: false
      };
    }

    const state = runtime.getParamsUndoRedoState?.();
    const isContextActive = Boolean(
      state?.isContextActive
      ?? state?.isParamsUndoRedoContextActive
      ?? state?.isHotkeyContextActive
      ?? runtime?.isParamsUndoRedoContextActive?.()
    );

    return {
      runtime,
      supported: Boolean(state?.supported ?? true),
      isContextActive,
      canUndo: Boolean(state?.canUndo ?? runtime?.canUndoParams?.()),
      canRedo: Boolean(state?.canRedo ?? runtime?.canRedoParams?.())
    };
  }

  function updateParamsUndoRedoButtonsState() {
    if (!paramsUndoButton || !paramsRedoButton) {
      return;
    }

    const state = getActiveParamsUndoRedoState();

    paramsUndoButton.disabled = !state.supported || !state.isContextActive || !state.canUndo;
    paramsRedoButton.disabled = !state.supported || !state.isContextActive || !state.canRedo;
  }

  async function triggerParamsUndo() {
    const state = getActiveParamsUndoRedoState();
    if (!state.runtime || !state.supported || !state.isContextActive || !state.canUndo) {
      updateParamsUndoRedoButtonsState();
      return;
    }

    await state.runtime.undoParams?.();
    updateParamsUndoRedoButtonsState();
  }

  async function triggerParamsRedo() {
    const state = getActiveParamsUndoRedoState();
    if (!state.runtime || !state.supported || !state.isContextActive || !state.canRedo) {
      updateParamsUndoRedoButtonsState();
      return;
    }

    await state.runtime.redoParams?.();
    updateParamsUndoRedoButtonsState();
  }

  paramsUndoButton?.addEventListener('click', () => {
    void triggerParamsUndo();
  });

  paramsRedoButton?.addEventListener('click', () => {
    void triggerParamsRedo();
  });

  document.addEventListener('focusin', () => {
    updateParamsUndoRedoButtonsState();
  });
  document.addEventListener('pointerdown', () => {
    updateParamsUndoRedoButtonsState();
  }, true);
  updateParamsUndoRedoButtonsState();


  projectManager = createProjectManager({
    logger,
    runtimeShell: shell,
    moduleRegistry,
    onProjectLoaded: ({ projectRuntime }) => {
      updatePlatformActionSurfaceState();
      void syncProcessSurfaceWithContext();
    },
    onProjectClosed: () => {
      stopBackendHeartbeat(APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.backendLockLifecycle.stopReasonClose);
      processExecutionOrchestrator?.clearSnapshot?.();
      updatePlatformActionSurfaceState();
    }
  });

  async function handleCreateComponentRequest(moduleId) {
    const module = moduleRegistry.getModule(moduleId);

    if (!module) {
      logger.warn(APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.loggerSources.projectTree, 'Не найден модуль для создания компонента', { moduleId });
      return;
    }

    const defaultName = moduleId === APP_CONFIG.project.moduleIds.metagen
      ? projectManager.getNextMetaGenDefaultName()
      : module.getDefaultName?.() || APP_CONFIG.ui.text.untitled;

    await tabs.startTemporaryDocumentCreation({
      moduleId,
      defaultName,
      onCommit: async ({ moduleId: confirmedModuleId, confirmedName }) => {
        return projectManager.createDocument(confirmedModuleId, confirmedName);
      }
    });
  }

  async function handleDeleteComponentRequest(documentRecord) {
    const documentIdentity = getDocumentIdentityKey(documentRecord);
    await projectManager.deleteDocument(documentIdentity);
    await tabs.closeTab(documentIdentity, { skipProjectSync: true });
  }

  const tree = createProjectTree({
    logger,
    projectManager,
    tabs,
    onCreateComponentRequest: handleCreateComponentRequest,
    onDeleteComponentRequest: handleDeleteComponentRequest
  });

  async function finalizeBackendProjectSaveFlow() {
    await tree.render();
    logger.clear();
    return true;
  }

  async function saveBackendProjectFlow(openDocuments) {
    let payload = null;
    try {
      payload = projectManager.buildBackendSavePayload(openDocuments);
    } catch (error) {
      logger.warn(
        APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.loggerSources.backend,
        APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendProjectLockLost,
        { message: error?.message || String(error) }
      );
      return false;
    }
    const commandResult = await executeBackendCommand(
      APP_CONFIG.platform.backend.commandContract.commands.saveAll,
      payload
    );

    if (!commandResult?.ok || !commandResult?.result) {
      return false;
    }

    projectManager.commitBackendSave(commandResult.result?.project || null);
    startBackendHeartbeatIfNeeded(APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.backendLockLifecycle.startReasonOpen);
    return finalizeBackendProjectSaveFlow();
  }

  async function saveBackendProjectAsFlow({ project, openDocuments }) {
    const initialName = String(
      project.backendProject?.name
      || project.project?.name
      || APP_CONFIG.project.defaultProjectName
    ).trim() || APP_CONFIG.project.defaultProjectName;
    const newName = await showTextInputDialog({
      title: APP_CONFIG.platform.app.dialogs.backendWorkspaceSaveProjectAsTitle,
      initialValue: initialName,
      confirmText: APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendWorkspaceSaveProjectAsConfirm,
      cancelText: APP_CONFIG.ui.text.cancel
    });

    if (!newName) {
      return false;
    }

    const payload = projectManager.buildBackendSaveAsPayload(newName, openDocuments);
    const commandResult = await executeBackendCommand(
      APP_CONFIG.platform.backend.commandContract.commands.saveProjectAs,
      payload
    );

    if (!commandResult?.ok || !commandResult?.result?.project || !commandResult?.result?.lockToken) {
      if (commandResult?.ok && !commandResult?.result?.lockToken) {
        logger.warn(
          APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.loggerSources.backend,
          APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendProjectLockLost
        );
        handleLostBackendProjectLock();
      }
      return false;
    }

    projectManager.commitBackendSaveAs({
      ...(commandResult.result?.project || {}),
      lockToken: commandResult.result?.lockToken
    });
    startBackendHeartbeatIfNeeded(APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.backendLockLifecycle.startReasonOpen);
    return finalizeBackendProjectSaveFlow();
  }

  async function saveProjectFlow({ forceSaveAs = false } = {}) {
    const project = projectManager.getCurrentProject();

    if (!project) {
      logger.warn(APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.loggerSources.project, APP_CONFIG.ui.text.noProjectToSave);
      return false;
    }

    if (project.source !== APP_CONFIG.project.sources.backend) {
      logger.warn(APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.loggerSources.project, APP_CONFIG.ui.text.backendSaveRequiresOpenedBackendProject, {
        source: project.source || ''
      });
      return false;
    }

    const openDocuments = await tabs.collectOpenDocumentRecords();
    if (forceSaveAs) {
      return saveBackendProjectAsFlow({ project, openDocuments });
    }

    return saveBackendProjectFlow(openDocuments);
  }

  async function confirmSaveIfDirty() {
    if (!projectManager.hasDirtyProject()) {
      return APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.closeFlowDecisions.continue;
    }

    const decision = await showSaveChangesDialog({
      title: APP_CONFIG.ui.text.saveChangesTitle
    });

    if (decision === APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.dialogResults.cancel) {
      return APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.closeFlowDecisions.cancel;
    }

    if (decision === APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.dialogResults.discard) {
      return APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.closeFlowDecisions.continue;
    }

    const saved = await saveProjectFlow();
    return saved
      ? APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.closeFlowDecisions.continue
      : APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.closeFlowDecisions.cancel;
  }

  async function newProjectFlow() {
    await runNewProjectCreateFirstTransition({
      confirmSaveIfDirty,
      cancelDecision: APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.closeFlowDecisions.cancel,
      releaseBackendProjectLockIfNeeded,
      stopReasonSwitch: APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.backendLockLifecycle.stopReasonSwitch,
      closeAllTabs: () => tabs.closeAllTabs(),
      clearLogs: () => logger.clear(),
      closeProject: () => projectManager.closeProject(),
      presentBackendWorkspaceBrowserForCreateFirst
    });
  }

  async function openProjectFlow() {
    await presentBackendWorkspaceBrowser({ refreshProjects: true });
  }

  async function closeProjectFlow() {
    await runCloseProjectTransition({
      getCurrentProject: () => projectManager.getCurrentProject(),
      confirmSaveIfDirty,
      cancelDecision: APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.closeFlowDecisions.cancel,
      releaseBackendProjectLockIfNeeded,
      stopReasonClose: APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.backendLockLifecycle.stopReasonClose,
      closeAllTabs: () => tabs.closeAllTabs(),
      clearLogs: () => logger.clear(),
      closeProject: () => projectManager.closeProject(),
      presentBackendWorkspaceBrowser
    });
  }

  const appCloseCoordinator = createAppCloseCoordinator({
    confirmSaveIfDirty,
    requestAppQuit: () => shell.requestApplicationExit(),
    approveWindowClose: () => shell.approveCloseIntent(),
    cancelWindowClose: () => shell.cancelCloseIntent()
  });

  async function exitFlow() {
    await appCloseCoordinator.requestExit();
  }

  function resolveCurrentBackendProjectForExport() {
    return resolveBackendProjectForExportFromCurrentProject({
      currentProject: projectManager?.getCurrentProject?.() || null,
      backendSource: APP_CONFIG.project.sources.backend
    });
  }

  async function exportWorkspaceProjectFlow() {
    const projectForExport = resolveCurrentBackendProjectForExport();
    if (!projectForExport) {
      await presentBackendWorkspaceBrowser({ refreshProjects: false });
      setBackendResult(platformActionStatusMessages[platformActionIds.exportWorkspaceProject] || '');
      return false;
    }

    return exportBackendProject(projectForExport);
  }

  const platformActionHandlers = new Map([
    [platformActionIds.createWorkspaceProject, async () => newProjectFlow()],
    [platformActionIds.browseWorkspaceProjects, async () => openProjectFlow()],
    [platformActionIds.closeWorkspaceProject, async () => closeProjectFlow()],
    [platformActionIds.saveWorkspaceProject, async () => saveProjectFlow()],
    [platformActionIds.saveWorkspaceProjectAs, async () => saveProjectFlow({ forceSaveAs: true })],
    [platformActionIds.importWorkspaceProject, async () => importBackendProject()],
    [platformActionIds.exportWorkspaceProject, async () => exportWorkspaceProjectFlow()],
    [platformActionIds.exit, async () => exitFlow()]
  ]);

  function resolvePlatformActionLoggerSource(source) {
    if (source === platformActionSource) {
      return platformActionLoggerSource;
    }
    return APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.loggerSources.platform;
  }

  async function dispatchPlatformAction(actionId, { source = platformActionSource } = {}) {
    const loggerSource = resolvePlatformActionLoggerSource(source);
    const stateVersionBeforeDispatch = platformActionSurfaceStateVersion;
    try {
      const transitionResult = await tabs.finalizeActiveEditorContextBeforeTransition({
        reason: `${platformActionTransitionPrefix}${actionId}`,
        blockOnFailure: true
      });

      if (!transitionResult.continued) {
        logger.error(loggerSource, platformActionDispatchMessages.blockedByEditorContext, {
          action: actionId,
          source,
          outcome: transitionResult.outcome,
          reason: transitionResult.reason
        });
        return false;
      }

      const actionHandler = platformActionHandlers.get(actionId);
      if (!actionHandler) {
        return false;
      }

      await actionHandler();
      if (platformActionSurfaceStateVersion === stateVersionBeforeDispatch) {
        updatePlatformActionSurfaceState();
      }
      return true;
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error(loggerSource, platformActionDispatchMessages.executionFailed, {
        action: actionId,
        source,
        message: error?.message || String(error)
      });
      if (platformActionSurfaceStateVersion === stateVersionBeforeDispatch) {
        updatePlatformActionSurfaceState();
      }
      return false;
    }
  }

  for (const actionId of webSurfacePlatformActionOrder) {
    const buttonNode = platformActionButtonsById.get(actionId);
    if (!buttonNode) {
      continue;
    }
    buttonNode.addEventListener('click', () => {
      void dispatchPlatformAction(actionId, { source: platformActionSource });
    });
  }

  async function handleCloseIntentRequested() {
    try {
      await appCloseCoordinator.handleWindowCloseRequested();
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error(APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.loggerSources.windowClose, 'Ошибка обработки запроса закрытия окна', {
        message: error?.message || String(error)
      });

      try {
        await shell.cancelCloseIntent();
      } catch (cancelError) {
        logger.error(APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.loggerSources.windowClose, 'Ошибка отмены закрытия окна', {
          message: cancelError?.message || String(cancelError)
        });
      }
    }
  }

  const disposePrimaryCloseIntent = shell.subscribeToCloseIntent(() => {
    void handleCloseIntentRequested();
  });

  window.addEventListener('beforeunload', () => {
    disposePrimaryCloseIntent?.();
    processExecutionOrchestrator?.dispose?.();
  });

  logger.info(APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.loggerSources.platform, 'Инициализация MetaPlatform...');
  await presentBackendWorkspaceBrowser({
    refreshProjects: shouldStartupRefreshBackendProjects(),
    refreshReason: backendListRefreshReasons.startup
  });
  await tree.render();
});



==================================================
FILE: ui/renderer/core/commandBus.js
==================================================

import { APP_CONFIG } from '../../config/app-config.js';

const COMMAND_BUS_LOG_SOURCE = APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.loggerSources.commandBus;
const COMMAND_BUS_MESSAGES = APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.commandBusMessages;

export function createCommandBus({ logger }) {
  const handlers = new Map();

  function register(commandType, handler) {
    handlers.set(commandType, handler);
  }

  async function execute(command) {
    const type = command?.type;

    if (!type) {
      throw new Error(COMMAND_BUS_MESSAGES.commandTypeRequired);
    }

    const handler = handlers.get(type);

    if (!handler) {
      logger.warn(COMMAND_BUS_LOG_SOURCE, `${COMMAND_BUS_MESSAGES.missingHandlerPrefix}${type}`);
      return null;
    }

    logger.info(COMMAND_BUS_LOG_SOURCE, `${COMMAND_BUS_MESSAGES.executionPrefix}${type}`, command?.meta || null);

    try {
      const result = await handler(command);
      logger.info(COMMAND_BUS_LOG_SOURCE, `${COMMAND_BUS_MESSAGES.successPrefix}${type}`);
      return result;
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error(COMMAND_BUS_LOG_SOURCE, `${COMMAND_BUS_MESSAGES.failurePrefix}${type}`, {
        message: error?.message || String(error)
      });
      throw error;
    }
  }

  return {
    register,
    execute
  };
}
