import { slugifyDocumentName } from './naming.js';

let transientIdCounter = 0;

// Platform-level helper for transient unique entity ids.
// This is infrastructure only: it does not know module schemas or document semantics.
export function createTransientEntityId(baseSlug, fallback = 'entity') {
  const normalizedBase = slugifyDocumentName(baseSlug) || slugifyDocumentName(fallback) || 'entity';
  const timestamp = Date.now().toString(36);
  transientIdCounter = (transientIdCounter + 1) % Number.MAX_SAFE_INTEGER;
  const counter = transientIdCounter.toString(36);

  return `${normalizedBase}_${timestamp}${counter}`;
}

export function slugifyDocumentName(name) {
  return String(name ?? '')
    .trim()
    .replace(/\s+/g, '_')
    .replace(/[^\w\-А-Яа-яЁё]/g, '')
    .toLowerCase();
}

==================================================
FILE: ui/renderer/runtime/processExecutionOrchestrator.js
==================================================

import { createProcessPollingLifecycle } from './processPollingLifecycle.js';

function cloneProcessSnapshot(snapshot) {
  return {
    process: snapshot.process ? { ...snapshot.process } : null,
    outputChunks: snapshot.outputChunks.map((chunk) => ({ ...chunk })),
    afterChunkId: snapshot.afterChunkId
  };
}

export function createProcessExecutionOrchestrator({
  executeBackendCommand,
  commandIds,
  terminalStatuses,
  pollingIntervalMs,
  onUpdate
}) {
  if (typeof executeBackendCommand !== 'function') {
    throw new Error('Process execution orchestrator requires executeBackendCommand()');
  }

  const terminalStatusSet = new Set(Array.isArray(terminalStatuses) ? terminalStatuses : []);
  const notify = typeof onUpdate === 'function' ? onUpdate : () => {};

  const state = {
    process: null,
    outputChunks: [],
    afterChunkId: 0,
    hasSeenTerminal: false
  };

  function updateState(nextProcess = state.process) {
    if (nextProcess) {
      state.process = { ...nextProcess };
      if (terminalStatusSet.has(String(nextProcess.status || '').trim())) {
        state.hasSeenTerminal = true;
      }
    } else if (!state.hasSeenTerminal) {
      state.process = null;
    }
    notify(cloneProcessSnapshot(state));
  }

  function appendChunks(chunks) {
    if (!Array.isArray(chunks) || chunks.length === 0) {
      return 0;
    }

    for (const chunk of chunks) {
      state.outputChunks.push(chunk);
      const chunkId = Number(chunk?.chunkId || 0);
      if (chunkId > state.afterChunkId) {
        state.afterChunkId = chunkId;
      }
    }
    return chunks.length;
  }

  async function pollTick() {
    const stateResult = await executeBackendCommand(commandIds.processGetState, {}, { presentResult: false });
    const activeProcess = stateResult?.process || null;

    const outputResult = await executeBackendCommand(
      commandIds.processReadOutput,
      { afterChunkId: state.afterChunkId },
      { presentResult: false }
    );
    const latestProcess = outputResult?.process || null;
    const readChunks = Array.isArray(outputResult?.chunks) ? outputResult.chunks : [];
    const chunkCount = appendChunks(readChunks);

    const effectiveProcess = latestProcess || activeProcess || state.process;
    updateState(effectiveProcess);

    if (!activeProcess && !latestProcess && !state.hasSeenTerminal) {
      return false;
    }

    if (state.hasSeenTerminal && !activeProcess && chunkCount === 0) {
      return false;
    }

    return true;
  }

  const pollingLifecycle = createProcessPollingLifecycle({
    intervalMs: pollingIntervalMs,
    tick: pollTick
  });

  function clearSnapshot() {
    pollingLifecycle.stop();
    state.process = null;
    state.outputChunks = [];
    state.afterChunkId = 0;
    state.hasSeenTerminal = false;
    notify(cloneProcessSnapshot(state));
  }

  async function syncActiveProcess() {
    const result = await executeBackendCommand(commandIds.processGetState, {}, { presentResult: false });
    const process = result?.process || null;
    updateState(process);
    if (process) {
      pollingLifecycle.start();
      await pollingLifecycle.runTickOnce();
    }
    return process;
  }

  async function launchGenerate(payload = {}) {
    clearSnapshot();

    const result = await executeBackendCommand(commandIds.metagenGenerate, payload, { presentResult: false });
    const process = result?.process || null;
    updateState(process);
    if (process) {
      pollingLifecycle.start();
      await pollingLifecycle.runTickOnce();
    }
    return process;
  }

  async function stopProcess() {
    const result = await executeBackendCommand(commandIds.processStop, {}, { presentResult: false });
    const process = result?.process || null;
    updateState(process);
    if (process) {
      pollingLifecycle.start();
      await pollingLifecycle.runTickOnce();
    }
    return process;
  }

  function dispose() {
    pollingLifecycle.dispose();
  }

  return {
    syncActiveProcess,
    launchGenerate,
    stopProcess,
    clearSnapshot,
    dispose,
    isPollingActive: () => pollingLifecycle.isActive(),
    getSnapshot: () => cloneProcessSnapshot(state)
  };
}


==================================================
FILE: ui/renderer/runtime/processPollingLifecycle.js
==================================================

export function createProcessPollingLifecycle({
  intervalMs,
  tick,
  setIntervalFn = setInterval,
  clearIntervalFn = clearInterval
}) {
  if (typeof tick !== 'function') {
    throw new Error('Process polling lifecycle requires tick()');
  }

  let timerId = null;
  let tickInFlight = false;

  async function runTickOnce() {
    if (tickInFlight) {
      return true;
    }

    tickInFlight = true;
    try {
      const shouldContinue = await tick();
      if (shouldContinue === false) {
        stop();
        return false;
      }
      return true;
    } finally {
      tickInFlight = false;
    }
  }

  function start() {
    if (timerId !== null) {
      return false;
    }

    timerId = setIntervalFn(() => {
      void runTickOnce();
    }, intervalMs);
    return true;
  }

  function stop() {
    if (timerId === null) {
      return false;
    }

    clearIntervalFn(timerId);
    timerId = null;
    return true;
  }

  function dispose() {
    stop();
  }

  return {
    start,
    stop,
    dispose,
    runTickOnce,
    isActive: () => timerId !== null,
    isTickInFlight: () => tickInFlight
  };
}

FILE: ui/renderer/runtime/projectPaths.js
==================================================

import { APP_CONFIG } from '../../config/app-config.js';

const PROJECT_MODULE_IDS = APP_CONFIG.project.moduleIds;
const PROJECT_FOLDERS = APP_CONFIG.project.folders;
const PRIMARY_PROJECT_MODULE_IDS = APP_CONFIG.project.primaryModuleIds || [];

export function getPrimaryProjectModuleIds() {
  return PRIMARY_PROJECT_MODULE_IDS.filter((moduleId) => Boolean(PROJECT_MODULE_IDS[moduleId]));
}

export function createPrimaryModuleDocumentBuckets() {
  return getPrimaryProjectModuleIds().reduce((acc, moduleId) => {
    acc[moduleId] = [];
    return acc;
  }, {});
}

export function flattenPrimaryModuleDocumentBuckets(documentsByModule = {}) {
  return getPrimaryProjectModuleIds().flatMap((moduleId) => documentsByModule[moduleId] || []);
}

export function getProjectModuleFolders() {
  return getPrimaryProjectModuleIds().reduce((acc, moduleId) => {
    acc[moduleId] = PROJECT_FOLDERS[moduleId];
    return acc;
  }, {});
}

export function joinProjectPath(...parts) {
  return parts
    .filter(Boolean)
    .join('/')
    .replace(/\\/g, '/')
    .replace(/\/{2,}/g, '/');
}

export function getFileExtension(fileName) {
  const normalized = String(fileName || '');
  const lastDotIndex = normalized.lastIndexOf('.');
  return lastDotIndex > 0 ? normalized.slice(lastDotIndex) : '';
}

export function stripFileExtension(fileName) {
  const normalized = String(fileName || '');
  const lastDotIndex = normalized.lastIndexOf('.');
  return lastDotIndex > 0 ? normalized.slice(0, lastDotIndex) : normalized;
}

export function dirnameOf(targetPath) {
  const normalized = String(targetPath || '').replace(/\\/g, '/').replace(/\/+$/, '');
  const index = normalized.lastIndexOf('/');

  if (index < 0) {
    return '';
  }

  if (index === 0) {
    return '/';
  }

  return normalized.slice(0, index);
}

export function normalizeProjectFilePath(projectFilePath) {
  const normalized = String(projectFilePath || '').trim().replace(/\\/g, '/').replace(/\/+$/, '');

  if (!normalized) {
    throw new Error('Project file path is required');
  }

  const baseName = normalized.split('/').pop() || '';
  if (!baseName || !baseName.includes('.')) {
    throw new Error(`Project file path must point to a YAML file: ${projectFilePath}`);
  }

  const ext = getFileExtension(baseName).toLowerCase();
  const allowed = APP_CONFIG.project.allowedProjectFileExtensions || ['.yaml', '.yml'];

  if (!allowed.includes(ext)) {
    throw new Error(`Project file path must point to a YAML file: ${projectFilePath}`);
  }

  return normalized;
}

export function getProjectRootFromProjectFile(projectFilePath) {
  const root = dirnameOf(projectFilePath);
  return root || '.';
}

export function buildProjectFilePath(projectRoot, projectFileName = APP_CONFIG.project.defaultProjectFileName) {
  return joinProjectPath(projectRoot, projectFileName);
}

export function getDefaultProjectModuleDirectories(projectRoot) {
  const moduleFolders = getProjectModuleFolders();

  return Object.entries(moduleFolders).reduce((acc, [moduleId, folder]) => {
    acc[moduleId] = joinProjectPath(projectRoot, folder);
    return acc;
  }, {});
}

export function getProjectOwnedPaths(targetProjectFilePath) {
  const normalizedProjectFilePath = normalizeProjectFilePath(targetProjectFilePath);
  const targetRoot = getProjectRootFromProjectFile(normalizedProjectFilePath);
  const targetProjectFileName = normalizedProjectFilePath.split('/').pop();
  const moduleDirectories = getDefaultProjectModuleDirectories(targetRoot);

  return {
    rootPath: targetRoot,
    projectFileName: targetProjectFileName,
    projectFilePath: buildProjectFilePath(targetRoot, targetProjectFileName),
    moduleDirectories,
    moduleFolders: getProjectModuleFolders()
  };
}


==================================================
FILE: ui/renderer/runtime/runtimeClient.js
==================================================

import { normalizeImportResponse, normalizeRuntimeRequest, normalizeRuntimeResponse } from './runtimeClientContract.js';

export function createRuntimeClient({ adapter }) {
  if (!adapter || typeof adapter.execute !== 'function') {
    throw new Error('Runtime client adapter with execute(request) is required');
  }

  async function execute(request) {
    const normalizedRequest = normalizeRuntimeRequest(request);
    const response = await adapter.execute(normalizedRequest);
    return normalizeRuntimeResponse(response, normalizedRequest.requestId);
  }

  async function downloadBinary(relativePath) {
    if (typeof adapter.downloadBinary !== 'function') {
      throw new Error('Runtime client adapter with downloadBinary(relativePath) is required');
    }
    return adapter.downloadBinary(relativePath);
  }

  async function importProjectArchive(payload) {
    if (typeof adapter.importProjectArchive !== 'function') {
      throw new Error('Runtime client adapter with importProjectArchive(payload) is required');
    }

    const response = await adapter.importProjectArchive(payload);
    return normalizeImportResponse(response);
  }

  return {
    execute,
    downloadBinary,
    importProjectArchive
  };
}


==================================================
FILE: ui/renderer/runtime/runtimeClientContract.js
==================================================

﻿const REQUIRED_STRING_FIELDS = ['requestId', 'module', 'command'];

function isPlainObject(value) {
  return Boolean(value) && typeof value === 'object' && !Array.isArray(value);
}

export function normalizeRuntimeRequest(input) {
  if (!isPlainObject(input)) {
    throw new Error('Runtime command request must be an object');
  }

  for (const field of REQUIRED_STRING_FIELDS) {
    const value = String(input[field] || '').trim();
    if (!value) {
      throw new Error(`Runtime command request field is required: ${field}`);
    }
  }

  const payload = input.payload;

  return {
    requestId: String(input.requestId).trim(),
    module: String(input.module).trim(),
    command: String(input.command).trim(),
    payload: isPlainObject(payload) ? payload : {}
  };
}

export function normalizeRuntimeResponse(input, fallbackRequestId = '') {
  if (!isPlainObject(input)) {
    throw new Error('Runtime command response must be an object');
  }

  const requestId = String(input.requestId || fallbackRequestId || '').trim();
  if (!requestId) {
    throw new Error('Runtime command response field is required: requestId');
  }

  const ok = Boolean(input.ok);
  const result = isPlainObject(input.result) ? input.result : null;
  const error = isPlainObject(input.error) ? input.error : null;

  if (ok && error) {
    throw new Error('Runtime command response cannot include error when ok=true');
  }

  if (!ok && !error) {
    throw new Error('Runtime command response must include error when ok=false');
  }

  return {
    requestId,
    ok,
    result,
    error
  };
}

export function normalizeImportResponse(input) {
  if (!isPlainObject(input)) {
    throw new Error('Import response must be an object');
  }

  const ok = Boolean(input.ok);
  const result = isPlainObject(input.result) ? input.result : null;
  const error = isPlainObject(input.error) ? input.error : null;

  if (ok && error) {
    throw new Error('Import response cannot include error when ok=true');
  }

  if (!ok && !error) {
    throw new Error('Import response must include error when ok=false');
  }

  return {
    ok,
    result,
    error
  };
}


==================================================
FILE: ui/renderer/runtime/shellContract.js
==================================================

function assertShellOperation(operation, operationName) {
  if (typeof operation !== 'function') {
    throw new Error(`Shell operation "${operationName}" must be a function`);
  }
}

function toUnsubscribe(handle) {
  return typeof handle === 'function' ? handle : () => {};
}

export function createRendererShellContract({
  adapterId = '',
  requestProjectImportArchive,
  requestBinarySaveAs,
  requestApplicationExit,
  approveCloseIntent,
  cancelCloseIntent,
  subscribeToCloseIntent
}) {
  assertShellOperation(requestProjectImportArchive, 'requestProjectImportArchive');
  assertShellOperation(requestBinarySaveAs, 'requestBinarySaveAs');
  assertShellOperation(requestApplicationExit, 'requestApplicationExit');
  assertShellOperation(approveCloseIntent, 'approveCloseIntent');
  assertShellOperation(cancelCloseIntent, 'cancelCloseIntent');
  assertShellOperation(subscribeToCloseIntent, 'subscribeToCloseIntent');

  return Object.freeze({
    adapterId: String(adapterId || '').trim(),
    requestProjectImportArchive,
    requestBinarySaveAs,
    requestApplicationExit,
    approveCloseIntent,
    cancelCloseIntent,
    subscribeToCloseIntent: (listener) => toUnsubscribe(subscribeToCloseIntent(listener))
  });
}

import { APP_CONFIG } from '../../config/app-config.js';
import { setNodeIconAndText } from './pngIconRenderer.js';

export function applyStaticText() {
  const titleNode = document.querySelector(APP_CONFIG.ui.dom.titleSelector);
  const topPanelTitleNode = document.querySelector(APP_CONFIG.ui.dom.topPanelTitleSelector);
  const paramsUndoButton = document.querySelector(APP_CONFIG.ui.dom.paramsUndoButtonSelector);
  const paramsRedoButton = document.querySelector(APP_CONFIG.ui.dom.paramsRedoButtonSelector);
  const logsHeaderNode = document.querySelector(APP_CONFIG.ui.dom.logsPanelHeaderSelector);

  if (titleNode) {
    titleNode.textContent = APP_CONFIG.platform.app.title;
  }

  if (topPanelTitleNode) {
    setNodeIconAndText(topPanelTitleNode, {
      iconAssetPath: APP_CONFIG.ui.icons.assets.topPanelTitle,
      labelText: APP_CONFIG.platform.app.topPanelTitle,
      textClassName: APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.topPanelTitleText
    });
  }

  if (logsHeaderNode) {
    setNodeIconAndText(logsHeaderNode, {
      iconAssetPath: APP_CONFIG.ui.panelHeaderIcons.logs,
      labelText: APP_CONFIG.ui.panelHeaders.logs,
      textClassName: APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.panelHeaderText
    });
  }

  if (paramsUndoButton) {
    paramsUndoButton.textContent = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.paramsUndoButton;
  }

  if (paramsRedoButton) {
    paramsRedoButton.textContent = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.paramsRedoButton;
  }
}


==================================================
FILE: ui/renderer/ui/createProjectTree.js
==================================================

import { APP_CONFIG } from '../../config/app-config.js';
import { METAGEN_CONFIG } from '../modules/metagen/metagenConfig.js';
import { METALAB_CONFIG } from '../modules/metalab/metalabConfig.js';
import { METAVIEW_CONFIG } from '../modules/metaview/metaviewConfig.js';
import {
  TREE_NODE_TYPES,
  buildProjectTreeNodes,
  createTreeBehaviorConfig,
  createTreeInteractionController,
  getNodeActions,
  getNodeRowClassNames
} from './projectTree/treeAdapter.js';
import { createPngIconNode, setNodeIconAndText } from './pngIconRenderer.js';

const TREE_CLASSNAMES = APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames;

function normalizeClassNames(classNames = []) {
  const normalizedClassNames = Array.isArray(classNames) ? classNames : [classNames];

  return normalizedClassNames.filter(Boolean).map((className) => {
    if (/\s/.test(className)) {
      throw new TypeError(
        `Invalid class token "${className}". Pass class names as separate tokens.`
      );
    }

    return className;
  });
}

function createElement(tagName, classNames = []) {
  const node = document.createElement(tagName);
  normalizeClassNames(classNames).forEach((className) => node.classList.add(className));
  return node;
}

function resolveNodeIconAssetPath(nodeData) {
  if (nodeData.nodeType === TREE_NODE_TYPES.project) {
    return APP_CONFIG.ui.tree.icons.project;
  }

  if (nodeData.nodeType === TREE_NODE_TYPES.module) {
    return APP_CONFIG.ui.tree.icons.moduleById[nodeData.moduleId];
  }

  return APP_CONFIG.ui.tree.icons.documentById[nodeData.moduleId];
}

export function createProjectTree({
  logger,
  projectManager,
  tabs,
  onCreateComponentRequest,
  onDeleteComponentRequest
}) {
  const treeRoot = document.getElementById(APP_CONFIG.ui.dom.projectTreeId);
  const projectPanelTitleNode = document.querySelector(APP_CONFIG.ui.dom.projectPanelTitleSelector);

  const moduleSections = [
    {
      moduleId: METAGEN_CONFIG.moduleId,
      moduleName: METAGEN_CONFIG.moduleName,
      getDefaultName: () => projectManager.getNextMetaGenDefaultName()
    },
    {
      moduleId: METALAB_CONFIG.moduleId,
      moduleName: METALAB_CONFIG.moduleName,
      getDefaultName: () => METALAB_CONFIG.defaults.newDocumentName
    },
    {
      moduleId: METAVIEW_CONFIG.moduleId,
      moduleName: METAVIEW_CONFIG.moduleName,
      getDefaultName: () => METAVIEW_CONFIG.defaults.newDocumentName
    }
  ];

  const behaviorConfig = createTreeBehaviorConfig();
  const treeSelectionState = {
    selectedNodeId: null
  };
  const moduleExpandState = new Map();

  function getProjectPanelTitle(project) {
    if (!project) {
      return '';
    }

    const projectName = String(project.project?.name || APP_CONFIG.ui.text.untitled).trim() || APP_CONFIG.ui.text.untitled;
    return project.isDirty ? `${projectName} ${APP_CONFIG.ui.text.dirtyMarker}` : projectName;
  }

  function renderProjectPanelTitle(project) {
    if (!projectPanelTitleNode) {
      return;
    }

    if (!project) {
      projectPanelTitleNode.innerHTML = '';
      return;
    }

    setNodeIconAndText(projectPanelTitleNode, {
      iconAssetPath: APP_CONFIG.ui.panelHeaderIcons.project,
      labelText: getProjectPanelTitle(project),
      iconSize: APP_CONFIG.ui.icons.sizes.defaultIcon,
      textClassName: TREE_CLASSNAMES.panelHeaderText
    });
  }

  function isModuleExpanded(moduleId) {
    if (!moduleExpandState.has(moduleId)) {
      moduleExpandState.set(moduleId, true);
    }

    return moduleExpandState.get(moduleId);
  }

  function toggleModuleExpanded(moduleId) {
    moduleExpandState.set(moduleId, !isModuleExpanded(moduleId));
  }

  async function startDocumentCreation(sectionConfig) {
    await tabs.startTemporaryDocumentCreation({
      moduleId: sectionConfig.moduleId,
      defaultName: sectionConfig.getDefaultName(),
      onCommit: async ({ moduleId, confirmedName }) => {
        return projectManager.createDocument(moduleId, confirmedName);
      }
    });
  }

  const interactionController = createTreeInteractionController({
    tabs,
    onCreateComponentRequest: onCreateComponentRequest || (async (moduleId, nodeData) => {
      const sectionConfig = moduleSections.find((section) => section.moduleId === moduleId);

      if (!sectionConfig) {
        logger.warn(APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.loggerSources.projectTree, 'Не найден модуль для создания компонента', {
          moduleId,
          nodeData
        });
        return;
      }

      await startDocumentCreation(sectionConfig);
    }),
    onDeleteComponentRequest: onDeleteComponentRequest || (async (documentRecord, nodeData) => {
      const documentIdentity = nodeData?.id || documentRecord;
      await tabs.closeTab(documentIdentity, { skipProjectSync: true });
      await projectManager.deleteDocument(documentIdentity);
    })
  });

  function renderNodeRow(nodeData, rowClassNames = [TREE_CLASSNAMES.treeNodeRow]) {
    const row = createElement('div', [...rowClassNames, ...getNodeRowClassNames(nodeData)]);
    row.dataset.nodeType = nodeData.nodeType;
    row.dataset.nodeId = nodeData.id;

    const label = createElement('button', [TREE_CLASSNAMES.treeNodeLabel]);
    label.type = 'button';

    const disclosureHost = createElement('span', [TREE_CLASSNAMES.treeNodeDisclosure]);
    if (nodeData.nodeType === TREE_NODE_TYPES.module) {
      const disclosureIconAssetPath = isModuleExpanded(nodeData.moduleId)
        ? APP_CONFIG.ui.tree.icons.disclosure.expanded
        : APP_CONFIG.ui.tree.icons.disclosure.collapsed;
      disclosureHost.appendChild(
        createPngIconNode(disclosureIconAssetPath, {
          size: APP_CONFIG.ui.icons.sizes.compactIcon,
          classNames: [TREE_CLASSNAMES.treeNodeIcon]
        })
      );
    } else {
      disclosureHost.classList.add(TREE_CLASSNAMES.treeNodeDisclosureSpacer);
    }

    label.appendChild(disclosureHost);
    label.appendChild(
      createPngIconNode(resolveNodeIconAssetPath(nodeData), {
        size: APP_CONFIG.ui.icons.sizes.defaultIcon,
        classNames: [TREE_CLASSNAMES.treeNodeIcon]
      })
    );

    const labelText = createElement('span', [TREE_CLASSNAMES.treeNodeLabelText]);
    labelText.textContent = nodeData.label;
    label.appendChild(labelText);

    label.addEventListener('click', async (event) => {
      event.preventDefault();
      treeSelectionState.selectedNodeId = nodeData.id;

      if (nodeData.nodeType === TREE_NODE_TYPES.module) {
        toggleModuleExpanded(nodeData.moduleId);
        await render();
        return;
      }

      await interactionController.onNodePrimaryClick(nodeData);
      await render();
    });

    row.appendChild(label);

    const actions = getNodeActions(nodeData);

    if (actions.length > 0) {
      const actionsContainer = createElement('div', [TREE_CLASSNAMES.treeNodeActions]);

      for (const action of actions) {
        if (!action.visible) {
          continue;
        }

        const actionButton = createElement('button', [TREE_CLASSNAMES.treeNodeActionButton]);
        actionButton.type = 'button';
        actionButton.title = action.title;
        actionButton.setAttribute('aria-label', action.title);
        actionButton.appendChild(
          createPngIconNode(action.iconAssetPath, {
            size: APP_CONFIG.ui.icons.sizes.compactIcon,
            classNames: [TREE_CLASSNAMES.treeNodeActionIcon]
          })
        );

        actionButton.addEventListener('click', async (event) => {
          await interactionController.onNodeActionClick({
            actionId: action.id,
            nodeData,
            event
          });
        });

        actionsContainer.appendChild(actionButton);
      }

      row.appendChild(actionsContainer);
    }

    if (treeSelectionState.selectedNodeId === nodeData.id) {
      row.classList.add(TREE_CLASSNAMES.selected);
    }

    return row;
  }

  async function render() {
    const project = projectManager.getCurrentProject();

    treeRoot.innerHTML = '';
    renderProjectPanelTitle(project);

    if (!project) {
      return;
    }

    const treeNodes = buildProjectTreeNodes({
      project,
      moduleSections,
      getDocumentsByModule: (moduleId) => projectManager.getDocumentsByModule(moduleId)
    });

    const projectNode = treeNodes.find((node) => node.nodeType === TREE_NODE_TYPES.project);

    if (projectNode) {
      const projectRootNode = createElement('div', [TREE_CLASSNAMES.projectNode]);
      projectRootNode.appendChild(renderNodeRow(projectNode, [TREE_CLASSNAMES.treeNodeRow]));
      treeRoot.appendChild(projectRootNode);
    }

    for (const nodeData of treeNodes) {
      if (nodeData.nodeType !== TREE_NODE_TYPES.module) {
        continue;
      }

      const moduleBlock = createElement('div', [TREE_CLASSNAMES.treeModuleBlock]);
      moduleBlock.appendChild(
        renderNodeRow(nodeData, [TREE_CLASSNAMES.treeSectionHeader, TREE_CLASSNAMES.treeNodeRow])
      );

      const documentsContainer = createElement('div', [TREE_CLASSNAMES.treeModuleChildren]);

      if (isModuleExpanded(nodeData.moduleId)) {
        for (const documentNode of nodeData.children || []) {
          const item = createElement('div', [TREE_CLASSNAMES.treeItem]);
          item.appendChild(
            renderNodeRow(documentNode, [TREE_CLASSNAMES.treeNodeRow, TREE_CLASSNAMES.treeNodeDocumentRow])
          );
          documentsContainer.appendChild(item);
        }
      }

      moduleBlock.appendChild(documentsContainer);
      treeRoot.appendChild(moduleBlock);
    }

    logger.info(APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.loggerSources.projectTree, 'Дерево проекта обновлено', {
      inlineRenameEnabled: behaviorConfig.inlineRenameEnabled,
      slowDoubleClickRenameEnabled: behaviorConfig.slowDoubleClickRenameEnabled
    });
  }

  projectManager.subscribe(() => {
    render().catch((error) => {
      logger.error(APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.loggerSources.projectTree, 'Ошибка рендера дерева проекта', {
        message: error?.message || String(error)
      });
    });
  });

  return { render, getProjectPanelTitle };
}


==================================================
FILE: ui/renderer/ui/createWorkbenchTabs.js
==================================================

import { APP_CONFIG } from '../../config/app-config.js';
import { finalizeEditingBeforeTabSwitch } from './tabEditLifecycle.js';
import { finalizeEditingBeforeContextTransition } from './editorContextLifecycle.js';
import { getDocumentLabel, getDocumentIdentityKey } from '../runtime/documentRecordIdentity.js';
import { createPngIconNode } from './pngIconRenderer.js';

function createElement(tagName, classNames = []) {
  const node = document.createElement(tagName);
  classNames.forEach((className) => node.classList.add(className));
  return node;
}

function normalizeName(name) {
  return String(name ?? '').trim();
}

function buildTabTitleNode(title) {
  const titleNode = createElement('span', [APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.tabTitle]);
  titleNode.textContent = title;
  return titleNode;
}

function buildCloseButtonNode(label) {
  const closeButtonNode = createElement('button', [APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.tabClose]);
  closeButtonNode.type = 'button';
  const iconHost = createPngIconNode(APP_CONFIG.ui.icons.assets.tabs.close, {
    size: APP_CONFIG.ui.icons.sizes.compactIcon
  });
  closeButtonNode.appendChild(
    iconHost
  );
  closeButtonNode.tabIndex = -1;
  closeButtonNode.setAttribute('aria-label', `${APP_CONFIG.ui.text.closeAriaPrefix} ${label}`);
  return closeButtonNode;
}

export function createWorkbenchTabs({ logger, openEditor, projectManager, onActiveEntryChanged }) {
  const tabsList = document.getElementById(APP_CONFIG.ui.dom.tabsListId);
  const editorHost = document.getElementById(APP_CONFIG.ui.dom.editorHostId);
  const tabs = new Map();
  let activeTabId = null;
  let temporaryCounter = 0;


  async function finalizeActiveEditorContextBeforeTransition({ reason, blockOnFailure = true } = {}) {
    const currentEntry = activeTabId && tabs.has(activeTabId) ? tabs.get(activeTabId) : null;
    const result = await finalizeEditingBeforeContextTransition({
      activeEntry: currentEntry,
      logger,
      source: APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.loggerSources.tabs,
      reason,
      blockOnFailure
    });

    return result;
  }

  async function activateTab(tabId) {
    const currentEntry = activeTabId && tabs.has(activeTabId) ? tabs.get(activeTabId) : null;
    const canActivate = await finalizeEditingBeforeTabSwitch({
      activeEntry: currentEntry,
      nextTabId: tabId,
      logger
    });

    if (!canActivate) {
      return false;
    }

    activeTabId = tabId;
    for (const entry of tabs.values()) {
      entry.tabNode.classList.toggle(APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.tabActive, entry.tabId === tabId);
      entry.pageNode.classList.toggle(APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.pageActive, entry.tabId === tabId);
    }

    onActiveEntryChanged?.(tabs.get(tabId) || null);

    return true;
  }

  function updateTabTitle(entry) {
    const titleNode = entry.tabNode.querySelector(`.${APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.tabTitle}`);
    if (titleNode) {
      titleNode.textContent = getDocumentLabel(entry.documentRecord);
    }
  }


  async function syncEntryDocumentRecordToProject(entry) {
    if (!entry) {
      return null;
    }

    let nextRecord = entry.documentRecord;

    if (typeof entry.runtime?.collectDocumentRecord === 'function') {
      nextRecord = await entry.runtime.collectDocumentRecord();

      if (nextRecord?.moduleId && nextRecord?.path && nextRecord?.document) {
        entry.documentRecord = nextRecord;
      } else {
        nextRecord = entry.documentRecord;
      }
    }

    if (nextRecord?.moduleId && nextRecord?.path && nextRecord?.document) {
      await projectManager?.replaceDocumentRecord?.(nextRecord);
    }

    return nextRecord;
  }

  function resolveTabId(targetIdentity) {
    if (tabs.has(targetIdentity)) {
      return targetIdentity;
    }

    const identityKeyFromRecord = targetIdentity && typeof targetIdentity === 'object'
      ? getDocumentIdentityKey(targetIdentity)
      : '';

    for (const [candidateTabId, candidateEntry] of tabs.entries()) {
      const candidateIdentityKey = getDocumentIdentityKey(candidateEntry.documentRecord);

      if (identityKeyFromRecord && candidateIdentityKey === identityKeyFromRecord) {
        return candidateTabId;
      }

      if (candidateIdentityKey && candidateIdentityKey === targetIdentity) {
        return candidateTabId;
      }

      if (candidateEntry.documentRecord === targetIdentity) {
        return candidateTabId;
      }

    }

    return null;
  }


  async function closeTab(tabId, options = {}) {
    const resolvedTabId = resolveTabId(tabId);
    const entry = resolvedTabId ? tabs.get(resolvedTabId) : null;

    if (!entry) {
      return;
    }

    const orderedEntries = Array.from(tabs.values());
    const index = orderedEntries.findIndex((tabEntry) => tabEntry.tabId === resolvedTabId);

    await finalizeEditingBeforeContextTransition({
      activeEntry: entry,
      logger,
      source: APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.loggerSources.tabs,
      reason: APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.transitionReasons.tabClose,
      blockOnFailure: false
    });

    if (!options.skipProjectSync) {
      try {
        await syncEntryDocumentRecordToProject(entry);
      } catch (error) {
        logger.error(APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.loggerSources.tabs, 'Ошибка синхронизации snapshot перед закрытием вкладки', {
          tabId: resolvedTabId,
          message: error?.message || String(error)
        });
      }
    }

    entry.runtime?.dispose?.();
    entry.pageNode.remove();
    entry.tabNode.remove();
    tabs.delete(resolvedTabId);

    if (activeTabId === resolvedTabId) {
      activeTabId = null;
    }

    const fallback = orderedEntries[index + 1] || orderedEntries[index - 1];

    if (fallback && tabs.has(fallback.tabId)) {
      await activateTab(fallback.tabId);
    } else {
      onActiveEntryChanged?.(null);
    }
  }

  function createTemporaryTabEntry({ tabId, initialTitle }) {
    const tabNode = createElement('button', [APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.tab]);
    tabNode.type = 'button';

    const titleNode = buildTabTitleNode(initialTitle || APP_CONFIG.ui.text.untitled);
    tabNode.appendChild(titleNode);

    const closeButton = buildCloseButtonNode(initialTitle || APP_CONFIG.ui.text.untitled);
    closeButton.addEventListener('click', (event) => {
      event.preventDefault();
      event.stopPropagation();
      closeTab(tabId);
    });
    tabNode.appendChild(closeButton);

    const pageNode = createElement('div', [APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.page]);
    pageNode.dataset.tabId = tabId;
    editorHost.appendChild(pageNode);

    const entry = {
      tabId,
      tabNode,
      pageNode,
      runtime: null,
      documentRecord: {
        moduleId: APP_CONFIG.project.moduleIds.temporary,
        path: tabId,
        document: { name: initialTitle || APP_CONFIG.ui.text.untitled }
      },
      isTemporary: true
    };

    tabNode.addEventListener('click', async () => {
      await activateTab(entry.tabId);
    });
    tabsList.appendChild(tabNode);
    tabs.set(tabId, entry);
    void activateTab(tabId);

    return entry;
  }

  async function startTemporaryDocumentCreation({ moduleId, defaultName = '', onCommit }) {
    const tabId = `${APP_CONFIG.project.temporaryDocumentPathPrefix}${moduleId}/${++temporaryCounter}`;
    const entry = createTemporaryTabEntry({ tabId, initialTitle: defaultName || APP_CONFIG.ui.text.untitled });

    const titleNode = entry.tabNode.querySelector(`.${APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.tabTitle}`);

    if (!titleNode) {
      return null;
    }

    const input = createElement('input', [APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.inlineRenameInput]);
    input.type = 'text';
    input.value = defaultName;
    titleNode.replaceWith(input);
    input.focus();
    input.select();

    let finalized = false;

    const cancel = () => {
      if (finalized) {
        return null;
      }

      finalized = true;
      closeTab(tabId);
      return null;
    };

    const commit = async () => {
      if (finalized) {
        return null;
      }

      const nextName = normalizeName(input.value);

      if (!nextName) {
        return cancel();
      }

      const created = await onCommit?.({ moduleId, confirmedName: nextName });

      if (!created) {
        logger.warn(APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.loggerSources.tabs, 'Создание документа отклонено', { moduleId, name: nextName });
        input.focus();
        input.select();
        return null;
      }

      finalized = true;
      closeTab(tabId);
      await openDocument(created);
      return created;
    };

    input.addEventListener('keydown', async (event) => {
      if (event.key === 'Enter') {
        event.preventDefault();
        await commit();
      }

      if (event.key === 'Escape') {
        event.preventDefault();
        cancel();
      }
    });

    input.addEventListener('blur', async () => {
      if (!normalizeName(input.value)) {
        cancel();
        return;
      }

      await commit();
    });

    return entry;
  }

  async function closeAllTabs(options = {}) {
    for (const tabId of Array.from(tabs.keys())) {
      await closeTab(tabId, options);
    }
  }

  function getActiveDocumentRecord() {
    if (!activeTabId || !tabs.has(activeTabId)) {
      return null;
    }

    return tabs.get(activeTabId).documentRecord;
  }

  function getActiveRuntime() {
    if (!activeTabId || !tabs.has(activeTabId)) {
      return null;
    }

    return tabs.get(activeTabId).runtime || null;
  }

  async function startRename(tabId) {
    const entry = tabs.get(tabId);

    if (!entry) {
      return false;
    }

    const titleNode = entry.tabNode.querySelector(`.${APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.tabTitle}`);

    if (!titleNode || titleNode.dataset.renaming === '1') {
      return false;
    }

    titleNode.dataset.renaming = '1';

    const previousName = getDocumentLabel(entry.documentRecord);
    const input = createElement('input', [APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.inlineRenameInput]);
    input.type = 'text';
    input.value = previousName;

    titleNode.replaceWith(input);
    input.focus();
    input.select();

    let finalized = false;

    const finalize = async (commit) => {
      if (finalized) {
        return false;
      }

      finalized = true;
      const nextName = normalizeName(input.value);
      let updatedTabId = tabId;

      if (commit) {
        if (!nextName) {
          logger.warn(APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.loggerSources.tabs, 'Пустое имя отклонено');
        } else {
          const renamed = await projectManager.renameDocument(getDocumentIdentityKey(entry.documentRecord), nextName);

          if (!renamed) {
            logger.warn(APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.loggerSources.tabs, 'Переименование отклонено', { name: nextName });
          } else {
            if (renamed.nextPath !== renamed.previousPath) {
              entry.documentRecord.path = renamed.nextPath;
            }

            updatedTabId = entry.tabId;
            entry.pageNode.dataset.tabId = entry.tabId;
            updateTabTitle(entry);
          }
        }
      }

      const restoredTitle = buildTabTitleNode(getDocumentLabel(entry.documentRecord));
      restoredTitle.dataset.renaming = '0';
      input.replaceWith(restoredTitle);

      return updatedTabId;
    };

    input.addEventListener('keydown', async (event) => {
      if (event.key === 'Enter') {
        event.preventDefault();
        const updatedTabId = await finalize(true);
        if (updatedTabId) {
          await activateTab(updatedTabId);
        }
      }

      if (event.key === 'Escape') {
        event.preventDefault();
        const updatedTabId = await finalize(false);
        if (updatedTabId) {
          await activateTab(updatedTabId);
        }
      }
    });

    input.addEventListener('blur', async () => {
      const updatedTabId = await finalize(true);
      if (updatedTabId) {
        await activateTab(updatedTabId);
      }
    });

    return true;
  }


  function findTabByDocument(documentRecord) {
    const identityKey = getDocumentIdentityKey(documentRecord);

    if (!identityKey) {
      return null;
    }

    for (const entry of tabs.values()) {
      if (getDocumentIdentityKey(entry.documentRecord) === identityKey) {
        return entry;
      }
    }

    return null;
  }

  async function openOrActivateDocument(documentRecord, options = {}) {
    const existingEntry = findTabByDocument(documentRecord);

    if (existingEntry) {
      await activateTab(existingEntry.tabId);
      return existingEntry;
    }

    return openDocument(documentRecord, options);
  }

  async function openDocument(documentRecord, { startRenameMode = false } = {}) {
    const tabId = getDocumentIdentityKey(documentRecord);

    const existingEntry = tabs.get(tabId) || findTabByDocument(documentRecord);
    if (existingEntry) {
      void activateTab(existingEntry.tabId);
      if (startRenameMode) {
        await startRename(existingEntry.tabId);
      }
      return existingEntry;
    }

    const tabNode = createElement('button', [APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.tab]);
    tabNode.type = 'button';

    const tabTitle = getDocumentLabel(documentRecord);
    tabNode.appendChild(buildTabTitleNode(tabTitle));

    const closeButton = buildCloseButtonNode(tabTitle);
    closeButton.addEventListener('click', (event) => {
      event.preventDefault();
      event.stopPropagation();
      closeTab(tabId);
    });
    tabNode.appendChild(closeButton);

    const pageNode = createElement('div', [APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.page]);
    pageNode.dataset.tabId = tabId;
    editorHost.appendChild(pageNode);

    const runtime = await openEditor({
      documentRecord,
      mountElement: pageNode
    });

    const entry = { tabId, tabNode, pageNode, runtime, documentRecord };
    tabs.set(tabId, entry);

    tabNode.addEventListener('click', async () => {
      await activateTab(entry.tabId);
    });
    tabNode.addEventListener('dblclick', async (event) => {
      event.preventDefault();
      event.stopPropagation();
      await startRename(entry.tabId);
    });

    tabsList.appendChild(tabNode);
    void activateTab(tabId);

    if (startRenameMode) {
      await startRename(entry.tabId);
    }

    logger.info(APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.loggerSources.tabs, 'Открыта вкладка', { tabId });
    return entry;
  }

  async function collectOpenDocumentRecords() {
    const output = [];

    await finalizeActiveEditorContextBeforeTransition({
      reason: APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.transitionReasons.collectOpenDocumentRecords,
      blockOnFailure: false
    });

    for (const entry of tabs.values()) {
      try {
        const nextRecord = await syncEntryDocumentRecordToProject(entry);
        output.push(nextRecord || entry.documentRecord);
      } catch (error) {
        logger.error(APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.loggerSources.tabs, 'Ошибка синхронизации snapshot открытого документа', {
          tabId: entry.tabId,
          message: error?.message || String(error)
        });
        output.push(entry.documentRecord);
      }
    }

    return output;
  }

  function updateTabPaths(pathMap) {
    if (!pathMap || typeof pathMap.entries !== 'function') {
      return;
    }

    for (const [identityKey, nextPath] of pathMap.entries()) {
      if (!tabs.has(identityKey)) {
        continue;
      }

      const entry = tabs.get(identityKey);
      entry.documentRecord.path = nextPath;
      entry.pageNode.dataset.tabId = identityKey;
    }
  }

  return {
    openDocument,
    openOrActivateDocument,
    findTabByDocument,
    activateTab,
    closeTab,
    closeAllTabs,
    getActiveDocumentRecord,
    getActiveRuntime,
    collectOpenDocumentRecords,
    startRename,
    updateTabPaths,
    startTemporaryDocumentCreation,
    finalizeActiveEditorContextBeforeTransition
  };
}

import { APP_CONFIG } from '../../config/app-config.js';

function createElement(tagName, className = '') {
  const node = document.createElement(tagName);

  if (className) {
    node.className = className;
  }

  return node;
}

export function showTextInputDialog({
  title,
  initialValue = '',
  confirmText = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.create,
  cancelText = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.cancel
}) {
  return new Promise((resolve) => {
    const overlay = createElement('div', APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.dialogOverlay);
    const modal = createElement('div', APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.dialog);
    const titleNode = createElement('div', APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.dialogTitle);
    titleNode.textContent = title;

    const input = createElement('input', APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.dialogInput);
    input.type = 'text';
    input.value = initialValue;

    const actions = createElement('div', APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.dialogActions);
    const cancelButton = createElement('button', APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.dialogButton);
    cancelButton.type = 'button';
    cancelButton.textContent = cancelText;

    const confirmButton = createElement('button', `${APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.dialogButton} ${APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.dialogPrimaryButton}`);
    confirmButton.type = 'button';
    confirmButton.textContent = confirmText;

    const close = (value) => {
      overlay.remove();
      resolve(value);
    };

    cancelButton.addEventListener('click', () => close(null));
    confirmButton.addEventListener('click', () => {
      const value = input.value.trim();
      close(value || null);
    });

    input.addEventListener('keydown', (event) => {
      if (event.key === 'Enter') {
        event.preventDefault();
        confirmButton.click();
      }

      if (event.key === 'Escape') {
        event.preventDefault();
        cancelButton.click();
      }
    });

    actions.appendChild(cancelButton);
    actions.appendChild(confirmButton);
    modal.appendChild(titleNode);
    modal.appendChild(input);
    modal.appendChild(actions);
    overlay.appendChild(modal);
    document.body.appendChild(overlay);

    input.focus();
    input.select();
  });
}

export function showSaveChangesDialog({
  title = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.saveChangesTitle,
  saveText = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.save,
  discardText = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.discard,
  cancelText = APP_CONFIG.ui.text.cancel
}) {
  return new Promise((resolve) => {
    const overlay = createElement('div', APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.dialogOverlay);
    const modal = createElement('div', APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.dialog);
    const titleNode = createElement('div', APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.dialogTitle);
    titleNode.textContent = title;

    const actions = createElement('div', APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.dialogActions);
    const cancelButton = createElement('button', APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.dialogButton);
    cancelButton.type = 'button';
    cancelButton.textContent = cancelText;

    const discardButton = createElement('button', APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.dialogButton);
    discardButton.type = 'button';
    discardButton.textContent = discardText;

    const saveButton = createElement('button', `${APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.dialogButton} ${APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames.dialogPrimaryButton}`);
    saveButton.type = 'button';
    saveButton.textContent = saveText;

    const close = (value) => {
      overlay.remove();
      resolve(value);
    };

    cancelButton.addEventListener('click', () => close(APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.dialogResults.cancel));
    discardButton.addEventListener('click', () => close(APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.dialogResults.discard));
    saveButton.addEventListener('click', () => close(APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.dialogResults.save));

    overlay.addEventListener('click', (event) => {
      if (event.target === overlay) {
        close(APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.dialogResults.cancel);
      }
    });

    actions.appendChild(cancelButton);
    actions.appendChild(discardButton);
    actions.appendChild(saveButton);
    modal.appendChild(titleNode);
    modal.appendChild(actions);
    overlay.appendChild(modal);
    document.body.appendChild(overlay);

    saveButton.focus();
  });
}

import { APP_CONFIG } from '../../config/app-config.js';

export async function finalizeEditingBeforeContextTransition({
  activeEntry,
  logger,
  source,
  reason,
  blockOnFailure = true
}) {
  const transitionOutcomes = APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.transitionOutcomes;

  if (!activeEntry?.runtime) {
    return { continued: true, outcome: transitionOutcomes.noOp, reason };
  }

  const runtime = activeEntry.runtime;

  try {
    if (typeof runtime.finalizeEditingBeforeContextLeave === 'function') {
      const result = await runtime.finalizeEditingBeforeContextLeave({ reason, blockOnFailure });
      return {
        continued: result?.continued !== false,
        outcome: result?.outcome || transitionOutcomes.noOp,
        reason: result?.reason || reason
      };
    }

    if (typeof runtime.finishActiveTableEditing === 'function') {
      const outcome = await runtime.finishActiveTableEditing();
      return { continued: true, outcome: outcome || transitionOutcomes.noOp, reason };
    }

    return { continued: true, outcome: transitionOutcomes.noOp, reason };
  } catch (error) {
    logger?.error?.(source, 'Ошибка завершения редактирования перед сменой контекста', {
      tabId: activeEntry.tabId,
      reason,
      message: error?.message || String(error)
    });

    return {
      continued: blockOnFailure ? false : true,
      outcome: transitionOutcomes.failed,
      reason
    };
  }
}

import { APP_CONFIG } from '../../../config/app-config.js';
import { getDocumentLabel, getDocumentIdentityKey } from '../../runtime/documentRecordIdentity.js';

export const TREE_NODE_TYPES = APP_CONFIG.project.tree.nodeTypes;
export const TREE_ACTION_IDS = APP_CONFIG.project.tree.actionIds;

const TREE_CLASS_NAMES = APP_CONFIG.ui.classNames;

const MODULE_ROW_CLASS_BY_MODULE = {
  [APP_CONFIG.project.moduleIds.metagen]: TREE_CLASS_NAMES.treeNodeModuleMetagen,
  [APP_CONFIG.project.moduleIds.metalab]: TREE_CLASS_NAMES.treeNodeModuleMetalab,
  [APP_CONFIG.project.moduleIds.metaview]: TREE_CLASS_NAMES.treeNodeModuleMetaview
};

const DOCUMENT_ROW_CLASS_BY_MODULE = {
  [APP_CONFIG.project.moduleIds.metagen]: TREE_CLASS_NAMES.treeNodeDocumentMetagen,
  [APP_CONFIG.project.moduleIds.metalab]: TREE_CLASS_NAMES.treeNodeDocumentMetalab,
  [APP_CONFIG.project.moduleIds.metaview]: TREE_CLASS_NAMES.treeNodeDocumentMetaview
};

export function createTreeBehaviorConfig() {
  return {
    inlineRenameEnabled: false,
    slowDoubleClickRenameEnabled: false
  };
}

export function buildProjectTreeNodes({ project, moduleSections, getDocumentsByModule }) {
  if (!project) {
    return [];
  }

  return [
    {
      nodeType: TREE_NODE_TYPES.project,
      id: `${APP_CONFIG.project.identity.treeProjectPrefix}${project.project?.id || APP_CONFIG.project.defaults.unnamedProject}`,
      label: APP_CONFIG.project.tree.labels.root,
      project
    },
    ...moduleSections.map((sectionConfig) => ({
      nodeType: TREE_NODE_TYPES.module,
      id: `${APP_CONFIG.project.identity.treeModulePrefix}${sectionConfig.moduleId}`,
      moduleId: sectionConfig.moduleId,
      moduleName: sectionConfig.moduleName,
      label: sectionConfig.moduleName,
      sectionConfig,
      children: getDocumentsByModule(sectionConfig.moduleId).map((documentRecord) => ({
        nodeType: TREE_NODE_TYPES.document,
        id: getDocumentIdentityKey(documentRecord),
        label: getDocumentLabel(documentRecord),
        moduleId: sectionConfig.moduleId,
        path: documentRecord.path,
        documentRecord
      }))
    }))
  ];
}

export function getNodeActions(nodeData) {
  if (nodeData?.nodeType === TREE_NODE_TYPES.module) {
    return [{
      id: TREE_ACTION_IDS.createComponent,
      title: APP_CONFIG.ui.tree.actions.createComponent.title,
      iconAssetPath: APP_CONFIG.ui.tree.actions.createComponent.iconAssetPath,
      visible: true
    }];
  }

  if (nodeData?.nodeType === TREE_NODE_TYPES.document) {
    return [{
      id: TREE_ACTION_IDS.deleteComponent,
      title: APP_CONFIG.ui.tree.actions.deleteComponent.title,
      iconAssetPath: APP_CONFIG.ui.tree.actions.deleteComponent.iconAssetPath,
      visible: true
    }];
  }

  return [];
}

export function getNodeRowClassNames(nodeData) {
  if (nodeData?.nodeType === TREE_NODE_TYPES.project) {
    return [TREE_CLASS_NAMES.treeNodeProjectRow];
  }

  if (nodeData?.nodeType === TREE_NODE_TYPES.module) {
    return [MODULE_ROW_CLASS_BY_MODULE[nodeData.moduleId]].filter(Boolean);
  }

  if (nodeData?.nodeType === TREE_NODE_TYPES.document) {
    return [DOCUMENT_ROW_CLASS_BY_MODULE[nodeData.moduleId]].filter(Boolean);
  }

  return [];
}

export function createTreeInteractionController({ tabs, onCreateComponentRequest, onDeleteComponentRequest }) {
  async function onNodePrimaryClick(nodeData) {
    if (nodeData?.nodeType !== TREE_NODE_TYPES.document) {
      return { handled: false, reason: APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.treeInteractionReasons.nonDocumentNode };
    }

    await tabs.openOrActivateDocument(nodeData.documentRecord);
    return { handled: true, reason: APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.treeInteractionReasons.documentOpenOrActivate };
  }

  async function onNodeActionClick({ actionId, nodeData, event }) {
    if (event) {
      event.preventDefault();
      event.stopPropagation();
    }

    if (actionId === TREE_ACTION_IDS.createComponent && nodeData?.nodeType === TREE_NODE_TYPES.module) {
      await onCreateComponentRequest?.(nodeData.moduleId, nodeData);
      return { handled: true, reason: TREE_ACTION_IDS.createComponent };
    }

    if (actionId === TREE_ACTION_IDS.deleteComponent && nodeData?.nodeType === TREE_NODE_TYPES.document) {
      await onDeleteComponentRequest?.(nodeData.documentRecord, nodeData);
      return { handled: true, reason: TREE_ACTION_IDS.deleteComponent };
    }

    return { handled: false, reason: APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.treeInteractionReasons.unsupportedAction };
  }

  return { onNodePrimaryClick, onNodeActionClick };
}

import { APP_CONFIG } from '../../config/app-config.js';
import { finalizeEditingBeforeContextTransition } from './editorContextLifecycle.js';

export async function finalizeEditingBeforeTabSwitch({ activeEntry, nextTabId, logger }) {
  if (!activeEntry || activeEntry.tabId === nextTabId) {
    return true;
  }

  const result = await finalizeEditingBeforeContextTransition({
    activeEntry,
    logger,
    source: APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.loggerSources.tabs,
    reason: APP_CONFIG.ui.runtime.transitionReasons.tabSwitch,
    blockOnFailure: true
  });

  if (!result.continued) {
    return false;
  }

  return true;
}

==================================================
FILE: rtb/README.md
==================================================

# MetaPlatform

Web-only IDE runtime: frontend on Vite + runtime backend on FastAPI.

## Project Runtime

- **Renderer UI** - web interface for the application.
- **Vite** - dev server for frontend.
- **Runtime backend** - Python API, backend workspace, import/export, process execution, lock/heartbeat/save/close semantics.

## Main Workflows

- **Primary flow:** backend workspace.
- **File operations:** only **import/export**.
- Backend runs **separately**.
- `npm run dev` **does not start backend**.

### Backend workspace

- Browse backend projects
- Create backend project
- Open backend project
- Save backend project
- Save As as a workspace copy
- Close backend project
- Delete backend project

### File operations

- **Import**
- **Export**

## Install

From repository root:

```bash
cd ui && npm install
python -m pip install -r rtb/requirements.txt
```

## Run In Development

Use **two terminals** from repository root.

### Terminal 1 - backend

```bash
python -m uvicorn rtb.app.main:app --host 127.0.0.1 --port 8000
```

### Terminal 2 - web UI

```bash
cd ui && npm run dev
```

## Test Suite

From repository root:

```bash
cd ./ui && npm.cmd test
cd ./ui && npm.cmd run test:integration
cd ./ui && npm.cmd run test:backend
```

Full required run:

```bash
cd ./ui && npm.cmd run test:all
```

﻿from fastapi import FastAPI

from rtb.app.api.commands import router as commands_router
from rtb.app.db.bootstrap import bootstrap_storage
from rtb.app.services.command_dispatcher import process_execution_service

app = FastAPI(title='MetaPlatform Runtime Backend')


@app.on_event('startup')
def _startup() -> None:
    bootstrap_storage()


@app.on_event('shutdown')
def _shutdown() -> None:
    process_execution_service.stop_active_process_if_any()


app.include_router(commands_router)

﻿from pathlib import Path
from typing import Any
from email.parser import BytesParser
from email.policy import default as email_default_policy

from fastapi import APIRouter, BackgroundTasks, HTTPException, Request
from fastapi.responses import FileResponse
from pydantic import ValidationError

from rtb.app.core.constants import (
    API_COMMANDS_ENDPOINT,
    API_PROJECT_EXPORTS_ENDPOINT,
    API_PROJECT_IMPORTS_ENDPOINT,
    COMMANDS,
    ERROR_CODES,
    PROJECT_IMPORT_POLICY,
)
from rtb.app.core.settings import SETTINGS
from rtb.app.models.command import CommandRequest
from rtb.app.services.command_dispatcher import (
    dispatch_command,
    ensure_platform_command_allowed_while_process_active,
    make_error_response,
    project_storage_service,
)
from rtb.app.services.errors import ActiveProcessBusyIssue, ProjectCreateIssue, ProjectImportIssue, ValidationIssue

router = APIRouter()


def _cleanup_export_artifact(path: Path) -> None:
    path.unlink(missing_ok=True)


def _extract_archive_from_multipart(content_type: str, body: bytes) -> tuple[str, bytes]:
    normalized_content_type = str(content_type or '').strip()
    if 'multipart/form-data' not in normalized_content_type.lower() or 'boundary=' not in normalized_content_type:
        raise ValidationIssue(
            'Multipart form-data payload is required',
            {'field': PROJECT_IMPORT_POLICY['archive_field_name']},
        )

    mime_message = BytesParser(policy=email_default_policy).parsebytes(
        (
            f'Content-Type: {normalized_content_type}\r\n'
            'MIME-Version: 1.0\r\n\r\n'
        ).encode('utf-8')
        + body
    )
    if not mime_message.is_multipart():
        raise ValidationIssue(
            'Multipart form-data payload is required',
            {'field': PROJECT_IMPORT_POLICY['archive_field_name']},
        )

    for part in mime_message.iter_parts():
        field_name = str(part.get_param('name', header='content-disposition') or '').strip()
        if field_name != PROJECT_IMPORT_POLICY['archive_field_name']:
            continue
        file_name = Path(str(part.get_filename() or '').strip()).name
        file_bytes = bytes(part.get_payload(decode=True) or b'')
        return file_name, file_bytes

    raise ValidationIssue(
        'Project archive field is required',
        {'field': PROJECT_IMPORT_POLICY['archive_field_name']},
    )


@router.post(API_COMMANDS_ENDPOINT)
def handle_commands(raw_payload: dict[str, Any], request: Request):
    request_id = str(raw_payload.get('requestId', '')).strip()
    request_user_id = str(
        request.headers.get(SETTINGS.request_user_id_header, SETTINGS.default_user_id)
    ).strip() or SETTINGS.default_user_id

    try:
        command_request = CommandRequest.model_validate(raw_payload)
    except ValidationError as error:
        return make_error_response(
            request_id,
            ERROR_CODES['validation'],
            'Invalid request payload',
            {'reason': str(error)},
        )

    return dispatch_command(command_request, user_id=request_user_id)


@router.get(f'{API_PROJECT_EXPORTS_ENDPOINT}' + '/{export_token}')
def download_project_export(export_token: str, background_tasks: BackgroundTasks):
    artifact = project_storage_service.consume_project_export_artifact(export_token)
    if artifact is None:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail='Project export not found')

    artifact_path = Path(str(artifact['path']))
    background_tasks.add_task(_cleanup_export_artifact, artifact_path)

    return FileResponse(
        artifact_path,
        media_type='application/zip',
        filename=str(artifact['fileName']),
    )


@router.post(API_PROJECT_IMPORTS_ENDPOINT)
async def import_project_archive(request: Request):
    request_id = PROJECT_IMPORT_POLICY['request_id']
    try:
        ensure_platform_command_allowed_while_process_active(COMMANDS['platform']['import_project'])
        normalized_file_name, archive_bytes = _extract_archive_from_multipart(
            content_type=request.headers.get('content-type', ''),
            body=await request.body(),
        )
        if not normalized_file_name:
            raise ValidationIssue(
                'Project archive filename is required',
                {'field': PROJECT_IMPORT_POLICY['archive_field_name']},
            )
        if Path(normalized_file_name).suffix.lower() != PROJECT_IMPORT_POLICY['archive_extension']:
            raise ProjectImportIssue(
                'Project archive must be a .zip file',
                {
                    'field': PROJECT_IMPORT_POLICY['archive_field_name'],
                    'fileName': normalized_file_name,
                    'reason': PROJECT_IMPORT_POLICY['invalid_zip_reason'],
                },
            )

        return {
            'ok': True,
            'result': project_storage_service.import_project_archive(
                archive_name=normalized_file_name,
                archive_bytes=archive_bytes,
            ),
        }
    except ValidationIssue as error:
        return make_error_response(
            request_id,
            ERROR_CODES['validation'],
            str(error),
            error.details,
        ).model_dump(by_alias=True)
    except ProjectCreateIssue as error:
        return make_error_response(
            request_id,
            ERROR_CODES['project_create_failed'],
            str(error),
            error.details,
        ).model_dump(by_alias=True)
    except ProjectImportIssue as error:
        error_reason = str((error.details or {}).get('reason', '')).strip()
        error_code = (
            ERROR_CODES['project_import_invalid_archive']
            if error_reason in PROJECT_IMPORT_POLICY['invalid_archive_reasons']
            else ERROR_CODES['project_import_failed']
        )
        return make_error_response(
            request_id,
            error_code,
            str(error),
            error.details,
        ).model_dump(by_alias=True)
    except ActiveProcessBusyIssue as error:
        return make_error_response(
            request_id,
            ERROR_CODES['active_process_busy'],
            str(error),
            error.details,
        ).model_dump(by_alias=True)

﻿from dataclasses import dataclass
from pathlib import Path

from .constants import (
    DEFAULT_USER,
    PROCESS_EXECUTION,
    PROJECT_LOCKS,
    RUNTIME_DATA_DIR_NAME,
    SQLITE_FILE_NAME,
    WORKSPACE_DELETED_PROJECTS_DIR,
    WORKSPACE_EXPORTS_DIR,
    WORKSPACE_IMPORTS_DIR,
    WORKSPACE_PROJECTS_DIR,
)


@dataclass(frozen=True)
class Settings:
    runtime_root: Path
    data_root: Path
    sqlite_path: Path
    workspace_projects_root: Path
    workspace_deleted_projects_root: Path
    workspace_project_exports_root: Path
    workspace_project_imports_root: Path
    default_user_id: str
    default_username: str
    request_user_id_header: str
    lock_ttl_seconds: int
    lock_heartbeat_interval_seconds: int
    session_mode_edit: str
    process_stream_drain_timeout_seconds: float
    process_stop_soft_timeout_seconds: float
    process_stop_force_timeout_seconds: float


def load_settings() -> Settings:
    runtime_root = Path(__file__).resolve().parents[2]
    data_root = runtime_root / RUNTIME_DATA_DIR_NAME
    return Settings(
        runtime_root=runtime_root,
        data_root=data_root,
        sqlite_path=data_root / SQLITE_FILE_NAME,
        workspace_projects_root=data_root / WORKSPACE_PROJECTS_DIR,
        workspace_deleted_projects_root=data_root / WORKSPACE_DELETED_PROJECTS_DIR,
        workspace_project_exports_root=data_root / WORKSPACE_EXPORTS_DIR,
        workspace_project_imports_root=data_root / WORKSPACE_IMPORTS_DIR,
        default_user_id=DEFAULT_USER['id'],
        default_username=DEFAULT_USER['username'],
        request_user_id_header=PROJECT_LOCKS['request_user_id_header'],
        lock_ttl_seconds=int(PROJECT_LOCKS['ttl_seconds']),
        lock_heartbeat_interval_seconds=int(PROJECT_LOCKS['heartbeat_interval_seconds']),
        session_mode_edit=PROJECT_LOCKS['session_mode_edit'],
        process_stream_drain_timeout_seconds=float(PROCESS_EXECUTION['stream_policy']['drain_timeout_seconds']),
        process_stop_soft_timeout_seconds=float(PROCESS_EXECUTION['stop_policy']['soft_timeout_seconds']),
        process_stop_force_timeout_seconds=float(PROCESS_EXECUTION['stop_policy']['force_timeout_seconds']),
    )


SETTINGS = load_settings()

﻿import sqlite3
from pathlib import Path

from rtb.app.core.settings import SETTINGS
from rtb.app.utils.time_utils import utc_now_iso


def connect(sqlite_path: Path | None = None) -> sqlite3.Connection:
    target = sqlite_path or SETTINGS.sqlite_path
    connection = sqlite3.connect(target)
    connection.row_factory = sqlite3.Row
    connection.execute('PRAGMA foreign_keys = ON;')
    return connection


def bootstrap_storage() -> None:
    SETTINGS.data_root.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    SETTINGS.workspace_projects_root.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    SETTINGS.workspace_deleted_projects_root.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    SETTINGS.workspace_project_exports_root.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    SETTINGS.workspace_project_imports_root.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

    with connect() as db:
        db.executescript(
            '''
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS users (
                id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
                username TEXT NOT NULL UNIQUE,
                created_at TEXT NOT NULL,
                updated_at TEXT NOT NULL
            );

            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS projects (
                id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
                user_id TEXT NOT NULL,
                name TEXT NOT NULL,
                slug TEXT NOT NULL UNIQUE,
                root_path TEXT NOT NULL,
                project_file_path TEXT NOT NULL,
                deleted_at TEXT NULL,
                deleted_root_path TEXT NULL,
                created_at TEXT NOT NULL,
                updated_at TEXT NOT NULL,
                FOREIGN KEY(user_id) REFERENCES users(id)
            );

            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS project_locks (
                project_id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
                user_id TEXT NOT NULL,
                lock_token TEXT NOT NULL,
                acquired_at TEXT NOT NULL,
                last_heartbeat_at TEXT NOT NULL,
                expires_at TEXT NOT NULL,
                created_at TEXT NOT NULL,
                updated_at TEXT NOT NULL,
                FOREIGN KEY(project_id) REFERENCES projects(id),
                FOREIGN KEY(user_id) REFERENCES users(id)
            );

            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS project_sessions (
                session_id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
                project_id TEXT NOT NULL,
                user_id TEXT NOT NULL,
                lock_token TEXT NOT NULL,
                opened_at TEXT NOT NULL,
                last_seen_at TEXT NOT NULL,
                mode TEXT NOT NULL,
                is_active INTEGER NOT NULL,
                closed_at TEXT NULL,
                created_at TEXT NOT NULL,
                updated_at TEXT NOT NULL,
                FOREIGN KEY(project_id) REFERENCES projects(id),
                FOREIGN KEY(user_id) REFERENCES users(id)
            );

            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS process_runs (
                process_id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
                command_id TEXT NOT NULL,
                status TEXT NOT NULL,
                pid INTEGER NULL,
                stop_requested INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
                exit_code INTEGER NULL,
                started_at TEXT NOT NULL,
                finished_at TEXT NULL,
                created_at TEXT NOT NULL,
                updated_at TEXT NOT NULL
            );

            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS process_output_chunks (
                chunk_id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,
                process_id TEXT NOT NULL,
                stream TEXT NOT NULL,
                content TEXT NOT NULL,
                created_at TEXT NOT NULL,
                FOREIGN KEY(process_id) REFERENCES process_runs(process_id) ON DELETE CASCADE
            );
            '''
        )
        _ensure_projects_soft_delete_columns(db)
        _ensure_project_locks_columns(db)
        _ensure_project_sessions_columns(db)

        now = utc_now_iso()
        db.execute(
            '''
            INSERT INTO users(id, username, created_at, updated_at)
            VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?)
            ON CONFLICT(id) DO UPDATE SET
                username=excluded.username,
                updated_at=excluded.updated_at
            ''',
            (SETTINGS.default_user_id, SETTINGS.default_username, now, now),
        )
        db.commit()


def _ensure_projects_soft_delete_columns(db: sqlite3.Connection) -> None:
    columns = {
        row['name']
        for row in db.execute("PRAGMA table_info(projects)").fetchall()
    }

    if 'deleted_at' not in columns:
        db.execute('ALTER TABLE projects ADD COLUMN deleted_at TEXT NULL')

    if 'deleted_root_path' not in columns:
        db.execute('ALTER TABLE projects ADD COLUMN deleted_root_path TEXT NULL')


def _ensure_project_locks_columns(db: sqlite3.Connection) -> None:
    if not _table_exists(db, 'project_locks'):
        return

    columns = {
        row['name']
        for row in db.execute("PRAGMA table_info(project_locks)").fetchall()
    }
    canonical_columns = {
        'project_id',
        'user_id',
        'lock_token',
        'acquired_at',
        'last_heartbeat_at',
        'expires_at',
        'created_at',
        'updated_at',
    }
    # Do not attempt pseudo-migration of lock schema through ALTER TABLE:
    # primary key/required columns must come from canonical CREATE TABLE bootstrap.
    if not canonical_columns.issubset(columns):
        return


def _ensure_project_sessions_columns(db: sqlite3.Connection) -> None:
    if not _table_exists(db, 'project_sessions'):
        return

    columns = {
        row['name']
        for row in db.execute("PRAGMA table_info(project_sessions)").fetchall()
    }
    canonical_required_columns = {
        'session_id',
        'project_id',
        'user_id',
        'lock_token',
        'opened_at',
        'last_seen_at',
        'mode',
        'is_active',
        'created_at',
        'updated_at',
    }
    # Same policy as locks: avoid partial ALTER-based migration for required columns.
    if not canonical_required_columns.issubset(columns):
        return

    # Optional lifecycle column can be added safely for already canonical-compatible schemas.
    if 'closed_at' not in columns:
        db.execute('ALTER TABLE project_sessions ADD COLUMN closed_at TEXT NULL')


def _table_exists(db: sqlite3.Connection, table_name: str) -> bool:
    row = db.execute(
        "SELECT 1 FROM sqlite_master WHERE type = 'table' AND name = ?",
        (table_name,),
    ).fetchone()
    return row is not None

﻿from typing import Any

from pydantic import BaseModel, Field, model_validator


class CommandRequest(BaseModel):
    request_id: str = Field(alias='requestId', min_length=1)
    module: str = Field(min_length=1)
    command: str = Field(min_length=1)
    payload: dict[str, Any] = Field(default_factory=dict)


class CommandError(BaseModel):
    code: str
    message: str
    details: dict[str, Any] | None = None


class CommandResponse(BaseModel):
    request_id: str = Field(alias='requestId')
    ok: bool
    result: dict[str, Any] | None = None
    error: CommandError | None = None

    @model_validator(mode='after')
    def validate_envelope(self) -> 'CommandResponse':
        if self.ok and self.error is not None:
            raise ValueError('ok response cannot contain error')
        if not self.ok and self.result is not None:
            raise ValueError('error response cannot contain result')
        return self

from typing import Any

from pydantic import BaseModel, Field


class ProjectSnapshotDocument(BaseModel):
    module_id: str = Field(alias='moduleId')
    path: str
    document: dict[str, Any]


class ProjectSnapshotProject(BaseModel):
    project_id: str = Field(alias='projectId')
    name: str
    slug: str
    updated_at: str = Field(alias='updatedAt')


class ProjectSnapshot(BaseModel):
    source: str
    project: ProjectSnapshotProject
    raw: dict[str, Any]
    documents: dict[str, list[ProjectSnapshotDocument]]


class ProjectSnapshotSave(BaseModel):
    raw: dict[str, Any]
    documents: dict[str, list[ProjectSnapshotDocument]]


class LockBoundProjectPayload(BaseModel):
    project_id: str = Field(alias='projectId')
    lock_token: str | None = Field(default=None, alias='lockToken')


class SaveAllPayload(LockBoundProjectPayload):
    project_snapshot: ProjectSnapshotSave = Field(alias='projectSnapshot')


class CloseProjectPayload(LockBoundProjectPayload):
    pass


class ProjectHeartbeatPayload(LockBoundProjectPayload):
    pass


class SaveProjectAsPayload(LockBoundProjectPayload):
    new_name: str = Field(alias='newName')
    project_snapshot: ProjectSnapshotSave = Field(alias='projectSnapshot')

==================================================
FILE: rtb/app/services/active_process_policy.py
