﻿from __future__ import annotations

from rtb.app.core.constants import ACTIVE_PROCESS_COMMAND_POLICY, PROCESS_EXECUTION
from rtb.app.services.errors import ActiveProcessBusyIssue


def is_command_allowed_during_active_process(command_id: str) -> bool:
    normalized_command_id = str(command_id or '').strip()
    if not normalized_command_id:
        return False

    allowed_commands = set(ACTIVE_PROCESS_COMMAND_POLICY['allow_during_active_process'])
    blocked_commands = set(ACTIVE_PROCESS_COMMAND_POLICY['block_during_active_process'])

    if normalized_command_id in allowed_commands:
        return True
    if normalized_command_id in blocked_commands:
        return False
    return True


def assert_command_allowed_during_active_process(*, command_id: str, active_process_state: dict) -> None:
    if not bool(active_process_state.get('isBlocking')):
        return

    if is_command_allowed_during_active_process(command_id):
        return

    raise ActiveProcessBusyIssue(
        PROCESS_EXECUTION['messages']['active_process_blocked'],
        {
            'command': str(command_id or '').strip(),
            'activeProcessId': str(active_process_state.get('processId') or '').strip() or None,
            'activeProcessStatus': str(active_process_state.get('status') or '').strip() or None,
        },
    )



==================================================
FILE: rtb/app/services/command_dispatcher.py
==================================================

﻿from pydantic import ValidationError

from rtb.app.core.constants import COMMANDS, ERROR_CODES
from rtb.app.core.settings import SETTINGS
from rtb.app.models.command import CommandRequest, CommandResponse
from rtb.app.services import project_catalog
from rtb.app.services.active_process_policy import assert_command_allowed_during_active_process
from rtb.app.services.errors import (
    ActiveProcessBusyIssue,
    LostProjectLockIssue,
    NoActiveProcessIssue,
    ProcessStopFailedIssue,
    ProjectCreateIssue,
    ProjectDeleteIssue,
    ProjectExportIssue,
    ProjectLockedIssue,
    ProjectNotFoundIssue,
    ProjectOpenIssue,
    ProjectSaveIssue,
    ValidationIssue,
)
from rtb.app.services.process_execution import ProcessExecutionService
from rtb.app.services.project_storage import ProjectStorageService

project_storage_service = ProjectStorageService()
process_execution_service = ProcessExecutionService()


def ensure_platform_command_allowed_while_process_active(command_id: str) -> None:
    active_process_state = process_execution_service.get_active_process_blocking_state()
    assert_command_allowed_during_active_process(
        command_id=command_id,
        active_process_state=active_process_state,
    )


def make_ok_response(request_id: str, result: dict) -> CommandResponse:
    return CommandResponse(requestId=request_id, ok=True, result=result)


def make_error_response(request_id: str, code: str, message: str, details: dict | None = None) -> CommandResponse:
    return CommandResponse(
        requestId=request_id,
        ok=False,
        error={
            'code': code,
            'message': message,
            'details': details,
        },
    )


def dispatch_command(request: CommandRequest, *, user_id: str | None = None) -> CommandResponse:
    normalized_user_id = str(user_id or '').strip() or SETTINGS.default_user_id
    try:
        platform_module = COMMANDS['platform']['module']
        if request.module != platform_module:
            raise ValidationIssue('Unsupported module', {'module': request.module})

        ensure_platform_command_allowed_while_process_active(request.command)

        if request.command == COMMANDS['platform']['list_projects']:
            return make_ok_response(request.request_id, project_catalog.list_projects())

        if request.command == COMMANDS['platform']['create_project']:
            return make_ok_response(request.request_id, project_catalog.create_project(request.payload))

        if request.command == COMMANDS['platform']['open_project']:
            return make_ok_response(
                request.request_id,
                project_storage_service.open_project_snapshot(request.payload, user_id=normalized_user_id),
            )

        if request.command == COMMANDS['platform']['delete_project']:
            return make_ok_response(request.request_id, project_catalog.delete_project(request.payload))

        if request.command == COMMANDS['platform']['save_all']:
            return make_ok_response(
                request.request_id,
                project_storage_service.save_project_snapshot(request.payload, user_id=normalized_user_id),
            )

        if request.command == COMMANDS['platform']['close_project']:
            return make_ok_response(
                request.request_id,
                project_storage_service.close_project_session(request.payload, user_id=normalized_user_id),
            )

        if request.command == COMMANDS['platform']['project_heartbeat']:
            return make_ok_response(
                request.request_id,
                project_storage_service.heartbeat_project_session(request.payload, user_id=normalized_user_id),
            )

        if request.command == COMMANDS['platform']['save_project_as']:
            return make_ok_response(
                request.request_id,
                project_storage_service.save_project_snapshot_as(request.payload, user_id=normalized_user_id),
            )

        if request.command == COMMANDS['platform']['export_project']:
            return make_ok_response(request.request_id, project_storage_service.export_project_archive(request.payload))

        if request.command == COMMANDS['platform']['metagen_generate']:
            return make_ok_response(request.request_id, process_execution_service.start_metagen_generate(request.payload))

        if request.command == COMMANDS['platform']['process_get_state']:
            return make_ok_response(request.request_id, process_execution_service.get_active_state(request.payload))

        if request.command == COMMANDS['platform']['process_read_output']:
            return make_ok_response(request.request_id, process_execution_service.read_output(request.payload))

        if request.command == COMMANDS['platform']['process_stop']:
            return make_ok_response(request.request_id, process_execution_service.stop_active_process(request.payload))

        raise ValidationIssue(
            'Unsupported command',
            {'module': request.module, 'command': request.command},
        )
    except ValidationIssue as error:
        return make_error_response(
            request.request_id,
            ERROR_CODES['validation'],
            str(error),
            error.details,
        )
    except ProjectCreateIssue as error:
        return make_error_response(
            request.request_id,
            ERROR_CODES['project_create_failed'],
            str(error),
            error.details,
        )
    except ProjectNotFoundIssue as error:
        return make_error_response(
            request.request_id,
            ERROR_CODES['project_not_found'],
            str(error),
            error.details,
        )
    except ProjectLockedIssue as error:
        return make_error_response(
            request.request_id,
            ERROR_CODES['project_locked'],
            str(error),
            error.details,
        )
    except ProjectOpenIssue as error:
        return make_error_response(
            request.request_id,
            ERROR_CODES['project_open_failed'],
            str(error),
            error.details,
        )
    except LostProjectLockIssue as error:
        return make_error_response(
            request.request_id,
            ERROR_CODES['lost_project_lock'],
            str(error),
            error.details,
        )
    except ProjectSaveIssue as error:
        return make_error_response(
            request.request_id,
            ERROR_CODES['project_save_failed'],
            str(error),
            error.details,
        )
    except ProjectDeleteIssue as error:
        return make_error_response(
            request.request_id,
            ERROR_CODES['project_delete_failed'],
            str(error),
            error.details,
        )
    except ProjectExportIssue as error:
        return make_error_response(
            request.request_id,
            ERROR_CODES['project_export_failed'],
            str(error),
            error.details,
        )
    except ActiveProcessBusyIssue as error:
        return make_error_response(
            request.request_id,
            ERROR_CODES['active_process_busy'],
            str(error),
            error.details,
        )
    except NoActiveProcessIssue as error:
        return make_error_response(
            request.request_id,
            ERROR_CODES['no_active_process'],
            str(error),
            error.details,
        )
    except ProcessStopFailedIssue as error:
        return make_error_response(
            request.request_id,
            ERROR_CODES['process_stop_failed'],
            str(error),
            error.details,
        )
    except (ValidationError, ValueError) as error:
        return make_error_response(
            request.request_id,
            ERROR_CODES['validation'],
            'Invalid request payload',
            {'reason': str(error)},
        )
    except Exception as error:  # noqa: BLE001
        return make_error_response(
            request.request_id,
            ERROR_CODES['internal'],
            'Unexpected internal error',
            {'reason': str(error)},
        )

﻿class ValidationIssue(Exception):
    def __init__(self, message: str, details: dict | None = None):
        super().__init__(message)
        self.details = details or {}


class ProjectCreateIssue(Exception):
    def __init__(self, message: str, details: dict | None = None):
        super().__init__(message)
        self.details = details or {}


class ProjectOpenIssue(Exception):
    def __init__(self, message: str, details: dict | None = None):
        super().__init__(message)
        self.details = details or {}


class ProjectNotFoundIssue(ProjectOpenIssue):
    pass


class ProjectLockedIssue(ProjectOpenIssue):
    pass


class ProjectSaveIssue(Exception):
    def __init__(self, message: str, details: dict | None = None):
        super().__init__(message)
        self.details = details or {}


class LostProjectLockIssue(ProjectSaveIssue):
    pass


class ProjectDeleteIssue(Exception):
    def __init__(self, message: str, details: dict | None = None):
        super().__init__(message)
        self.details = details or {}


class ProjectExportIssue(Exception):
    def __init__(self, message: str, details: dict | None = None):
        super().__init__(message)
        self.details = details or {}


class ProjectImportIssue(Exception):
    def __init__(self, message: str, details: dict | None = None):
        super().__init__(message)
        self.details = details or {}

    def __init__(self, message: str, details: dict | None = None):
        super().__init__(message)
        self.details = details or {}

    pass

    pass

﻿from __future__ import annotations

import subprocess
import sys
import threading
from dataclasses import dataclass
from typing import Any, TextIO
from uuid import uuid4

from rtb.app.core.constants import COMMANDS, PROCESS_EXECUTION
from rtb.app.core.settings import SETTINGS
from rtb.app.db.bootstrap import connect
from rtb.app.models.process_execution import (
    MetaGenGeneratePayload,
    ProcessReadOutputPayload,
    ProcessStatePayload,
    ProcessStopPayload,
)
from rtb.app.services.errors import ActiveProcessBusyIssue, NoActiveProcessIssue, ProcessStopFailedIssue, ValidationIssue
from rtb.app.utils.time_utils import utc_now_iso


@dataclass
class ActiveProcessHandle:
    process_id: str
    process: subprocess.Popen[str]
    stream_threads: list[threading.Thread]
    waiter_thread: threading.Thread


class ProcessExecutionService:
    def __init__(self, db_connect=connect):
        self._db_connect = db_connect
        self._lock = threading.Lock()
        self._active_process: ActiveProcessHandle | None = None

    def start_metagen_generate(self, payload: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
        try:
            generate_payload = MetaGenGeneratePayload.model_validate(payload or {})
        except Exception as error:  # noqa: BLE001
            raise ValidationIssue('Invalid MetaGen generate payload', {'reason': str(error)}) from error

        with self._lock:
            if self._active_process is not None and self._active_process.process.poll() is None:
                raise ActiveProcessBusyIssue(
                    'Active process is already running',
                    {'activeProcessId': self._active_process.process_id},
                )

            process_id = f'proc_{uuid4().hex}'
            command_id = COMMANDS['platform']['metagen_generate']
            args = self._build_metagen_runner_command(generate_payload)
            now_iso = utc_now_iso()

            try:
                process = subprocess.Popen(
                    args,
                    stdout=subprocess.PIPE,
                    stderr=subprocess.PIPE,
                    text=True,
                    encoding='utf-8',
                    errors='replace',
                    bufsize=1,
                )
            except Exception as error:  # noqa: BLE001
                raise ValidationIssue(
                    'Failed to start MetaGen process',
                    {'reason': str(error)},
                ) from error

            self._insert_process_run(
                process_id=process_id,
                command_id=command_id,
                status=PROCESS_EXECUTION['statuses']['running'],
                pid=process.pid,
                started_at=now_iso,
            )

            stream_threads: list[threading.Thread] = []
            stdout_thread = self._start_stream_consumer(
                process_id=process_id,
                stream_name=PROCESS_EXECUTION['streams']['stdout'],
                stream_pipe=process.stdout,
            )
            if stdout_thread is not None:
                stream_threads.append(stdout_thread)

            stderr_thread = self._start_stream_consumer(
                process_id=process_id,
                stream_name=PROCESS_EXECUTION['streams']['stderr'],
                stream_pipe=process.stderr,
            )
            if stderr_thread is not None:
                stream_threads.append(stderr_thread)

            waiter_thread = threading.Thread(
                target=self._wait_for_completion,
                args=(process_id, process, stream_threads),
                daemon=True,
            )
            waiter_thread.start()
            self._active_process = ActiveProcessHandle(
                process_id=process_id,
                process=process,
                stream_threads=stream_threads,
                waiter_thread=waiter_thread,
            )

        return {'process': self._read_process_state(process_id)}

    def get_active_state(self, payload: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
        try:
            ProcessStatePayload.model_validate(payload or {})
        except Exception as error:  # noqa: BLE001
            raise ValidationIssue('Invalid process state payload', {'reason': str(error)}) from error

        with self._lock:
            active_process_id = self._active_process.process_id if self._active_process is not None else None
            is_running = self._active_process is not None and self._active_process.process.poll() is None

        if not active_process_id or not is_running:
            return {'process': None}
        return {'process': self._read_process_state(active_process_id)}

    def read_output(self, payload: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
        try:
            read_payload = ProcessReadOutputPayload.model_validate(payload or {})
        except Exception as error:  # noqa: BLE001
            raise ValidationIssue('Invalid process output payload', {'reason': str(error)}) from error

        process_row = self._get_latest_process_row()
        if process_row is None:
            return {'process': None, 'chunks': []}

        chunks = self._read_output_chunks(
            process_id=str(process_row['process_id']),
            after_chunk_id=int(read_payload.after_chunk_id),
        )
        return {
            'process': self._serialize_process_row(process_row),
            'chunks': chunks,
        }

    def stop_active_process(self, payload: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
        try:
            ProcessStopPayload.model_validate(payload or {})
        except Exception as error:  # noqa: BLE001
            raise ValidationIssue('Invalid process stop payload', {'reason': str(error)}) from error

        with self._lock:
            handle = self._active_process

        if handle is None or handle.process.poll() is not None:
            raise NoActiveProcessIssue('No active process to stop')

        now_iso = utc_now_iso()
        self._mark_stop_requested(
            process_id=handle.process_id,
            status=PROCESS_EXECUTION['statuses']['stopping'],
            updated_at=now_iso,
        )

        soft_timeout = SETTINGS.process_stop_soft_timeout_seconds
        force_timeout = SETTINGS.process_stop_force_timeout_seconds

        try:
            handle.process.terminate()
            handle.process.wait(timeout=soft_timeout)
        except subprocess.TimeoutExpired:
            try:
                handle.process.kill()
                handle.process.wait(timeout=force_timeout)
            except Exception as error:  # noqa: BLE001
                raise ProcessStopFailedIssue(
                    'Failed to stop active process',
                    {'processId': handle.process_id, 'reason': str(error)},
                ) from error
        except Exception as error:  # noqa: BLE001
            raise ProcessStopFailedIssue(
                'Failed to stop active process',
                {'processId': handle.process_id, 'reason': str(error)},
            ) from error

        handle.waiter_thread.join(timeout=max(soft_timeout, force_timeout))
        return {'process': self._read_process_state(handle.process_id)}

    def stop_active_process_if_any(self) -> None:
        try:
            self.stop_active_process({})
        except NoActiveProcessIssue:
            return

    def get_active_process_blocking_state(self) -> dict[str, Any]:
        with self._lock:
            handle = self._active_process
            if handle is None:
                return {'isBlocking': False, 'processId': None, 'status': None}
            is_running = handle.process.poll() is None
            process_id = handle.process_id

        if not is_running:
            return {'isBlocking': False, 'processId': process_id, 'status': None}

        process_row = self._get_process_row(process_id)
        status = (
            str(process_row['status'])
            if process_row is not None and process_row['status'] is not None
            else PROCESS_EXECUTION['statuses']['running']
        )
        is_blocking = status in set(PROCESS_EXECUTION['active_statuses'])
        return {'isBlocking': is_blocking, 'processId': process_id, 'status': status}

    def _build_metagen_runner_command(self, payload: MetaGenGeneratePayload) -> list[str]:
        runner_policy = PROCESS_EXECUTION['metagen_runner']

        steps = self._bounded_int(
            payload.steps,
            default_value=runner_policy['default_steps'],
            min_value=runner_policy['min_steps'],
            max_value=runner_policy['max_steps'],
            field='steps',
        )
        step_delay_ms = self._bounded_int(
            payload.step_delay_ms,
            default_value=runner_policy['default_step_delay_ms'],
            min_value=runner_policy['min_step_delay_ms'],
            max_value=runner_policy['max_step_delay_ms'],
            field='stepDelayMs',
        )
        stderr_every = self._bounded_int(
            payload.stderr_every,
            default_value=runner_policy['default_stderr_every'],
            min_value=runner_policy['min_stderr_every'],
            max_value=runner_policy['max_stderr_every'],
            field='stderrEvery',
        )

        return [
            sys.executable,
            '-m',
            runner_policy['module_path'],
            '--steps',
            str(steps),
            '--step-delay-ms',
            str(step_delay_ms),
            '--stderr-every',
            str(stderr_every),
        ]

    @staticmethod
    def _bounded_int(
        value: int | None,
        *,
        default_value: int,
        min_value: int,
        max_value: int,
        field: str,
    ) -> int:
        if value is None:
            return default_value
        try:
            normalized = int(value)
        except (TypeError, ValueError) as error:
            raise ValidationIssue('Process parameter must be an integer', {'field': field}) from error
        if normalized < min_value or normalized > max_value:
            raise ValidationIssue(
                'Process parameter is out of allowed bounds',
                {'field': field, 'min': min_value, 'max': max_value},
            )
        return normalized

    def _wait_for_completion(
        self,
        process_id: str,
        process: subprocess.Popen[str],
        stream_threads: list[threading.Thread],
    ) -> None:
        return_code = process.wait()
        stream_drain_timeout = SETTINGS.process_stream_drain_timeout_seconds
        for stream_thread in stream_threads:
            stream_thread.join(timeout=stream_drain_timeout)
        row = self._get_process_row(process_id)
        stop_requested = bool(row and row['stop_requested'])

        status = PROCESS_EXECUTION['statuses']['stopped'] if stop_requested else (
            PROCESS_EXECUTION['statuses']['completed'] if return_code == 0 else PROCESS_EXECUTION['statuses']['failed']
        )
        now_iso = utc_now_iso()
        with self._db_connect() as db:
            db.execute(
                '''
                UPDATE process_runs
                SET status = ?, exit_code = ?, finished_at = ?, updated_at = ?
                WHERE process_id = ?
                ''',
                (status, int(return_code), now_iso, now_iso, process_id),
            )
            db.commit()

        with self._lock:
            if self._active_process is not None and self._active_process.process_id == process_id:
                self._active_process = None

    def _start_stream_consumer(
        self,
        *,
        process_id: str,
        stream_name: str,
        stream_pipe: TextIO | None,
    ) -> threading.Thread | None:
        if stream_pipe is None:
            return None

        thread = threading.Thread(
            target=self._consume_stream,
            args=(process_id, stream_name, stream_pipe),
            daemon=True,
        )
        thread.start()
        return thread

    def _consume_stream(self, process_id: str, stream_name: str, stream_pipe: TextIO) -> None:
        try:
            for line in iter(stream_pipe.readline, ''):
                content = line.rstrip('\r\n')
                self._append_output_chunk(
                    process_id=process_id,
                    stream_name=stream_name,
                    content=content,
                )
        finally:
            stream_pipe.close()

    def _insert_process_run(self, *, process_id: str, command_id: str, status: str, pid: int, started_at: str) -> None:
        with self._db_connect() as db:
            db.execute(
                '''
                INSERT INTO process_runs(
                    process_id, command_id, status, pid, stop_requested, exit_code, started_at, finished_at, created_at, updated_at
                )
                VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, 0, NULL, ?, NULL, ?, ?)
                ''',
                (process_id, command_id, status, int(pid), started_at, started_at, started_at),
            )
            db.commit()

    def _mark_stop_requested(self, *, process_id: str, status: str, updated_at: str) -> None:
        with self._db_connect() as db:
            db.execute(
                '''
                UPDATE process_runs
                SET stop_requested = 1, status = ?, updated_at = ?
                WHERE process_id = ?
                ''',
                (status, updated_at, process_id),
            )
            db.commit()

    def _append_output_chunk(self, *, process_id: str, stream_name: str, content: str) -> None:
        with self._db_connect() as db:
            db.execute(
                '''
                INSERT INTO process_output_chunks(process_id, stream, content, created_at)
                VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?)
                ''',
                (process_id, stream_name, content, utc_now_iso()),
            )
            db.commit()

    def _get_latest_process_row(self):
        with self._db_connect() as db:
            return db.execute(
                '''
                SELECT process_id, command_id, status, pid, stop_requested, exit_code, started_at, finished_at, created_at, updated_at
                FROM process_runs
                ORDER BY created_at DESC, process_id DESC
                LIMIT 1
                '''
            ).fetchone()

    def _get_process_row(self, process_id: str):
        with self._db_connect() as db:
            return db.execute(
                '''
                SELECT process_id, command_id, status, pid, stop_requested, exit_code, started_at, finished_at, created_at, updated_at
                FROM process_runs
                WHERE process_id = ?
                ''',
                (process_id,),
            ).fetchone()

    def _read_process_state(self, process_id: str) -> dict[str, Any] | None:
        row = self._get_process_row(process_id)
        if row is None:
            return None
        return self._serialize_process_row(row)

    def _read_output_chunks(self, *, process_id: str, after_chunk_id: int) -> list[dict[str, Any]]:
        with self._db_connect() as db:
            rows = db.execute(
                '''
                SELECT chunk_id, stream, content, created_at
                FROM process_output_chunks
                WHERE process_id = ? AND chunk_id > ?
                ORDER BY chunk_id ASC
                ''',
                (process_id, after_chunk_id),
            ).fetchall()

        return [
            {
                'chunkId': int(row['chunk_id']),
                'stream': str(row['stream']),
                'content': str(row['content']),
                'createdAt': str(row['created_at']),
            }
            for row in rows
        ]

    @staticmethod
    def _serialize_process_row(row) -> dict[str, Any]:
        return {
            'processId': str(row['process_id']),
            'command': str(row['command_id']),
            'status': str(row['status']),
            'pid': int(row['pid']) if row['pid'] is not None else None,
            'stopRequested': bool(row['stop_requested']),
            'exitCode': int(row['exit_code']) if row['exit_code'] is not None else None,
            'startedAt': str(row['started_at']),
            'finishedAt': str(row['finished_at']) if row['finished_at'] is not None else None,
            'updatedAt': str(row['updated_at']),
        }



==================================================
FILE: rtb/app/services/project_catalog.py

﻿from __future__ import annotations

import shutil
from dataclasses import dataclass
from pathlib import Path

from rtb.app.core.constants import PROJECT_STRUCTURE
from rtb.app.core.settings import SETTINGS
from rtb.app.db.bootstrap import connect
from rtb.app.services.errors import ProjectCreateIssue, ProjectDeleteIssue, ProjectNotFoundIssue, ValidationIssue
from rtb.app.utils.id_utils import make_project_id, slugify
from rtb.app.utils.time_utils import utc_now_iso


@dataclass(frozen=True)
class PreparedProjectMetadata:
    project_id: str
    name: str
    slug: str
    root_path: Path
    project_file_path: Path
    created_at: str
    updated_at: str


def _to_summary(row) -> dict:
    locked_by_user_id = str(row['locked_by_user_id'] or '').strip()
    locked_by_display_name = str(row['locked_by_display_name'] or '').strip()
    locked_by = None
    if locked_by_user_id:
        locked_by = {
            'userId': locked_by_user_id,
            'displayName': locked_by_display_name or locked_by_user_id,
        }

    return {
        'id': row['id'],
        'name': row['name'],
        'slug': row['slug'],
        'updatedAt': row['updated_at'],
        'lockedBy': locked_by,
    }


def cleanup_stale_project_runtime_state(*, db, project_id: str | None = None, now_iso: str | None = None) -> None:
    normalized_project_id = str(project_id or '').strip()
    normalized_now_iso = str(now_iso or '').strip() or utc_now_iso()

    query = '''
        SELECT project_id
        FROM project_locks
        WHERE expires_at <= ?
    '''
    params: list[str] = [normalized_now_iso]
    if normalized_project_id:
        query += ' AND project_id = ?'
        params.append(normalized_project_id)

    stale_rows = db.execute(query, tuple(params)).fetchall()
    stale_project_ids = [str(row['project_id']) for row in stale_rows if str(row['project_id'] or '').strip()]
    if not stale_project_ids:
        return

    placeholders = ','.join(['?'] * len(stale_project_ids))
    db.execute(
        f'''
        UPDATE project_sessions
        SET
            is_active = 0,
            closed_at = COALESCE(closed_at, ?),
            last_seen_at = ?,
            updated_at = ?
        WHERE is_active = 1 AND project_id IN ({placeholders})
        ''',
        (normalized_now_iso, normalized_now_iso, normalized_now_iso, *stale_project_ids),
    )
    db.execute(
        f'''
        DELETE FROM project_locks
        WHERE project_id IN ({placeholders})
        ''',
        tuple(stale_project_ids),
    )


def _serialize_project_yaml(project_id: str, project_name: str) -> str:
    escaped_name = project_name.replace('"', '\\"')
    lines = [
        f"kind: {PROJECT_STRUCTURE['kind']}",
        f"version: {PROJECT_STRUCTURE['version']}",
        'project:',
        f'  id: "{project_id}"',
        f'  name: "{escaped_name}"',
        '  description: ""',
        'modules:',
    ]

    for item in PROJECT_STRUCTURE['module_display_names']:
        lines.append(f'  - {item}')

    lines.extend(
        [
            'paths:',
            f"  metagen: {PROJECT_STRUCTURE['module_dirs'][0]}",
            f"  metalab: {PROJECT_STRUCTURE['module_dirs'][1]}",
            f"  metaview: {PROJECT_STRUCTURE['module_dirs'][2]}",
            f"  generated: {PROJECT_STRUCTURE['generated_dir']}",
            '',
        ]
    )
    return '\n'.join(lines)


def _next_available_slug(base_slug: str) -> str:
    with connect() as db:
        slug = base_slug
        suffix = 2
        while True:
            existing = db.execute('SELECT 1 FROM projects WHERE slug = ?', (slug,)).fetchone()
            if existing is None:
                return slug
            slug = f'{base_slug}-{suffix}'
            suffix += 1


def validate_project_name(name: str, *, field: str = 'name') -> str:
    normalized = str(name or '').strip()
    if not normalized:
        raise ValidationIssue('Project name is required', {'field': field})

    if len(normalized) > 120:
        raise ValidationIssue('Project name is too long', {'field': field, 'maxLength': 120})

    return normalized


def prepare_new_project_metadata(name: str, *, field: str = 'name') -> PreparedProjectMetadata:
    normalized_name = validate_project_name(name, field=field)
    base_slug = slugify(normalized_name)
    if not base_slug:
        raise ValidationIssue('Project name cannot be transformed into slug', {'field': field})

    slug = _next_available_slug(base_slug)
    project_id = make_project_id()
    now = utc_now_iso()
    project_root: Path = SETTINGS.workspace_projects_root / slug
    project_file_path = project_root / PROJECT_STRUCTURE['project_file_name']

    return PreparedProjectMetadata(
        project_id=project_id,
        name=normalized_name,
        slug=slug,
        root_path=project_root,
        project_file_path=project_file_path,
        created_at=now,
        updated_at=now,
    )


def register_prepared_project(metadata: PreparedProjectMetadata) -> dict:
    try:
        with connect() as db:
            db.execute(
                '''
                INSERT INTO projects(id, user_id, name, slug, root_path, project_file_path, created_at, updated_at)
                VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)
                ''',
                (
                    metadata.project_id,
                    SETTINGS.default_user_id,
                    metadata.name,
                    metadata.slug,
                    metadata.root_path.as_posix(),
                    metadata.project_file_path.as_posix(),
                    metadata.created_at,
                    metadata.updated_at,
                ),
            )
            db.commit()
    except Exception as error:  # noqa: BLE001
        raise ProjectCreateIssue(
            'Failed to save project record',
            {'slug': metadata.slug, 'reason': str(error)},
        ) from error

    return {
        'project': {
            'id': metadata.project_id,
            'name': metadata.name,
            'slug': metadata.slug,
            'updatedAt': metadata.updated_at,
            'lockedBy': None,
        }
    }


def list_projects() -> dict:
    with connect() as db:
        cleanup_stale_project_runtime_state(db=db)
        rows = db.execute(
            '''
            SELECT
                projects.id,
                projects.name,
                projects.slug,
                projects.updated_at,
                project_locks.user_id AS locked_by_user_id,
                users.username AS locked_by_display_name
            FROM projects
            LEFT JOIN project_locks ON project_locks.project_id = projects.id
            LEFT JOIN users ON users.id = project_locks.user_id
            WHERE projects.deleted_at IS NULL
            ORDER BY projects.updated_at DESC, projects.id DESC
            '''
        ).fetchall()
        db.commit()

    return {'projects': [_to_summary(row) for row in rows]}


def create_project(payload: dict) -> dict:
    prepared = prepare_new_project_metadata(payload.get('name', ''), field='name')

    try:
        prepared.root_path.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=False)
        for folder in PROJECT_STRUCTURE['module_dirs']:
            (prepared.root_path / folder).mkdir(parents=False, exist_ok=False)
        (prepared.root_path / PROJECT_STRUCTURE['generated_dir']).mkdir(parents=False, exist_ok=False)
        prepared.project_file_path.write_text(
            _serialize_project_yaml(prepared.project_id, prepared.name),
            encoding='utf-8',
        )
    except Exception as error:  # noqa: BLE001
        if prepared.root_path.exists():
            shutil.rmtree(prepared.root_path, ignore_errors=True)
        raise ProjectCreateIssue(
            'Failed to create project files',
            {'slug': prepared.slug, 'reason': str(error)},
        ) from error

    try:
        return register_prepared_project(prepared)
    except ProjectCreateIssue:
        if prepared.root_path.exists():
            shutil.rmtree(prepared.root_path, ignore_errors=True)
        raise


def delete_project(payload: dict) -> dict:
    project_id = str(payload.get('projectId', '')).strip()
    if not project_id:
        raise ValidationIssue('Project id is required', {'field': 'projectId'})

    now = utc_now_iso()

    with connect() as db:
        cleanup_stale_project_runtime_state(db=db, project_id=project_id, now_iso=now)
        row = db.execute(
            '''
            SELECT id, slug, root_path, deleted_at
            FROM projects
            WHERE id = ?
            ''',
            (project_id,),
        ).fetchone()

        if row is None:
            raise ProjectNotFoundIssue('Project not found', {'projectId': project_id})

        if row['deleted_at'] is not None:
            return {
                'projectId': project_id,
                'deleted': True,
                'alreadyDeleted': True,
            }

        lock_row = db.execute(
            '''
            SELECT project_locks.user_id AS user_id, users.username AS display_name
            FROM project_locks
            LEFT JOIN users ON users.id = project_locks.user_id
            WHERE project_locks.project_id = ?
            ''',
            (project_id,),
        ).fetchone()
        if lock_row is not None:
            locked_by_user_id = str(lock_row['user_id'] or '').strip()
            locked_by_display_name = str(lock_row['display_name'] or '').strip()
            raise ProjectDeleteIssue(
                'Cannot delete project while a live lock is active',
                {
                    'projectId': project_id,
                    'lockedBy': {
                        'userId': locked_by_user_id,
                        'displayName': locked_by_display_name or locked_by_user_id,
                    },
                },
            )

        project_root = Path(str(row['root_path']))
        deleted_root = SETTINGS.workspace_deleted_projects_root / f'{row["slug"]}__{project_id}'

        try:
            SETTINGS.workspace_deleted_projects_root.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
            if project_root.exists():
                if deleted_root.exists():
                    shutil.rmtree(deleted_root, ignore_errors=True)
                project_root.rename(deleted_root)
            db.execute(
                '''
                UPDATE projects
                SET deleted_at = ?, deleted_root_path = ?, updated_at = ?
                WHERE id = ?
                ''',
                (now, deleted_root.as_posix(), now, project_id),
            )
            db.commit()
        except Exception as error:  # noqa: BLE001
            raise ProjectDeleteIssue(
                'Failed to delete project',
                {'projectId': project_id, 'reason': str(error)},
            ) from error

    return {
        'projectId': project_id,
        'deleted': True,
        'alreadyDeleted': False,
    }
