﻿from __future__ import annotations

import shutil
import time
import zipfile
from datetime import datetime, timedelta, timezone
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Any
from uuid import uuid4

import yaml

from rtb.app.core.constants import (
    API_PROJECT_EXPORTS_ENDPOINT,
    PROJECT_EXPORT_ARTIFACT_MAX_AGE_SECONDS,
    PROJECT_IMPORT_POLICY,
    PROJECT_STRUCTURE,
)
from rtb.app.core.settings import SETTINGS
from rtb.app.db.bootstrap import connect
from rtb.app.models.project_snapshot import (
    CloseProjectPayload,
    ProjectSnapshot,
    ProjectSnapshotDocument,
    ProjectHeartbeatPayload,
    ProjectSnapshotProject,
    SaveProjectAsPayload,
    SaveAllPayload,
)
from rtb.app.services import project_catalog
from rtb.app.services.errors import (
    LostProjectLockIssue,
    ProjectCreateIssue,
    ProjectExportIssue,
    ProjectImportIssue,
    ProjectLockedIssue,
    ProjectNotFoundIssue,
    ProjectOpenIssue,
    ProjectSaveIssue,
    ValidationIssue,
)
from rtb.app.utils.time_utils import utc_now_iso


class ProjectStorageService:
    def __init__(self, db_connect=connect):
        self._db_connect = db_connect
        self._project_export_artifacts: dict[str, dict[str, str | float]] = {}

    def open_project_snapshot(self, payload: dict[str, Any], *, user_id: str) -> dict[str, Any]:
        project_id = str(payload.get('projectId', '')).strip()
        if not project_id:
            raise ValidationIssue('Project id is required', {'field': 'projectId'})

        project_row = self._load_project_metadata(project_id)
        normalized_user_id = self._normalize_user_id(user_id)
        project_root = Path(str(project_row['root_path']))
        project_file_path = Path(str(project_row['project_file_path']))
        self._verify_workspace_storage(
            project_id=project_id,
            project_slug=str(project_row['slug']),
            project_root=project_root,
            project_file_path=project_file_path,
        )

        if not project_root.exists():
            raise ProjectOpenIssue(
                'Project root path does not exist',
                {'projectId': project_id, 'rootPath': project_root.as_posix()},
            )

        raw = self._read_yaml_object(
            project_file_path,
            details={'projectId': project_id, 'projectFilePath': project_file_path.as_posix()},
        )
        lock_token = self._acquire_or_refresh_project_lock(
            project_id=project_id,
            user_id=normalized_user_id,
        )

        snapshot = ProjectSnapshot(
            source=PROJECT_STRUCTURE['project_source_backend'],
            project=ProjectSnapshotProject(
                projectId=str(project_row['id']),
                name=str(project_row['name']),
                slug=str(project_row['slug']),
                updatedAt=str(project_row['updated_at']),
            ),
            raw=raw,
            documents={
                module_id: self._read_module_documents(
                    project_root=project_root,
                    project_id=project_id,
                    module_id=module_id,
                )
                for module_id in PROJECT_STRUCTURE['module_dirs']
            },
        )

        return {
            'snapshot': snapshot.model_dump(by_alias=True),
            'lockToken': lock_token,
        }

    def save_project_snapshot(self, payload: dict[str, Any], *, user_id: str) -> dict[str, Any]:
        try:
            save_payload = SaveAllPayload.model_validate(payload)
        except Exception as error:  # noqa: BLE001
            raise ValidationIssue('Invalid save payload', {'reason': str(error)}) from error

        project_id = save_payload.project_id
        if not project_id:
            raise ValidationIssue('Project id is required', {'field': 'projectId'})

        normalized_user_id = self._normalize_user_id(user_id)
        lock_token = str(save_payload.lock_token or '').strip()
        project_row = self._load_project_metadata(project_id)
        self._validate_owned_project_lock(
            project_id=project_id,
            user_id=normalized_user_id,
            lock_token=lock_token,
            lock_token_field='lockToken',
        )
        project_root = Path(str(project_row['root_path']))
        project_file_path = Path(str(project_row['project_file_path']))
        try:
            self._verify_workspace_storage(
                project_id=project_id,
                project_slug=str(project_row['slug']),
                project_root=project_root,
                project_file_path=project_file_path,
            )
        except ProjectOpenIssue as error:
            raise ProjectSaveIssue(str(error), error.details) from error

        if not project_root.exists():
            raise ProjectSaveIssue(
                'Project root path does not exist',
                {'projectId': project_id, 'rootPath': project_root.as_posix()},
            )

        raw = save_payload.project_snapshot.raw
        if not isinstance(raw, dict):
            raise ValidationIssue('Project snapshot raw is required', {'field': 'projectSnapshot.raw'})

        normalized_raw = self._normalize_raw_project(raw, project_id)
        normalized_documents = self._normalize_snapshot_documents(
            project_id=project_id,
            documents=save_payload.project_snapshot.documents,
        )

        staging_root = project_root / '.save-staging'
        backup_root = project_root / '.save-backup'
        promoted_modules: list[str] = []
        project_file_promoted = False
        project_name_for_catalog = str(project_row['name'])

        try:
            self._clear_path(staging_root)
            self._clear_path(backup_root)
            self._build_staging_snapshot(
                staging_root=staging_root,
                raw=normalized_raw,
                normalized_documents=normalized_documents,
            )

            for module_id in PROJECT_STRUCTURE['module_dirs']:
                self._promote_module_dir(
                    project_root=project_root,
                    module_id=module_id,
                    staging_root=staging_root,
                    backup_root=backup_root,
                )
                promoted_modules.append(module_id)

            self._promote_project_file(
                project_file_path=project_file_path,
                staging_root=staging_root,
                backup_root=backup_root,
            )
            project_file_promoted = True
            project_name_for_catalog = self._extract_project_name(normalized_raw, default_name=project_name_for_catalog)
        except ValidationIssue:
            raise
        except ProjectNotFoundIssue:
            raise
        except Exception as error:  # noqa: BLE001
            rollback_errors = self._rollback_promoted_paths(
                project_root=project_root,
                project_file_path=project_file_path,
                backup_root=backup_root,
                promoted_modules=promoted_modules,
                project_file_promoted=project_file_promoted,
            )
            details = {'projectId': project_id, 'reason': str(error)}
            if rollback_errors:
                details['rollbackIssues'] = rollback_errors
            raise ProjectSaveIssue(
                'Failed to save project snapshot',
                details,
            ) from error
        finally:
            self._clear_path(staging_root)

        self._clear_path(backup_root)
        updated_at = self._touch_project_metadata(
            project_id=project_id,
            project_name=project_name_for_catalog,
        )
        project_meta = ProjectSnapshotProject(
            projectId=project_id,
            name=project_name_for_catalog,
            slug=str(project_row['slug']),
            updatedAt=updated_at,
        )
        return {
            'project': project_meta.model_dump(by_alias=True)
        }

    def close_project_session(self, payload: dict[str, Any], *, user_id: str) -> dict[str, Any]:
        try:
            close_payload = CloseProjectPayload.model_validate(payload)
        except Exception as error:  # noqa: BLE001
            raise ValidationIssue('Invalid close payload', {'reason': str(error)}) from error

        project_id = str(close_payload.project_id or '').strip()
        if not project_id:
            raise ValidationIssue('Project id is required', {'field': 'projectId'})

        lock_token = str(close_payload.lock_token or '').strip()
        normalized_user_id = self._normalize_user_id(user_id)
        self._load_project_metadata(project_id)
        self._validate_owned_project_lock(
            project_id=project_id,
            user_id=normalized_user_id,
            lock_token=lock_token,
            lock_token_field='lockToken',
        )
        now_iso = utc_now_iso()
        with self._db_connect() as db:
            db.execute(
                '''
                DELETE FROM project_locks
                WHERE project_id = ? AND user_id = ? AND lock_token = ?
                ''',
                (project_id, normalized_user_id, lock_token),
            )
            db.execute(
                '''
                UPDATE project_sessions
                SET is_active = 0, closed_at = ?, last_seen_at = ?, updated_at = ?
                WHERE project_id = ? AND user_id = ? AND lock_token = ? AND is_active = 1
                ''',
                (now_iso, now_iso, now_iso, project_id, normalized_user_id, lock_token),
            )
            db.commit()

        return {
            'projectId': project_id,
            'closed': True,
        }

    def heartbeat_project_session(self, payload: dict[str, Any], *, user_id: str) -> dict[str, Any]:
        try:
            heartbeat_payload = ProjectHeartbeatPayload.model_validate(payload)
        except Exception as error:  # noqa: BLE001
            raise ValidationIssue('Invalid heartbeat payload', {'reason': str(error)}) from error

        project_id = str(heartbeat_payload.project_id or '').strip()
        if not project_id:
            raise ValidationIssue('Project id is required', {'field': 'projectId'})

        lock_token = str(heartbeat_payload.lock_token or '').strip()
        normalized_user_id = self._normalize_user_id(user_id)
        self._load_project_metadata(project_id)
        self._validate_owned_project_lock(
            project_id=project_id,
            user_id=normalized_user_id,
            lock_token=lock_token,
            lock_token_field='lockToken',
        )
        expires_at = self._refresh_project_lock_and_session(
            project_id=project_id,
            user_id=normalized_user_id,
            lock_token=lock_token,
        )
        return {
            'projectId': project_id,
            'lockToken': lock_token,
            'expiresAt': expires_at,
        }

    def save_project_snapshot_as(self, payload: dict[str, Any], *, user_id: str) -> dict[str, Any]:
        try:
            save_as_payload = SaveProjectAsPayload.model_validate(payload)
        except Exception as error:  # noqa: BLE001
            raise ValidationIssue('Invalid save-as payload', {'reason': str(error)}) from error

        source_project_id = str(save_as_payload.project_id or '').strip()
        if not source_project_id:
            raise ValidationIssue('Project id is required', {'field': 'projectId'})

        new_name = str(save_as_payload.new_name or '').strip()
        if not new_name:
            raise ValidationIssue('Project name is required', {'field': 'newName'})

        lock_token = str(save_as_payload.lock_token or '').strip()
        normalized_user_id = self._normalize_user_id(user_id)
        self._load_project_metadata(source_project_id)
        self._validate_owned_project_lock(
            project_id=source_project_id,
            user_id=normalized_user_id,
            lock_token=lock_token,
            lock_token_field='lockToken',
        )
        try:
            prepared = project_catalog.prepare_new_project_metadata(new_name, field='newName')
            raw = save_as_payload.project_snapshot.raw
            if not isinstance(raw, dict):
                raise ValidationIssue('Project snapshot raw is required', {'field': 'projectSnapshot.raw'})

            normalized_raw = self._normalize_raw_project(raw, prepared.project_id)
            normalized_raw['project']['id'] = prepared.project_id
            normalized_raw['project']['name'] = prepared.name

            normalized_documents = self._normalize_snapshot_documents(
                project_id=prepared.project_id,
                documents=save_as_payload.project_snapshot.documents,
            )

            save_result = self._save_project_snapshot_as_new_project(
                source_project_id=source_project_id,
                prepared=prepared,
                normalized_raw=normalized_raw,
                normalized_documents=normalized_documents,
            )
            next_lock_token = self._acquire_or_refresh_project_lock(
                project_id=prepared.project_id,
                user_id=normalized_user_id,
            )
            self._release_project_lock_and_session(
                project_id=source_project_id,
                user_id=normalized_user_id,
                lock_token=lock_token,
            )
            return {
                **save_result,
                'lockToken': next_lock_token,
            }
        except ProjectNotFoundIssue:
            raise
        except ProjectCreateIssue:
            raise
        except ValidationIssue:
            raise
        except ProjectSaveIssue:
            raise
        except Exception as error:  # noqa: BLE001
            raise ProjectSaveIssue(
                'Failed to save project snapshot as new project',
                {'projectId': source_project_id, 'reason': str(error)},
            ) from error

    def _release_project_lock_and_session(self, *, project_id: str, user_id: str, lock_token: str) -> None:
        now_iso = utc_now_iso()
        with self._db_connect() as db:
            db.execute(
                '''
                DELETE FROM project_locks
                WHERE project_id = ? AND user_id = ? AND lock_token = ?
                ''',
                (project_id, user_id, lock_token),
            )
            db.execute(
                '''
                UPDATE project_sessions
                SET is_active = 0, closed_at = ?, last_seen_at = ?, updated_at = ?
                WHERE project_id = ? AND user_id = ? AND lock_token = ? AND is_active = 1
                ''',
                (now_iso, now_iso, now_iso, project_id, user_id, lock_token),
            )
            db.commit()

    def _load_project_metadata(self, project_id: str):
        with self._db_connect() as db:
            row = db.execute(
                '''
                SELECT id, name, slug, root_path, project_file_path, updated_at
                FROM projects
                WHERE id = ? AND deleted_at IS NULL
                ''',
                (project_id,),
            ).fetchone()

        if row is None:
            raise ProjectNotFoundIssue('Project not found', {'projectId': project_id})

        return row

    @staticmethod
    def _normalize_user_id(user_id: str | None) -> str:
        normalized_user_id = str(user_id or '').strip()
        return normalized_user_id or SETTINGS.default_user_id

    @staticmethod
    def _iso_to_utc_datetime(value: str) -> datetime | None:
        normalized = str(value or '').strip()
        if not normalized:
            return None
        try:
            return datetime.fromisoformat(normalized.replace('Z', '+00:00')).astimezone(timezone.utc)
        except ValueError:
            return None

    @staticmethod
    def _compute_lock_expiry_iso(now_iso: str) -> str:
        base_time = ProjectStorageService._iso_to_utc_datetime(now_iso)
        if base_time is None:
            base_time = datetime.now(timezone.utc)
        return (base_time + timedelta(seconds=max(1, SETTINGS.lock_ttl_seconds))).isoformat(timespec='seconds').replace('+00:00', 'Z')

    def _acquire_or_refresh_project_lock(self, *, project_id: str, user_id: str) -> str:
        now_iso = utc_now_iso()
        expires_at = self._compute_lock_expiry_iso(now_iso)
        next_lock_token = uuid4().hex
        now_utc = self._iso_to_utc_datetime(now_iso) or datetime.now(timezone.utc)
        with self._db_connect() as db:
            self._ensure_user_exists(db=db, user_id=user_id, now_iso=now_iso)
            project_catalog.cleanup_stale_project_runtime_state(
                db=db,
                project_id=project_id,
                now_iso=now_iso,
            )
            current_row = db.execute(
                '''
                SELECT project_id, user_id, lock_token, expires_at
                FROM project_locks
                WHERE project_id = ?
                ''',
                (project_id,),
            ).fetchone()

            if current_row is None:
                db.execute(
                    '''
                    INSERT INTO project_locks(
                        project_id, user_id, lock_token, acquired_at, last_heartbeat_at, expires_at, created_at, updated_at
                    )
                    VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)
                    ''',
                    (project_id, user_id, next_lock_token, now_iso, now_iso, expires_at, now_iso, now_iso),
                )
                lock_token = next_lock_token
            else:
                current_expires = self._iso_to_utc_datetime(str(current_row['expires_at']))
                lock_is_live = current_expires is not None and current_expires > now_utc
                current_owner = str(current_row['user_id'] or '').strip()
                current_token = str(current_row['lock_token'] or '').strip()

                if lock_is_live and current_owner and current_owner != user_id:
                    raise ProjectLockedIssue(
                        'Project is locked by another user',
                        {
                            'projectId': project_id,
                            'lockedBy': current_owner,
                            'expiresAt': str(current_row['expires_at'] or ''),
                        },
                    )

                lock_token = (
                    current_token
                    if lock_is_live and current_owner == user_id and current_token
                    else next_lock_token
                )
                db.execute(
                    '''
                    UPDATE project_locks
                    SET user_id = ?, lock_token = ?, acquired_at = ?, last_heartbeat_at = ?, expires_at = ?, updated_at = ?
                    WHERE project_id = ?
                    ''',
                    (user_id, lock_token, now_iso, now_iso, expires_at, now_iso, project_id),
                )

            self._activate_project_session_db(
                db=db,
                project_id=project_id,
                user_id=user_id,
                lock_token=lock_token,
                now_iso=now_iso,
            )
            db.commit()

        return lock_token

    @staticmethod
    def _ensure_user_exists(*, db, user_id: str, now_iso: str) -> None:
        normalized_user_id = str(user_id or '').strip()
        if not normalized_user_id:
            return
        db.execute(
            '''
            INSERT INTO users(id, username, created_at, updated_at)
            VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?)
            ON CONFLICT(id) DO UPDATE SET
                username = excluded.username,
                updated_at = excluded.updated_at
            ''',
            (normalized_user_id, normalized_user_id, now_iso, now_iso),
        )

    def _validate_owned_project_lock(
        self,
        *,
        project_id: str,
        user_id: str,
        lock_token: str,
        lock_token_field: str,
    ) -> None:
        normalized_lock_token = str(lock_token or '').strip()
        if not normalized_lock_token:
            raise LostProjectLockIssue(
                'Project lock token is required',
                {'projectId': project_id, 'field': lock_token_field},
            )

        now_iso = utc_now_iso()
        now_utc = self._iso_to_utc_datetime(now_iso) or datetime.now(timezone.utc)
        with self._db_connect() as db:
            project_catalog.cleanup_stale_project_runtime_state(
                db=db,
                project_id=project_id,
                now_iso=now_iso,
            )
            row = db.execute(
                '''
                SELECT user_id, lock_token, expires_at
                FROM project_locks
                WHERE project_id = ?
                ''',
                (project_id,),
            ).fetchone()

            if row is None:
                raise LostProjectLockIssue('Project lock is missing', {'projectId': project_id})

            expires_at = self._iso_to_utc_datetime(str(row['expires_at']))
            if expires_at is None or expires_at <= now_utc:
                raise LostProjectLockIssue('Project lock has expired', {'projectId': project_id})

            owner = str(row['user_id'] or '').strip()
            token = str(row['lock_token'] or '').strip()
            if owner != user_id or token != normalized_lock_token:
                raise LostProjectLockIssue(
                    'Project lock ownership does not match',
                    {'projectId': project_id, 'ownerUserId': owner},
                )

    def _refresh_project_lock_and_session(self, *, project_id: str, user_id: str, lock_token: str) -> str:
        now_iso = utc_now_iso()
        expires_at = self._compute_lock_expiry_iso(now_iso)
        with self._db_connect() as db:
            updated_rows = db.execute(
                '''
                UPDATE project_locks
                SET last_heartbeat_at = ?, expires_at = ?, updated_at = ?
                WHERE project_id = ? AND user_id = ? AND lock_token = ?
                ''',
                (now_iso, expires_at, now_iso, project_id, user_id, lock_token),
            ).rowcount
            if updated_rows != 1:
                raise LostProjectLockIssue('Project lock is missing', {'projectId': project_id})

            self._activate_project_session_db(
                db=db,
                project_id=project_id,
                user_id=user_id,
                lock_token=lock_token,
                now_iso=now_iso,
            )
            db.commit()

        return expires_at

    def _activate_project_session_db(
        self,
        *,
        db,
        project_id: str,
        user_id: str,
        lock_token: str,
        now_iso: str,
    ) -> None:
        db.execute(
            '''
            UPDATE project_sessions
            SET is_active = 0, closed_at = ?, updated_at = ?
            WHERE project_id = ? AND is_active = 1 AND (user_id <> ? OR lock_token <> ?)
            ''',
            (now_iso, now_iso, project_id, user_id, lock_token),
        )

        existing = db.execute(
            '''
            SELECT session_id
            FROM project_sessions
            WHERE project_id = ? AND user_id = ? AND lock_token = ? AND is_active = 1
            ORDER BY opened_at DESC, session_id DESC
            LIMIT 1
            ''',
            (project_id, user_id, lock_token),
        ).fetchone()

        if existing is None:
            db.execute(
                '''
                INSERT INTO project_sessions(
                    session_id, project_id, user_id, lock_token, opened_at, last_seen_at, mode, is_active, closed_at, created_at, updated_at
                )
                VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?, 1, NULL, ?, ?)
                ''',
                (
                    uuid4().hex,
                    project_id,
                    user_id,
                    lock_token,
                    now_iso,
                    now_iso,
                    SETTINGS.session_mode_edit,
                    now_iso,
                    now_iso,
                ),
            )
            return

        db.execute(
            '''
            UPDATE project_sessions
            SET last_seen_at = ?, mode = ?, is_active = 1, closed_at = NULL, updated_at = ?
            WHERE session_id = ?
            ''',
            (now_iso, SETTINGS.session_mode_edit, now_iso, str(existing['session_id'])),
        )

    def _save_project_snapshot_as_new_project(
        self,
        *,
        source_project_id: str,
        prepared: project_catalog.PreparedProjectMetadata,
        normalized_raw: dict[str, Any],
        normalized_documents: dict[str, list[tuple[str, dict[str, Any]]]],
    ) -> dict[str, Any]:
        project_root = prepared.root_path
        project_file_path = prepared.project_file_path
        staging_root = project_root / '.save-staging'
        backup_root = project_root / '.save-backup'
        promoted_modules: list[str] = []
        project_file_promoted = False
        created_project_root = False

        try:
            project_root.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=False)
            created_project_root = True
            self._clear_path(staging_root)
            self._clear_path(backup_root)
            self._build_staging_snapshot(
                staging_root=staging_root,
                raw=normalized_raw,
                normalized_documents=normalized_documents,
            )

            for module_id in PROJECT_STRUCTURE['module_dirs']:
                self._promote_module_dir(
                    project_root=project_root,
                    module_id=module_id,
                    staging_root=staging_root,
                    backup_root=backup_root,
                )
                promoted_modules.append(module_id)

            self._promote_project_file(
                project_file_path=project_file_path,
                staging_root=staging_root,
                backup_root=backup_root,
            )
            project_file_promoted = True
            (project_root / PROJECT_STRUCTURE['generated_dir']).mkdir(parents=False, exist_ok=False)
        except ValidationIssue:
            raise
        except ProjectNotFoundIssue:
            raise
        except Exception as error:  # noqa: BLE001
            rollback_errors = self._rollback_promoted_paths(
                project_root=project_root,
                project_file_path=project_file_path,
                backup_root=backup_root,
                promoted_modules=promoted_modules,
                project_file_promoted=project_file_promoted,
            )
            if created_project_root:
                self._clear_path(project_root)
            details = {'projectId': source_project_id, 'reason': str(error)}
            if rollback_errors:
                details['rollbackIssues'] = rollback_errors
            raise ProjectSaveIssue(
                'Failed to save project snapshot as new project',
                details,
            ) from error
        finally:
            self._clear_path(staging_root)
            self._clear_path(backup_root)

        try:
            project_catalog.register_prepared_project(prepared)
        except ProjectCreateIssue as error:
            if created_project_root:
                self._clear_path(project_root)
            raise ProjectCreateIssue(
                str(error),
                {'projectId': source_project_id, **(error.details or {})},
            ) from error
        except Exception as error:  # noqa: BLE001
            if created_project_root:
                self._clear_path(project_root)
            raise ProjectCreateIssue(
                'Failed to save project record',
                {'projectId': source_project_id, 'slug': prepared.slug, 'reason': str(error)},
            ) from error

        project_meta = ProjectSnapshotProject(
            projectId=prepared.project_id,
            name=prepared.name,
            slug=prepared.slug,
            updatedAt=prepared.updated_at,
        )
        return {'project': project_meta.model_dump(by_alias=True)}

    def export_project_archive(self, payload: dict[str, Any]) -> dict[str, Any]:
        self._prune_project_export_artifacts()

        project_id = str(payload.get('projectId', '')).strip()
        if not project_id:
            raise ValidationIssue('Project id is required', {'field': 'projectId'})

        with self._db_connect() as db:
            project_catalog.cleanup_stale_project_runtime_state(db=db, project_id=project_id)
            db.commit()

        project_row = self._load_project_metadata(project_id)
        project_slug = str(project_row['slug'])
        project_root = Path(str(project_row['root_path']))
        project_file_path = Path(str(project_row['project_file_path']))
        try:
            self._verify_workspace_storage(
                project_id=project_id,
                project_slug=project_slug,
                project_root=project_root,
                project_file_path=project_file_path,
            )
        except ProjectOpenIssue as error:
            raise ProjectExportIssue(str(error), error.details) from error

        if not project_root.exists():
            raise ProjectExportIssue(
                'Project root path does not exist',
                {'projectId': project_id, 'rootPath': project_root.as_posix()},
            )

        export_token = f'export_{uuid4().hex}'
        archive_file_name = f'{project_slug}.zip'
        export_root = SETTINGS.workspace_project_exports_root
        export_root.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
        archive_path = export_root / f'{export_token}.zip'

        try:
            if archive_path.exists():
                archive_path.unlink(missing_ok=True)

            with zipfile.ZipFile(archive_path, mode='w', compression=zipfile.ZIP_DEFLATED) as archive:
                archive.write(project_file_path, arcname=PROJECT_STRUCTURE['project_file_name'])
                self._write_project_dir_to_archive(archive, project_root, PROJECT_STRUCTURE['module_dirs'])
                self._write_project_dir_to_archive(archive, project_root, [PROJECT_STRUCTURE['generated_dir']])
        except Exception as error:  # noqa: BLE001
            archive_path.unlink(missing_ok=True)
            raise ProjectExportIssue(
                'Failed to export project archive',
                {'projectId': project_id, 'reason': str(error)},
            ) from error

        self._project_export_artifacts[export_token] = {
            'path': archive_path.as_posix(),
            'fileName': archive_file_name,
            'projectId': project_id,
            'createdAt': time.time(),
        }
        return {
            'exportToken': export_token,
            'downloadUrl': f'{API_PROJECT_EXPORTS_ENDPOINT}/{export_token}',
            'fileName': archive_file_name,
        }

    def import_project_archive(self, *, archive_name: str, archive_bytes: bytes) -> dict[str, Any]:
        normalized_archive_name = Path(str(archive_name or '').strip() or 'project.zip').name
        if not archive_bytes:
            raise ProjectImportIssue(
                'Project archive is required',
                {
                    'field': PROJECT_IMPORT_POLICY['archive_field_name'],
                    'reason': PROJECT_IMPORT_POLICY['invalid_zip_reason'],
                },
            )
        if Path(normalized_archive_name).suffix.lower() != PROJECT_IMPORT_POLICY['archive_extension']:
            raise ProjectImportIssue(
                'Project archive must be a .zip file',
                {
                    'field': PROJECT_IMPORT_POLICY['archive_field_name'],
                    'fileName': normalized_archive_name,
                    'reason': PROJECT_IMPORT_POLICY['invalid_zip_reason'],
                },
            )

        imports_root = SETTINGS.workspace_project_imports_root
        imports_root.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
        import_token = uuid4().hex
        upload_path = imports_root / f"{PROJECT_IMPORT_POLICY['upload_file_prefix']}{import_token}.zip"
        extract_root = imports_root / f"{PROJECT_IMPORT_POLICY['extract_dir_prefix']}{import_token}"
        imported_project_root: Path | None = None
        prepared: project_catalog.PreparedProjectMetadata | None = None

        try:
            upload_path.write_bytes(archive_bytes)
            try:
                with zipfile.ZipFile(upload_path) as archive:
                    archive.extractall(extract_root)
            except zipfile.BadZipFile as error:
                raise ProjectImportIssue(
                    'Invalid zip archive',
                    {
                        'reason': PROJECT_IMPORT_POLICY['invalid_zip_reason'],
                        'fileName': normalized_archive_name,
                    },
                ) from error
            except Exception as error:  # noqa: BLE001
                raise ProjectImportIssue(
                    'Failed to unpack project archive',
                    {
                        'reason': PROJECT_IMPORT_POLICY['invalid_zip_reason'],
                        'fileName': normalized_archive_name,
                        'details': str(error),
                    },
                ) from error

            imported_project_root = self._resolve_import_root(extract_root)
            self._validate_import_structure(imported_project_root)
            imported_raw = self._read_import_yaml(project_root=imported_project_root)
            imported_name = self._extract_import_name(
                raw=imported_raw,
                archive_name=normalized_archive_name,
            )
            prepared = project_catalog.prepare_new_project_metadata(imported_name, field='archiveName')

            shutil.copytree(imported_project_root, prepared.root_path, dirs_exist_ok=False)
            generated_root = prepared.root_path / PROJECT_STRUCTURE['generated_dir']
            if generated_root.exists() and not generated_root.is_dir():
                raise ProjectImportIssue(
                    'Imported generated path must be a directory',
                    {
                        'reason': PROJECT_IMPORT_POLICY['invalid_structure_reason'],
                        'generatedPath': generated_root.as_posix(),
                    },
                )
            generated_root.mkdir(parents=False, exist_ok=True)

            imported_raw['project']['id'] = prepared.project_id
            imported_raw['project']['name'] = prepared.name
            self._write_yaml_object(prepared.project_file_path, imported_raw)
            return project_catalog.register_prepared_project(prepared)
        except ValidationIssue:
            raise
        except ProjectCreateIssue:
            raise
        except ProjectImportIssue:
            raise
        except Exception as error:  # noqa: BLE001
            raise ProjectImportIssue(
                'Failed to import project archive',
                {'reason': PROJECT_IMPORT_POLICY['invalid_structure_reason'], 'details': str(error)},
            ) from error
        finally:
            upload_path.unlink(missing_ok=True)
            self._clear_path(extract_root)
            if prepared is not None and prepared.root_path.exists():
                is_registered = False
                try:
                    with self._db_connect() as db:
                        row = db.execute(
                            'SELECT 1 FROM projects WHERE id = ? AND deleted_at IS NULL',
                            (prepared.project_id,),
                        ).fetchone()
                    is_registered = row is not None
                except Exception:  # noqa: BLE001
                    is_registered = False

                if not is_registered:
                    self._clear_path(prepared.root_path)

    def consume_project_export_artifact(self, export_token: str) -> dict[str, str] | None:
        self._prune_project_export_artifacts()

        normalized_token = str(export_token or '').strip()
        if not normalized_token:
            return None
        artifact = self._project_export_artifacts.pop(normalized_token, None)
        if artifact is None:
            return None

        artifact_path = Path(str(artifact['path']))
        if not artifact_path.exists() or not artifact_path.is_file():
            return None

        return {
            'path': str(artifact['path']),
            'fileName': str(artifact['fileName']),
            'projectId': str(artifact['projectId']),
        }

    def _prune_project_export_artifacts(self) -> None:
        now = time.time()
        max_age_seconds = PROJECT_EXPORT_ARTIFACT_MAX_AGE_SECONDS
        export_root = SETTINGS.workspace_project_exports_root
        export_root.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

        expired_tokens: list[str] = []
        for token, artifact in self._project_export_artifacts.items():
            created_at = float(artifact.get('createdAt') or 0.0)
            if created_at > 0 and now - created_at <= max_age_seconds:
                continue

            artifact_path = Path(str(artifact.get('path', '')))
            artifact_path.unlink(missing_ok=True)
            expired_tokens.append(token)

        for token in expired_tokens:
            self._project_export_artifacts.pop(token, None)

        for artifact_path in export_root.glob('*.zip'):
            try:
                if now - artifact_path.stat().st_mtime > max_age_seconds:
                    artifact_path.unlink(missing_ok=True)
            except OSError:
                continue

    @staticmethod
    def _verify_workspace_storage(
        *,
        project_id: str,
        project_slug: str,
        project_root: Path,
        project_file_path: Path,
    ) -> None:
        workspace_root = SETTINGS.workspace_projects_root.resolve()
        expected_project_root = (workspace_root / project_slug).resolve()
        resolved_project_root = project_root.resolve()

        if resolved_project_root != expected_project_root:
            raise ProjectOpenIssue(
                'Project root path is inconsistent with workspace storage',
                {
                    'projectId': project_id,
                    'rootPath': project_root.as_posix(),
                    'workspaceProjectsRoot': workspace_root.as_posix(),
                    'expectedRootPath': expected_project_root.as_posix(),
                },
            )

        expected_project_file = (expected_project_root / PROJECT_STRUCTURE['project_file_name']).resolve()
        resolved_project_file = project_file_path.resolve()

        if resolved_project_file != expected_project_file:
            raise ProjectOpenIssue(
                'Project file path is inconsistent with workspace storage',
                {
                    'projectId': project_id,
                    'projectFilePath': project_file_path.as_posix(),
                    'expectedProjectFilePath': expected_project_file.as_posix(),
                },
            )

    def _read_module_documents(self, project_root: Path, project_id: str, module_id: str) -> list[dict[str, Any]]:
        module_path = project_root / module_id
        if not module_path.exists() or not module_path.is_dir():
            return []

        records: list[dict[str, Any]] = []
        for file_path in sorted(module_path.iterdir(), key=lambda entry: entry.name.lower()):
            if not file_path.is_file():
                continue
            if file_path.suffix.lower() not in PROJECT_STRUCTURE['module_file_extensions']:
                continue

            document = self._read_yaml_object(
                file_path,
                details={
                    'projectId': project_id,
                    'moduleId': module_id,
                    'path': file_path.as_posix(),
                },
            )
            records.append(
                ProjectSnapshotDocument(
                    moduleId=module_id,
                    path=f"backend://{project_id}/{module_id}/{file_path.name}",
                    document=document,
                ).model_dump(by_alias=True)
            )

        return records

    @staticmethod
    def _extract_project_name(raw: dict[str, Any], default_name: str) -> str:
        project_node = raw.get('project')
        if not isinstance(project_node, dict):
            return default_name

        value = str(project_node.get('name', '')).strip()
        return value or default_name

    @staticmethod
    def _normalize_raw_project(raw: dict[str, Any], project_id: str) -> dict[str, Any]:
        cloned = yaml.safe_load(yaml.safe_dump(raw, sort_keys=False, allow_unicode=True))
        if not isinstance(cloned, dict):
            raise ValidationIssue('Project snapshot raw must be an object', {'field': 'projectSnapshot.raw'})

        project = cloned.get('project')
        if not isinstance(project, dict):
            project = {}

        project['id'] = str(project.get('id') or project_id)
        project['name'] = str(project.get('name', '') or 'project').strip() or 'project'
        project['description'] = str(project.get('description', '') or '')
        cloned['project'] = project
        return cloned

    def _normalize_snapshot_documents(
        self,
        *,
        project_id: str,
        documents: dict[str, list[ProjectSnapshotDocument]],
    ) -> dict[str, list[tuple[str, dict[str, Any]]]]:
        normalized: dict[str, list[tuple[str, dict[str, Any]]]] = {}

        for module_id in PROJECT_STRUCTURE['module_dirs']:
            module_entries = documents.get(module_id, [])
            if not isinstance(module_entries, list):
                raise ValidationIssue('Project snapshot documents must be grouped by module', {'moduleId': module_id})

            occupied_file_names: set[str] = set()
            module_records: list[tuple[str, dict[str, Any]]] = []
            for index, entry in enumerate(module_entries):
                if not isinstance(entry.document, dict):
                    raise ValidationIssue(
                        'Project snapshot document payload must be an object',
                        {'moduleId': module_id, 'index': index},
                    )

                file_name = self._resolve_document_file_name(
                    project_id=project_id,
                    module_id=module_id,
                    index=index,
                    entry=entry,
                )
                normalized_file_name = file_name.lower()
                if normalized_file_name in occupied_file_names:
                    raise ValidationIssue(
                        'Filename collision detected in project snapshot',
                        {'moduleId': module_id, 'fileName': file_name},
                    )

                occupied_file_names.add(normalized_file_name)
                module_records.append((file_name, entry.document))

            normalized[module_id] = module_records

        return normalized

    @staticmethod
    def _resolve_document_file_name(
        *,
        project_id: str,
        module_id: str,
        index: int,
        entry: ProjectSnapshotDocument,
    ) -> str:
        path_value = str(entry.path or '').strip()
        name = Path(path_value).name
        if not name:
            name = f'{module_id}-{index + 1}.yaml'
        if '/' in name or '\\' in name:
            raise ValidationIssue(
                'Document path must resolve to a single file name',
                {'projectId': project_id, 'moduleId': module_id, 'path': path_value},
            )
        if Path(name).suffix.lower() not in PROJECT_STRUCTURE['module_file_extensions']:
            name = f'{Path(name).stem}.yaml'

        safe_name = Path(name).name.strip()
        if not safe_name:
            safe_name = f'{module_id}-{index + 1}.yaml'
        return safe_name

    def _build_staging_snapshot(
        self,
        *,
        staging_root: Path,
        raw: dict[str, Any],
        normalized_documents: dict[str, list[tuple[str, dict[str, Any]]]],
    ) -> None:
        staging_root.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=False)

        for module_id in PROJECT_STRUCTURE['module_dirs']:
            (staging_root / module_id).mkdir(parents=False, exist_ok=False)

        for module_id, records in normalized_documents.items():
            module_root = staging_root / module_id
            for file_name, document in records:
                self._write_yaml_object(module_root / file_name, document)

        self._write_yaml_object(staging_root / PROJECT_STRUCTURE['project_file_name'], raw)

    @staticmethod
    def _clear_path(target_path: Path) -> None:
        if not target_path.exists():
            return
        if target_path.is_dir():
            shutil.rmtree(target_path, ignore_errors=True)
            return
        target_path.unlink(missing_ok=True)

    def _promote_module_dir(
        self,
        *,
        project_root: Path,
        module_id: str,
        staging_root: Path,
        backup_root: Path,
    ) -> None:
        current_path = project_root / module_id
        staged_path = staging_root / module_id
        backup_path = backup_root / module_id

        backup_path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
        self._clear_path(backup_path)
        if current_path.exists():
            current_path.rename(backup_path)
        staged_path.rename(current_path)

    def _promote_project_file(
        self,
        *,
        project_file_path: Path,
        staging_root: Path,
        backup_root: Path,
    ) -> None:
        staged_project_file = staging_root / PROJECT_STRUCTURE['project_file_name']
        backup_project_file = backup_root / PROJECT_STRUCTURE['project_file_name']

        backup_project_file.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
        self._clear_path(backup_project_file)
        if project_file_path.exists():
            project_file_path.rename(backup_project_file)
        staged_project_file.rename(project_file_path)

    def _rollback_promoted_paths(
        self,
        *,
        project_root: Path,
        project_file_path: Path,
        backup_root: Path,
        promoted_modules: list[str],
        project_file_promoted: bool,
    ) -> list[str]:
        rollback_errors: list[str] = []

        if project_file_promoted:
            backup_project_file = backup_root / PROJECT_STRUCTURE['project_file_name']
            try:
                self._clear_path(project_file_path)
                if backup_project_file.exists():
                    backup_project_file.rename(project_file_path)
            except Exception as error:  # noqa: BLE001
                rollback_errors.append(f'project.yaml rollback failed: {error}')

        for module_id in reversed(promoted_modules):
            current_path = project_root / module_id
            backup_path = backup_root / module_id
            try:
                self._clear_path(current_path)
                if backup_path.exists():
                    backup_path.rename(current_path)
            except Exception as error:  # noqa: BLE001
                rollback_errors.append(f'{module_id} rollback failed: {error}')

        return rollback_errors

    def _touch_project_metadata(self, *, project_id: str, project_name: str) -> str:
        updated_at = utc_now_iso()
        with self._db_connect() as db:
            db.execute(
                'UPDATE projects SET name = ?, updated_at = ? WHERE id = ?',
                (project_name, updated_at, project_id),
            )
            db.commit()

        return updated_at

    @staticmethod
    def _write_project_dir_to_archive(
        archive: zipfile.ZipFile,
        project_root: Path,
        folder_names: list[str],
    ) -> None:
        for folder_name in folder_names:
            folder_root = project_root / folder_name
            if not folder_root.exists() or not folder_root.is_dir():
                continue

            archive.writestr(f'{folder_name}/', b'')
            for file_path in sorted(folder_root.rglob('*')):
                if file_path.is_dir():
                    continue
                relative_path = file_path.relative_to(project_root).as_posix()
                archive.write(file_path, arcname=relative_path)

    @staticmethod
    def _resolve_import_root(extract_root: Path) -> Path:
        if not extract_root.exists() or not extract_root.is_dir():
            raise ProjectImportIssue(
                'Imported archive cannot be extracted',
                {'reason': PROJECT_IMPORT_POLICY['invalid_zip_reason']},
            )

        ignored = set(PROJECT_IMPORT_POLICY['ignored_top_level_entries'])
        top_level_entries = [
            entry
            for entry in sorted(extract_root.iterdir(), key=lambda item: item.name.lower())
            if entry.name not in ignored
        ]
        if not top_level_entries:
            raise ProjectImportIssue(
                'Archive does not contain project files',
                {'reason': PROJECT_IMPORT_POLICY['invalid_layout_reason']},
            )

        if ProjectStorageService._has_canonical_layout(top_level_entries, extract_root):
            return extract_root

        top_level_names = {entry.name for entry in top_level_entries}
        has_any_required_module = any(
            module_dir in top_level_names
            for module_dir in PROJECT_IMPORT_POLICY['required_module_dirs']
        )

        if len(top_level_entries) == 1 and top_level_entries[0].is_dir():
            wrapper_root = top_level_entries[0]
            wrapper_entries = [entry for entry in wrapper_root.iterdir() if entry.name not in ignored]
            if ProjectStorageService._has_canonical_layout(wrapper_entries, wrapper_root):
                return wrapper_root
            wrapper_names = {entry.name for entry in wrapper_entries}
            has_wrapper_modules = any(
                module_dir in wrapper_names
                for module_dir in PROJECT_IMPORT_POLICY['required_module_dirs']
            )
            if has_wrapper_modules and PROJECT_STRUCTURE['project_file_name'] not in wrapper_names:
                raise ProjectImportIssue(
                    'Archive does not contain project.yaml',
                    {'reason': PROJECT_IMPORT_POLICY['missing_project_yaml_reason']},
                )

        if has_any_required_module and PROJECT_STRUCTURE['project_file_name'] not in top_level_names:
            raise ProjectImportIssue(
                'Archive does not contain project.yaml',
                {'reason': PROJECT_IMPORT_POLICY['missing_project_yaml_reason']},
            )

        raise ProjectImportIssue(
            'Archive layout is not supported',
            {
                'reason': PROJECT_IMPORT_POLICY['invalid_layout_reason'],
                'entries': [entry.name for entry in top_level_entries],
            },
        )

    @staticmethod
    def _has_canonical_layout(entries: list[Path], root: Path) -> bool:
        if not entries:
            return False
        names = {entry.name for entry in entries}
        _ = root
        return PROJECT_STRUCTURE['project_file_name'] in names

    @staticmethod
    def _validate_import_structure(project_root: Path) -> None:
        project_file_path = project_root / PROJECT_STRUCTURE['project_file_name']
        if not project_file_path.exists() or not project_file_path.is_file():
            raise ProjectImportIssue(
                'Archive does not contain project.yaml',
                {'reason': PROJECT_IMPORT_POLICY['missing_project_yaml_reason']},
            )

        for module_dir in PROJECT_IMPORT_POLICY['required_module_dirs']:
            module_path = project_root / module_dir
            if not module_path.exists() or not module_path.is_dir():
                raise ProjectImportIssue(
                    'Archive has invalid project structure',
                    {'reason': PROJECT_IMPORT_POLICY['invalid_structure_reason'], 'module': module_dir},
                )

        generated_path = project_root / PROJECT_STRUCTURE['generated_dir']
        if generated_path.exists() and not generated_path.is_dir():
            raise ProjectImportIssue(
                'Archive has invalid generated structure',
                {'reason': PROJECT_IMPORT_POLICY['invalid_structure_reason'], 'path': generated_path.as_posix()},
            )

    def _read_import_yaml(self, *, project_root: Path) -> dict[str, Any]:
        project_file = project_root / PROJECT_STRUCTURE['project_file_name']
        try:
            payload = self._read_yaml_object(project_file, details={'path': project_file.as_posix()})
        except ProjectOpenIssue as error:
            raise ProjectImportIssue(
                'Archive project.yaml is invalid',
                {'reason': PROJECT_IMPORT_POLICY['invalid_structure_reason'], **(error.details or {})},
            ) from error

        normalized = self._normalize_raw_project(payload, project_id='imported-project')
        return normalized

    @staticmethod
    def _extract_import_name(*, raw: dict[str, Any], archive_name: str) -> str:
        project = raw.get('project')
        if isinstance(project, dict):
            name = str(project.get('name') or '').strip()
            if name:
                return name

        archive_stem = Path(archive_name).stem.strip()
        if archive_stem:
            return archive_stem
        return 'Imported Project'

    @staticmethod
    def _read_yaml_object(path: Path, details: dict[str, Any] | None = None) -> dict[str, Any]:
        if not path.exists():
            raise ProjectOpenIssue('YAML file does not exist', {**(details or {}), 'path': path.as_posix()})

        try:
            parsed = yaml.safe_load(path.read_text(encoding='utf-8'))
        except Exception as error:  # noqa: BLE001
            raise ProjectOpenIssue(
                'Failed to read YAML file',
                {**(details or {}), 'path': path.as_posix(), 'reason': str(error)},
            ) from error

        if not isinstance(parsed, dict):
            raise ProjectOpenIssue(
                'YAML root must be an object',
                {**(details or {}), 'path': path.as_posix()},
            )

        return parsed

    @staticmethod
    def _write_yaml_object(path: Path, payload: dict[str, Any]) -> None:
        path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
        path.write_text(
            yaml.safe_dump(payload, sort_keys=False, allow_unicode=True),
            encoding='utf-8',
        )

﻿import re
import uuid


NON_ALNUM = re.compile(r'[^a-z0-9]+')
TRIM_DASH = re.compile(r'^-+|-+$')


def make_project_id() -> str:
    return f"proj_{uuid.uuid4().hex[:12]}"


def slugify(value: str) -> str:
    normalized = NON_ALNUM.sub('-', value.strip().lower())
    return TRIM_DASH.sub('', normalized)


==================================================
FILE: rtb/app/utils/metagen_runner.py
==================================================

from __future__ import annotations

import argparse
import sys
import time


def parse_args() -> argparse.Namespace:
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description='Minimal bounded MetaGen runner')
    parser.add_argument('--steps', type=int, required=True)
    parser.add_argument('--step-delay-ms', type=int, required=True)
    parser.add_argument('--stderr-every', type=int, required=True)
    return parser.parse_args()


def main() -> int:
    args = parse_args()
    steps = max(1, int(args.steps))
    delay_seconds = max(0, int(args.step_delay_ms)) / 1000.0
    stderr_every = max(1, int(args.stderr_every))

    print('metagen:start', flush=True)
    for index in range(1, steps + 1):
        print(f'metagen:stdout:{index}', flush=True)
        if index % stderr_every == 0:
            print(f'metagen:stderr:{index}', file=sys.stderr, flush=True)
        if delay_seconds > 0:
            time.sleep(delay_seconds)
    print('metagen:done', flush=True)
    return 0


if __name__ == '__main__':
    raise SystemExit(main())

﻿from datetime import datetime, timezone


def utc_now_iso() -> str:
    return datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat(timespec='seconds').replace('+00:00', 'Z')
